# Surah 18 — Al-Kahf

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 98/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.109 · Longest prose run 27 words · Em dashes 0

_Translated by claude-sonnet-5 (opus-4.8 on flagged revisions); graded by gemini-3.1-pro-preview at 2026-07-07T11:06:06.474Z. Quality metrics are surah-level. Review each translation against the Arabic below, never against any other translation._

**Overlap spans to check:** "chain that the prophet said whoever recites surat al kahf as it was revealed it will be a light for him on the day of resurrection in"

**Examiner verdict:** The translation is highly accurate and faithful to the Arabic text, with only one minor mistranslation of an idiom.

---

## 18:1-5 — verses 1-5 (shared commentary)

### Translation

[In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful, and by Him we seek help]

Tafsir of Surat al-Kahf

It is Meccan.

Mention of what has been reported concerning its virtue, and the ten verses from its beginning and its end, and that it is a protection from the Dajjal (the Antichrist):

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] I heard al-Bara' say: A man recited al-Kahf while there was an animal in the house, and it began to shy away. He looked and saw a mist, or a cloud, that had enveloped it. He mentioned that to the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Recite, so-and-so, for that is the sakinah (tranquility) descending because of the Qur'an, or descending for the Qur'an."

Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Shu'bah, with this chain. This man who was reciting it was Usayd ibn al-Hudayr, as was mentioned previously in the tafsir of al-Baqarah.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu al-Darda', from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Whoever memorizes ten verses from the beginning of Surat al-Kahf will be protected from the Dajjal."

Muslim, Abu Dawud, al-Nasa'i, and al-Tirmidhi narrated it from the hadith of Qatadah, with this chain. The wording of al-Tirmidhi is: "Whoever memorizes the three verses from the beginning of al-Kahf," and he said: hasan sahih (good and authentic).

Another route: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu al-Darda', from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Whoever recites the last ten verses of Surat al-Kahf will be protected from the trial of the Dajjal."

Muslim and al-Nasa'i also narrated it from the hadith of Qatadah, with this chain. In the wording of al-Nasa'i: "Whoever recites ten verses from al-Kahf," and he mentioned it.

Another hadith: al-Nasa'i narrated it in "al-Yawm wa'l-Laylah" from Muhammad ibn Abd al-A'la, from Khalid, from Shu'bah, from Qatadah, from Salim ibn Abi al-Ja'd, from Thawban, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Whoever recites the last ten verses of Surat al-Kahf, it will be a protection for him from the Dajjal."

It is possible that Salim heard it from both Thawban and Abu al-Darda'.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Mu'adh ibn Anas al-Juhani, from his father, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Whoever recites the beginning of Surat al-Kahf and its end, it will be a light for him from his feet to his head, and whoever recites all of it, it will be a light for him from the earth to the sky." Ahmad narrated this alone and the others did not include it.

The hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh narrated, in his tafsir, with a gharib (singular) chain of his, from Khalid ibn Sa'id ibn Abi Maryam, from Nafi', from Ibn Umar, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever recites Surat al-Kahf on the day of Friday, a light will radiate for him from beneath his feet to the horizon of the sky, illuminating for him on the Day of Resurrection, and he will be forgiven for what is between the two Fridays."

There is doubt about this hadith being marfu' (raised to the Prophet); its best status is as mawquf (halted, i.e. attributed only to the Companion).

Likewise, the imam Sa'id ibn Mansur narrated in his Sunan, from Hushaym ibn Bashir, from Abu Hashim, from Abu Mijlaz, from Qays ibn Abbad, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may Allah be pleased with him, that he said: Whoever recites Surat al-Kahf on the day of Friday, light will shine for him between him and the Ancient House.

It occurred in this way as mawquf, and likewise al-Thawri narrated it from Abu Hashim, with this chain, from the hadith of Abu Sa'id al-Khudri.

Al-Hakim narrated it in his Mustadrak from Abu Bakr Muhammad ibn al-Mu'ammal: [chain] from Abu Sa'id, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "Whoever recites Surat al-Kahf on the day of Friday, light will shine for him between him and the two Fridays." Then he said: this is a hadith sahih in its chain, and they [Bukhari and Muslim] did not include it.

Likewise the hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi narrated it in his Sunan, from al-Hakim. Then al-Bayhaqi said: Yahya ibn Kathir narrated it from Shu'bah, from Abu Hashim with his chain, that the Prophet ﷺ said: "Whoever recites Surat al-Kahf as it was revealed, it will be a light for him on the Day of Resurrection." [And Allah knows best.]

In "al-Mukhtarah" of the hafiz al-Diya' al-Maqdisi, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Mus'ab ibn Manzur ibn Zayd ibn Khalid al-Juhani, from Ali ibn al-Husayn, from his father, from Ali, marfu' (raised to the Prophet): "Whoever recites Surat al-Kahf on the day of Friday will be protected for eight days from every trial, and if the Dajjal should emerge, he will be protected from him." In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

[My Lord, grant me success]

It has already been mentioned at the beginning of the tafsir that He, exalted, praises His own sanctified Self at the openings and conclusions of matters, for He is praised in every circumstance, and to Him belongs praise in the first life and the last. Therefore He praised Himself for sending down His mighty Book upon His noble Messenger Muhammad ﷺ, for it is the greatest blessing that Allah bestowed upon the people of the earth, since He brought them out by it from darkness into light, having made it a straight book in which there is no crookedness and no deviation, but rather it guides to a straight path, clear, plain, manifest, a warner to the disbelievers and a bearer of glad tidings to the believers. Therefore He said: {and has not made in it any crookedness}, meaning: He did not place in it any crookedness, nor deviation, nor inclination, but rather made it balanced and straight. Therefore He said: {qayyiman (upright)}, meaning: straight.

{To warn of severe punishment from Him}, meaning: for whoever opposes it, denies it, and does not believe in it, He warns him of severe punishment, immediate chastisement in this world and delayed chastisement in the Hereafter. {from Him}, meaning: from Allah, whose punishment none can inflict, and whose binding none can bind.

{And to give good tidings to the believers}, meaning: by means of this Qur'an, to those who have confirmed their faith with righteous deeds, {that they will have a good reward}, meaning: a beautiful recompense with Allah.

{In which they will remain} in their reward with Allah, which is Paradise, abiding therein {forever}, permanently, with no cessation and no ending.

{And to warn those who say, "Allah has taken a son."} Ibn Ishaq said: they are the polytheists of the Arabs, in their saying: We worship the angels, and they are the daughters of Allah.

{They have no knowledge of it}, meaning: of this statement which they invented and fabricated, they have no knowledge, {nor did their fathers}, meaning: their forefathers.

{Grave is the word}: this is in the accusative as a specification (tamyiz), its meaning being: this statement of theirs is grave as a word.

It has also been said: it is an expression of astonishment, its meaning being: how grave is their word as a word, just as one says "akrim bi Zaydin rajulan" (how noble is Zayd as a man), as some Basran grammarians said. Some reciters of Mecca read it: {kaburat kalimatan} in the nominative, as one would say: "your word became great" and "your affair became great."

The meaning according to the reading of the majority is more apparent, for this is a condemnation of their statement and an emphasis on the enormity of their falsehood. Therefore He said: {a grave word it is that comes out of their mouths}, meaning: it has no support except their own claim, and they have no proof for it except their lying and fabrication. Therefore He said: {they say nothing but a lie}.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq mentioned the reason for the revelation of this noble surah. He said: An old man from the people of Egypt who came to us more than forty years ago narrated to me, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Quraysh sent al-Nadr ibn al-Harith and Uqbah ibn Abi Mu'ayt to the rabbis of the Jews in Medina, and said to them: Ask them about Muhammad, describe his description to them, and tell them of his sayings, for they are the people of the earlier Scripture, and they have knowledge of the prophets that we do not have. So the two of them set out until they arrived in Medina, and they asked the rabbis of the Jews about the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and described to them his affair and some of his sayings, and said: You are the people of the Torah, and we have come to you so that you may inform us about this companion of ours. He said: They said to them: Ask him about three things which we instruct you concerning; if he informs you of them, then he is a sent prophet, and if he does not, then the man is a fabricator, so form your own opinion about him. Ask him about young men who departed in ancient times, what was their story? For they had a wondrous tale. And ask him about a man who traveled widely, who reached the easts and wests of the earth, what was his account? [And ask him about the spirit, what is it?] If he informs you of that, then he is a prophet, so follow him, and if he does not inform you, then he is a man who fabricates, so do with his case as you see fit.

Al-Nadr and Uqbah returned until they came to Quraysh, and said: O assembly of Quraysh, we have brought you a decisive matter between you and Muhammad. The rabbis of the Jews instructed us to ask him about certain matters, and they told them what they were. So they came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said: O Muhammad, tell us, and they asked him about what they had been instructed to ask. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to them: "I will tell you tomorrow about what you have asked," without saying "if Allah wills." So they left him, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ remained fifteen nights during which Allah did not send down to him any revelation concerning that matter, nor did Gabriel, peace be upon him, come to him, until the people of Mecca began to spread rumors and say: Muhammad promised us tomorrow, and today is the fifteenth day we have entered into it, and he has not told us anything about what we asked him. And the delay of revelation grieved the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and what the people of Mecca were saying distressed him. Then Gabriel, peace be upon him, came to him from Allah, mighty and majestic, with Surat Ashab al-Kahf (the Companions of the Cave), in which there was a rebuke of him for his grief over them, and the account of what they had asked him about, the matter of the young men and the traveling man, and the saying of Allah, mighty and majestic: {And they ask you about the spirit. Say: The spirit is of the affair of my Lord, and you have not been given of knowledge except a little} [al-Isra: 85].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

[بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ وَبِهِ نَسْتَعِينُ] 

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ

وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ.

ذِكْرُ مَا وَرَدَ فِي فَضْلِهَا، وَالْعَشَرِ الْآيَاتِ مِنْ أَوَّلِهَا وَآخِرِهَا، وَأَنَّهَا عِصْمَةٌ مِنَ الدَّجَّالِ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ الْبَرَاءَ يَقُولُ: قَرَأَ رَجُلٌ الْكَهْفَ، وَفِي الدَّارِ دَابَّةٌ، فَجَعَلَتْ تَنْفِرُ، فَنَظَرَ فَإِذَا ضَبَابَةٌ -أَوْ: سَحَابَةٌ-قَدْ غَشِيَتْهُ، فَذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: " اقْرَأْ فُلَانُ، فَإِنَّهَا السَّكِينَةُ تَنَزَّلَتْ عِنْدَ الْقُرْآنِ، أَوْ تَنَزَّلَتْ لِلْقُرْآنِ ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، بِهِ . وَهَذَا الرَّجُلُ الَّذِي كَانَ يَتْلُوهَا هُوَ: أسَيْدُ بْنُ الحُضَيْر، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ الْبَقَرَةِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حدثنا يزيد، أخبرنا هَمّام بن يحيى، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ أَبِي الْجَعْدِ، عَنْ مَعْدان بْنِ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: " مَنْ حَفظ عَشْرَ آيَاتٍ مِنْ أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ، عُصِم مِنَ الدَّجَّالِ ".

رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ قَتَادَةَ بِهِ . وَلَفْظُ التِّرْمِذِيِّ: " مَنْ حَفِظَ الثَّلَاثَ الْآيَاتَ مَنْ أَوَّلِ الْكَهْفِ " وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

طَرِيقٌ أُخْرَى: قَالَ] الْإِمَامُ [ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجٌ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ سَمِعْتُ سَالِمَ بْنَ أَبِي الْجَعْدِ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ مَعْدَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: " من قَرَأَ الْعَشْرَ الْأَوَاخِرَ مِنْ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ عُصِم مِنْ فِتْنَةِ الدَّجَّالِ ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ أَيْضًا وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ قَتَادَةَ، بِهِ . وَفِي لَفْظِ النَّسَائِيِّ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ عَشْرَ آيَاتٍ مِنَ الْكَهْفِ "، فَذَكَرَهُ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي " الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ " عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، عَنْ خَالِدٍ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ أَبِي الْجَعْدِ، عَنْ ثَوْبان عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ الْعَشْرَ الْأَوَاخِرَ مِنْ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ، فَإِنَّهُ عِصْمَةٌ لَهُ مِنَ الدَّجَّالِ " .

فَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّ سالما سمعه من ثوبان ومن أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنٌ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، حَدَّثَنَا زبَّان بْنُ فَايِدٍ عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ مُعَاذِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ الْجُهَنِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ أَوَّلَ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ وَآخِرَهَا، كَانَتْ لَهُ نُورًا مِنْ قَدَمِهِ إِلَى رَأْسِهِ، وَمَنْ قَرَأَهَا كُلَّهَا كَانَتْ لَهُ نُورًا مَا بَيْنَ الْأَرْضِ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ " انْفَرَدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجُوهُ 

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُويْه [فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ] بِإِسْنَادٍ لَهُ غَرِيبٍ، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ فِي يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ، سَطَعَ لَهُ نُورٌ مِنْ تَحْتِ قَدَمِهِ إِلَى عَنَانِ السَّمَاءِ، يُضِيءُ لَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وغُفر لَهُ مَا بَيْنَ الْجُمُعَتَيْنِ " .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ فِي رَفْعِهِ نَظَرٌ، وَأَحْسَنُ أَحْوَالِهِ الْوَقْفُ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى الْإِمَامُ: " سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ " فِي سُنَنِهِ، عَنْ هُشَيْم بْنِ بشيرٍ ، عَنْ أَبِي هَاشِمٍ ، عَنْ أَبِي مِجْلَز، عَنْ قَيْسِ بْنِ عَبَّادٍ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: مَنْ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ فِي يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ، أَضَاءَ لَهُ مِنَ النُّورِ مَا بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ الْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ.

هَكَذَا وَقَعَ مَوْقُوفًا، وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي هَاشِمٍ ، بِهِ . مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ.

وَقَدْ أَخْرَجَهُ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرٍ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْمُؤَمَّلِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْفُضَيْلُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الشَّعراني، حَدَّثَنَا نُعَيم بْنُ حمَّاد، حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هَاشِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مِجْلَز، عَنْ قَيْسِ بْنِ عُبَاد، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ فِي يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ، أَضَاءَ لَهُ مِنَ النُّورِ مَا بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ الْجُمُعَتَيْنِ "، ثُمَّ قَالَ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ صَحِيحُ الْإِسْنَادِ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ فِي سُنَنِهِ، عَنِ الْحَاكِمِ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: وَرَوَاهُ يَحْيَى بْنُ كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هَاشِمٍ بِإِسْنَادِهِ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: " مَنْ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ كما أنزلت كانت لَهُ نُورًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ". [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

وَفِي " الْمُخْتَارَةِ " لِلْحَافِظِ الضِّيَاءِ الْمُقَدِّسِيِّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُصْعَبِ بْنِ مَنْظُورِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ خَالِدٍ الْجُهَنِيِّ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ مَرْفُوعًا: " مَنْ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ يَوْمَ الْجُمُعَةِ، فَهُوَ مَعْصُومٌ إِلَى ثَمَانِيَةِ أَيَّامٍ مِنْ كُلِّ فِتْنَةٍ، وَإِنْ خَرَجَ الدَّجَّالُ عُصِمَ مِنْهُ " بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

[رَبِّ وَفِّقْنِي] 

* *

قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ التَّفْسِيرِ أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى يَحْمَدُ نَفْسَهُ الْمُقَدَّسَةَ عِنْدَ فَوَاتِحَ الْأُمُورِ وَخَوَاتِيمِهَا، فَإِنَّهُ الْمَحْمُودُ عَلَى كُلِّ حَالٍ، وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ فِي الْأُولَى وَالْآخِرَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا حَمِدَ نَفْسَهُ عَلَى إِنْزَالِهِ كِتَابَهُ الْعَزِيزَ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ الْكَرِيمِ مُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ؛ فَإِنَّهُ أَعْظَمُ نِعْمَةً أَنْعَمَهَا اللَّهُ عَلَى أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ؛ إِذْ أَخْرَجَهُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ، حَيْثُ جَعَلَهُ كِتَابًا مُسْتَقِيمًا لَا اعْوِجَاجَ فِيهِ وَلَا زَيْغَ، بَلْ يَهْدِي إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ، بَيِّنًا وَاضِحًا جَلِيًّا نَذِيرًا لِلْكَافِرِينَ وَبَشِيرًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَمْ يَجْعَلْ لَهُ عِوَجَا﴾ أَيْ: لَمْ يَجْعَلْ فِيهِ اعْوِجَاجًا وَلَا زَيْغًا وَلَا مَيْلًا بَلْ جَعَلَهُ مُعْتَدِلًا مُسْتَقِيمًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿قَيِّمًا﴾ أَيْ: مُسْتَقِيمًا.

﴿لِيُنْذِرَ بَأْسًا شَدِيدًا مِنْ لَدُنْهُ﴾ أَيْ: لِمَنْ خَالَفَهُ وَكَذَّبَهُ وَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِهِ، يُنْذِرُهُ بَأْسًا شَدِيدًا، عُقُوبَةً عَاجِلَةً فِي الدُّنْيَا وَآجِلَةً فِي الْآخِرَةِ ﴿مِنْ لَدُنْهُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي لَا يُعَذّب عَذَابَهُ أَحَدٌ، وَلَا يُوثِقُ وَثَاقَهُ أَحَدٌ.

﴿وَيُبَشِّرُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ الَّذِينَ صَدَّقُوا إِيمَانَهُمْ بِالْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ أَجْرًا حَسَنًا﴾ أَيْ: مَثُوبَةً عِنْدَ اللَّهِ جَمِيلَةً

﴿مَاكِثِينَ فِيهِ﴾ فِي ثَوَابِهِمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، وَهُوَ الْجَنَّةُ، خَالِدِينَ فِيهِ ﴿أَبَدًا﴾ دَائِمًا لَا زَوَالَ لَهُ وَلَا انْقِضَاءَ.

﴿وَيُنْذِرَ الَّذِينَ (٤) قَالُوا اتَّخَذَ اللَّهُ وَلَدًا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَهُمْ مُشْرِكُو الْعَرَبِ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: نَحْنُ نَعْبُدُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ، وَهُمْ بَنَاتُ اللَّهِ.

﴿مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِهَذَا الْقَوْلِ الَّذِي افْتَرَوْهُ وَائْتَفَكُوهُ مِنْ عِلْمٍ ﴿وَلا لآبَائِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَسْلَافِهِمْ.

﴿كَبُرَتْ كَلِمَةً﴾ : نُصِبَ عَلَى التَّمْيِيزِ، تَقْدِيرُهُ: كَبُرَتْ كَلِمَتُهُمْ هَذِهِ كَلِمَةً.

وَقِيلَ: عَلَى التَّعَجُّبِ، تَقْدِيرُهُ: أَعْظِمْ بِكَلِمَتِهِمْ كَلِمَةً، كَمَا تَقُولُ: أَكْرِمْ بِزَيْدٍ رَجُلًا قَالَهُ بَعْضُ الْبَصْرِيِّينَ. وَقَرَأَ ذَلِكَ بَعْضُ قُرَّاءِ مَكَّةَ: ﴿كَبُرَتْ كَلِمَةً﴾ كَمَا يُقَالُ: عَظُم قولُك، وَكَبُرَ شأنُك.

وَالْمَعْنَى عَلَى قِرَاءَةِ الْجُمْهُورِ أَظْهَرُ؛ فَإِنَّ هَذَا تَبْشِيعٌ لِمَقَالَتِهِمْ وَاسْتِعْظَامٌ لِإِفْكِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كَبُرَتْ كَلِمَةً تَخْرُجُ مِنْ أَفْوَاهِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ لَهَا مُسْتَنَدٌ سِوَى قَوْلِهِمْ، وَلَا دَلِيلَ لَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا إِلَّا كَذِبُهُمْ وَافْتِرَاؤُهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ يَقُولُونَ إِلا كَذِبًا﴾ .

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ سَبَبَ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ، فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي شَيْخٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ مِصْرَ قَدِمَ عَلَيْنَا مُنْذُ بِضْعٍ وَأَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: بَعَثَتْ قُرَيْشٌ النَّضْرَ بْنَ الْحَارِثِ، وَعُقْبَةَ بْنَ أَبِي مُعَيط، إِلَى أَحْبَارِ يَهُودَ بِالْمَدِينَةِ، فَقَالُوا لَهُمْ: سَلُوهُمْ عَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَصِفُوا لَهُمْ صِفَتَهُ، وَأَخْبِرُوهُمْ بِقَوْلِهِ؛ فَإِنَّهُمْ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ الْأَوَّلِ، وَعِنْدَهُمْ مَا لَيْسَ عِنْدَنَا مِنْ عِلْمِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ. فَخَرَجَا حَتَّى قَدِمَا الْمَدِينَةَ، فَسَأَلُوا أَحْبَارَ يَهُودَ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَوَصَفُوا لَهُمْ أَمْرَهُ وَبَعْضَ قَوْلِهِ، وَقَالَا إِنَّكُمْ أَهْلُ التَّوْرَاةِ، وَقَدْ جِئْنَاكُمْ لِتُخْبِرُونَا عَنْ صَاحِبِنَا هَذَا. قَالَ: فَقَالَتْ لَهُمْ: سَلُوهُ عَنْ ثَلَاثٍ نَأْمُرُكُمْ بِهِنَّ، فَإِنْ أَخْبَرَكُمْ بِهِن، فَهُوَ نَبِيٌّ مُرْسَلٌ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَفْعَلْ فَالرَّجُلُ مُتَقَول فَرَوا فِيهِ رَأْيَكُمْ: سَلُوهُ عَنْ فِتْيَةٍ ذَهَبُوا فِي الدَّهْرِ الْأَوَّلِ، مَا كَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِمْ؟ فَإِنَّهُمْ قَدْ كَانَ لَهُمْ حَدِيثٌ عَجِيبٌ. وَسَلُوهُ عَنْ رَجُلٍ طَوَّافٍ بَلَغَ مَشَارِقَ الْأَرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا، مَا كَانَ نبَؤه ؟ [وَسَلُوهُ عَنِ الرُّوحِ، مَا هُوَ؟] فَإِنْ أَخْبَرَكُمْ بِذَلِكَ فَهُوَ نَبِيٌّ فَاتَّبِعُوهُ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يُخْبِرْكُمْ فَإِنَّهُ رَجُلٌ مُتَقَوِّلٌ، فَاصْنَعُوا فِي أَمْرِهِ مَا بَدَا لَكُمْ.

فَأَقْبَلَ النَّضْرُ وَعُقْبَةُ حَتَّى قَدِمَا عَلَى قُرَيْشٍ، فَقَالَا يَا مَعْشَرَ قُرَيْشٍ، قَدْ جِئْنَاكُمْ بِفَصْلِ مَا بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَ مُحَمَّدٍ، قَدْ أَمَرَنَا أَحْبَارُ يَهُودَ أَنْ نَسْأَلَهُ عَنْ أُمُورٍ، فَأَخْبَرُوهُمْ بِهَا، فَجَاءُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالُوا: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَخْبِرْنَا: فَسَأَلُوهُ عَمَّا أَمَرُوهُمْ بِهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُخْبِرُكُمْ غَدًا بِمَا سَأَلْتُمْ عَنْهُ". وَلَمْ يَسْتَثْنِ، فَانْصَرَفُوا عَنْهُ، وَمَكَثَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَمْسَ عَشْرَةَ لَيْلَةً، لَا يُحدث اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ فِي ذَلِكَ وَحْيًا، وَلَا يَأْتِيهِ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حَتَّى أَرْجَفَ أَهْلُ مَكَّةَ وَقَالُوا: وَعَدَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ غَدًا، وَالْيَوْمُ خمسَ عشرةَ قَدْ أَصْبَحْنَا فِيهَا، لَا يُخبرنا بِشَيْءٍ عَمَّا سَأَلْنَاهُ عَنْهُ. وَحَتَّى أحزنَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مكثُ الْوَحْيِ عَنْهُ، وَشَقَّ عَلَيْهِ مَا يَتَكَلَّمُ بِهِ أَهْلُ مَكَّةَ، ثُمَّ جَاءَهُ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، بِسُورَةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ، فِيهَا مُعَاتَبَتُهُ إِيَّاهُ عَلَى حُزْنِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وخَبَر مَا سَأَلُوهُ عَنْهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْفِتْيَةِ وَالرَّجُلِ الطَّوَّافِ، وَقَوْلُ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الرُّوحِ قُلِ الرُّوحُ مِنْ أَمْرِ رَبِّي وَمَا أُوتِيتُمْ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٨٥]

---

## 18:6-8 — verses 6-8 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, consoling His Messenger ﷺ in his grief over the polytheists, because of their abandonment of faith and their remoteness from it, as He, the Exalted, said: {So do not let yourself perish in grief over them} [Fatir: 8], and He said {And do not grieve over them} [al-Nahl: 127], and He said {Perhaps you would kill yourself with grief that they will not become believers} [al-Shu'ara: 3]

Bakhi': meaning destroying yourself through your grief over them. This is why He said {So perhaps you would kill yourself, following after them, out of grief, if they do not believe in this narration}, meaning the Qur'an, {out of sorrow}. He is saying: do not destroy yourself out of sorrow.

Qatadah said: kill yourself out of anger and grief over them. Mujahid said: out of distress. The meaning is close in both cases, that is: do not grieve over them, but rather convey to them the message of Allah. Whoever is guided, it is for his own soul, and whoever goes astray, he only goes astray against it, so do not let yourself perish in grief over them.

Then the Almighty informs that He made this world a perishing abode, adorned with a fleeting adornment. He made it a house of testing, not a house of permanent settlement, so He said: {Indeed, We have made what is on the earth an adornment for it, that We may test them as to which of them is best in deed}.

Qatadah reported from Abu Nadrah, from Abu Sa'id, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Indeed this world is green and sweet, and Allah is making you successors in it, watching what you will do. So beware of this world, and beware of women, for the first trial of the Children of Israel was through women."

Then the Almighty informs of its passing away and its perishing, its emptying out and its termination, its departure and its ruin, so He said: {And indeed, We will make what is upon it a barren ground}, meaning: We will turn it, after its adornment, into ruin and destruction, and We will make everything upon it perish, {a barren ground}: that grows nothing and from which no benefit can be derived, as al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas, concerning the saying of the Almighty {And indeed, We will make what is upon it a barren ground}: he says, everything upon it will perish and vanish. Mujahid said: {a barren ground} means a bare wasteland.

Qatadah said: al-sa'id (the ground) is land in which there is neither tree nor plant.

Ibn Zayd said: al-sa'id is land in which there is nothing at all. Do you not see the saying of the Almighty: {Have they not seen that We drive water to the barren land and bring forth thereby crops from which their livestock and they themselves eat? Then do they not see?} [al-Sajdah: 27].

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: {And indeed, We will make what is upon it a barren ground} means the earth, that whatever is upon it is perishing and vanishing, and that the return is indeed to Allah, so do not grieve, and let not what you hear and see sadden you.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُسَلِّيًا رَسُولَهُ ﷺ فِي حُزْنِهِ عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ، لِتَرْكِهِمُ الْإِيمَانَ وَبُعْدِهِمْ عَنْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلا تَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسَرَاتٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ:٨] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَلا تَحْزَنْ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:١٢٧] ، وَقَالَ ﴿لَعَلَّكَ بَاخِعٌ نَفْسَكَ أَلا يَكُونُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:٣] 

بَاخِعٌ: أَيْ مَهْلِكٌ نَفْسَكَ بِحُزْنِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ﴿فَلَعَلَّكَ بَاخِعٌ نَفْسَكَ عَلَى آثَارِهِمْ إِنْ لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنَ ﴿أَسَفًا﴾ يَقُولُ: لَا تُهْلِكْ نَفْسَكَ أَسَفًا.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَاتِل نَفْسَكَ غَضَبًا وَحُزْنًا عَلَيْهِمْ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: جَزَعًا. وَالْمَعْنَى مُتَقَارِبٌ، أَيْ: لَا تَأْسَفْ عَلَيْهِمْ، بَلْ أَبْلِغْهُمْ رِسَالَةَ اللَّهِ، فَمَنِ اهْتَدَى فَلِنَفْسِهِ، وَمَنْ ضَلَّ فَإِنَّمَا يَضِلُّ عَلَيْهَا، فَلَا تَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسَرَاتٍ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ جَعَلَ الدُّنْيَا دَارًا فَانِيَةً مُزيَّنة بِزِينَةٍ زَائِلَةٍ. وَإِنَّمَا جَعَلَهَا دَارَ اخْتِبَارٍ لَا دَارَ قَرَارٍ، فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّا جَعَلْنَا مَا عَلَى الأرْضِ زِينَةً لَهَا لِنَبْلُوَهُمْ أَيُّهُمْ أَحْسَنُ عَمَلا﴾ .

قَالَ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرة، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِنَّ الدُّنْيَا خَضِرَةٌ حُلْوَةٌ وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مُسْتَخْلِفُكُمْ فِيهَا فَنَاظِرٌ مَاذَا تَعْمَلُونَ، فَاتَّقُوا الدُّنْيَا ، وَاتَّقُوا النِّسَاءَ، فَإِنَّ أَوَّلَ فِتْنَةِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ كَانَتْ فِي النِّسَاءِ" 

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى بِزَوَالِهَا وَفَنَائِهَا، وَفَرَاغِهَا وَانْقِضَائِهَا، وَذَهَابِهَا وَخَرَابِهَا، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِنَّا لَجَاعِلُونَ مَا عَلَيْهَا صَعِيدًا جُرُزًا﴾ أَيْ: وَإِنَّا لَمُصَيِّرُوهَا بَعْدَ الزِّينَةِ إِلَى الْخَرَابِ وَالدَّمَارِ، فَنَجْعَلُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ عَلَيْهَا هَالِكًا ﴿صَعِيدًا جُرُزًا﴾ : لَا يُنْبِت وَلَا يُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿وَإِنَّا لَجَاعِلُونَ مَا عَلَيْهَا صَعِيدًا جُرُزًا﴾ يَقُولُ: يَهْلَكُ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ عَلَيْهَا وَيَبِيدُ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿صَعِيدًا جُرُزًا﴾ بَلْقَعًا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: الصَّعِيدُ: الْأَرْضُ الَّتِي لَيْسَ فِيهَا شَجَرٌ وَلَا نَبَاتٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: الصَّعِيدُ: الْأَرْضُ الَّتِي لَيْسَ فِيهَا شَيْءٌ، أَلَا تَرَى إِلَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّا نَسُوقُ الْمَاءَ إِلَى الأرْضِ الْجُرُزِ فَنُخْرِجُ بِهِ زَرْعًا تَأْكُلُ مِنْهُ أَنْعَامُهُمْ وَأَنْفُسُهُمْ أَفَلا يُبْصِرُونَ﴾ [السَّجْدَةِ:٢٧] .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: ﴿وَإِنَّا لَجَاعِلُونَ مَا عَلَيْهَا صَعِيدًا جُرُزًا﴾ يَعْنِي الْأَرْضَ، إِنَّ مَا عَلَيْهَا لِفَانٍ وَبَائِدٌ، وَإِنَّ الْمَرْجِعَ لَإِلَى اللَّهِ فَلَا تَأْسَ ولا يحزنك ما تسمع وترى.

---

## 18:9-12 — verses 9-12 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report about the story of the People of the Cave [and al-Raqim] in summary and abbreviated form, then He elaborates upon it afterward, saying: {Or do you think} meaning: O Muhammad, {that the companions of the cave and al-Raqim were, among Our signs, a wonder} that is, their affair is not something wondrous within Our power and dominion, for the creation of the heavens and the earth, the alternation of night and day, the subjugation of the sun, the moon, and the stars, and other mighty signs pointing to the power of God, exalted is He, and that He is capable of whatever He wills and nothing can render Him incapable, all of that is more wondrous than the reports about the companions of the cave [and al-Raqim]. As Ibn Jurayj said, from Mujahid: {Or do you think that the companions of the cave and al-Raqim were, among Our signs, a wonder} he says: We had signs more wondrous than that!

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: {Or do you think that the companions of the cave and al-Raqim were, among Our signs, a wonder} he says: What I have given you of knowledge, the Sunnah, and the Book is more excellent than the affair of the companions of the cave and al-Raqim.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: What I have made manifest of My proofs upon My servants is more wondrous than the affair of the companions of the cave and al-Raqim.

[As for "the cave," it is the cavern in the mountain, the one to which these mentioned youths took refuge. As for "al-Raqim,"] al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: it is a valley near Aylah. 'Atiyyah al-'Awfi and Qatadah said the same.

Al-Dahhak said: As for "the cave," it is the cavern of the valley, and "al-Raqim" is the name of the valley.

Mujahid said: "al-Raqim" was their building. Some said: it is the valley in which their cave is located.

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Al-Thawri informed us, from Simak, from 'Ikrimah, from Ibn 'Abbas concerning His saying "al-Raqim," he said: Ka'b claims that it is the town.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Ibn 'Abbas: "al-Raqim" is the mountain in which the cave is located.

Ibn Ishaq said, from 'Abdullah ibn Abi Najih, from [Mujahid, from] Ibn 'Abbas, who said: the name of that mountain is Banjalus.

Ibn Jurayj said: Wahb ibn Sulayman informed me, from Shu'ayb al-Jabba'i: that the name of the mountain of the cave is Banjalus, the name of the cave is Hayzam, and the dog is Hamran.

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Isra'il informed us, from Simak, from 'Ikrimah, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: I know the Qur'an except for Hanan, al-Awwah, and al-Raqim.

Ibn Jurayj said: 'Amr ibn Dinar informed me, that he heard 'Ikrimah say: Ibn 'Abbas said: I do not know what al-Raqim is, is it a writing or a building?

'Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn 'Abbas: al-Raqim is the writing. Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: [al-Raqim] is a tablet of stone, on which they wrote the story of the companions of the cave, and then placed it at the door of the cave.

'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: al-Raqim is the writing. Then he recited: {a written record (kitabun marqum)} [al-Mutaffifin: 9]

This is the apparent meaning of the verse, and it is the choice of Ibn Jarir, who said: "al-Raqim" is of the pattern fa'il with the meaning of marqum (written), just as one says of a slain person qatil, and of a wounded person jarih. And God knows best.

His saying: {When the youths took refuge in the cave and said, "Our Lord, grant us mercy from Yourself and prepare for us right guidance in our affair"}. He, exalted is He, informs us about those youths who fled with their religion from their people, so that their people would not tempt them away from it. They fled from them and took refuge in a cave in a mountain to hide from their people. So they said, when they entered, asking God, exalted is He, for His mercy and His kindness toward them: {Our Lord, grant us mercy from Yourself} that is, bestow upon us from Your presence a mercy by which You show mercy to us and conceal us from our people. {And prepare for us right guidance in our affair} that is, decree for us, in this affair of ours, right guidance, meaning: make our outcome one of right guidance, just as it has come in the hadith: "and whatever decree You have decreed for us, make its outcome right guidance." And in the Musnad, from the hadith of Busr ibn Abi Artat, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he used to supplicate: "O Allah, make good our outcome in all our affairs, and protect us from the disgrace of this world and the punishment of the Hereafter."

His saying: {So We sealed their ears in the cave for a number of years} that is, We cast sleep upon them when they entered the cave, and they slept for many years. {Then We raised them up} that is, from that sleep of theirs, and one of them went out with dirhams he had with him to buy food for them to eat, as will come with its explanation and detail. Therefore He said: {Then We raised them up so that We might know which of the two parties} that is, of those who differed concerning them, {better calculated the extent of time they had remained}. It was said: the number, and it was said: the limit, for al-amad means the limit, as in the saying:

The racehorse outstripped when it reached the limit (al-amad).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ قِصَّةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ [وَالرَّقِيمِ] عَلَى سَبِيلِ الْإِجْمَالِ وَالِاخْتِصَارِ، ثُمَّ بَسَطَهَا بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ فَقَالَ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتَ﴾ يَعْنِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿أَنَّ أَصْحَابَ الْكَهْفِ وَالرَّقِيمِ كَانُوا مِنْ آيَاتِنَا عَجَبًا﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ أَمْرُهُمْ عَجِيبًا فِي قُدْرَتِنَا وَسُلْطَانِنَا، فَإِنَّ خلْق السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ، وَاخْتِلَافَ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، وَتَسْخِيرَ الشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ وَالْكَوَاكِبِ، وَغَيْرَ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْعَظِيمَةِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى قُدْرَةِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، وَأَنَّهُ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ قَادِرٌ وَلَا يُعْجِزُهُ شَيْءٌ أَعْجَبُ مِنْ أَخْبَارِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ [وَالرَّقِيمِ] كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتَ أَنَّ أَصْحَابَ الْكَهْفِ وَالرَّقِيمِ كَانُوا مِنْ آيَاتِنَا عَجَبًا﴾ يَقُولُ: قَدْ كَانَ مِنْ آيَاتِنَا مَا هُوَ أَعْجَبُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ!

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتَ أَنَّ أَصْحَابَ الْكَهْفِ وَالرَّقِيمِ كَانُوا مِنْ آيَاتِنَا عَجَبًا﴾ يَقُولُ: الَّذِي آتَيْتُكَ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ وَالسُّنَّةِ وَالْكِتَابِ، أَفْضَلُ مِنْ شَأْنِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ وَالرَّقِيمِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: مَا أَظْهَرْتُ مِنْ حُجَجِي عَلَى الْعِبَادِ، أَعْجَبَ مِنْ شَأْنِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ وَالرَّقِيمِ.

[وَأَمَّا "الْكَهْفُ" فَهُوَ: الْغَارُ فِي الْجَبَلِ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي لَجَأَ إِلَيْهِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْفِتْيَةُ الْمَذْكُورُونَ. وَأَمَّا "الرَّقِيمُ"] فَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ وَادٍ قَرِيبٌ مِنْ أيلَة. وَكَذَا قَالَ عَطِيَّةُ الْعَوْفِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: أَمَّا "الْكَهْفُ" فَهُوَ: غَارُ الْوَادِي، وَ "الرَّقِيمُ": اسْمُ الْوَادِي.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: "الرَّقِيمُ": كَانَ بُنْيَانَهُمْ وَيَقُولُ بَعْضُهُمْ: هُوَ الْوَادِي الَّذِي فِيهِ كَهْفُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: "الرَّقِيمُ"، قَالَ: يَزْعُمُ كَعْبٌ أَنَّهَا الْقَرْيَةُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: "الرَّقِيمُ" الْجَبَلُ الَّذِي فِيهِ الْكَهْفُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ [مُجَاهِدٍ عَنِ] ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: اسْمُ ذَلِكَ الْجَبَلِ بَنْجَلُوسُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: أَخْبَرَنِي وَهْبُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ شُعَيْبٍ الْجَبَّائِيِّ: أَنَّ اسْمَ جَبَلِ الْكَهْفِ بَنْجَلُوسُ، واسم الكهف حيزم، والكلب حمران.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَنْبَأَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ سِمَاكٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: الْقُرْآنُ أَعْلَمُهُ إِلَّا حَنَانًا، وَالْأَوَّاهَ، وَالرَّقِيمَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ عِكْرِمَةَ يَقُولُ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: مَا أَدْرِي مَا الرَّقِيمُ؟ أَكِتَابٌ أَمْ بُنْيَانٌ؟

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الرَّقِيمُ: الْكِتَابُ. وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: [الرَّقِيمُ] لَوْحٌ مِنْ حِجَارَةٍ، كَتَبُوا فِيهِ قِصَصَ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ ثُمَّ وَضَعُوهُ عَلَى بَابِ الْكَهْفِ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: الرَّقِيمُ: الْكِتَابُ. ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿كِتَابٌ مَرْقُومٌ﴾ [الْمُطَفِّفِينَ:٩]

وَهَذَا هُوَ الظَّاهِرُ مِنَ الْآيَةِ، وَهُوَ اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ قَالَ: "الرَّقِيمُ" فَعِيلٌ بِمَعْنَى مَرْقُومٍ، كَمَا يَقُولُ لِلْمَقْتُولِ: قَتِيلٌ، وَلِلْمَجْرُوحِ: جَرِيحٌ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِذْ أَوَى الْفِتْيَةُ إِلَى الْكَهْفِ فَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا آتِنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ رَحْمَةً وَهَيِّئْ لَنَا مِنْ أَمْرِنَا رَشَدًا﴾ يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ أُولَئِكَ الْفِتْيَةِ، الَّذِينَ فَرُّوا بِدِينِهِمْ مِنْ قَوْمِهِمْ لِئَلَّا يَفْتِنُوهُمْ عنه، فَهَرَبوا منه فَلَجَؤُوا إِلَى غَارٍ فِي جَبَلٍ لِيَخْتَفُوا عَنْ قَوْمِهِمْ، فَقَالُوا حِينَ دَخَلُوا سَائِلِينَ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى رَحْمَتَهُ وَلُطْفَهُ بِهِمْ: ﴿رَبَّنَا آتِنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ رَحْمَةً﴾ أَيْ: هَبْ لَنَا مِنْ عِنْدِكَ رَحْمَةً تَرْحَمُنَا بِهَا وَتَسْتُرُنَا عَنْ قَوْمِنَا ﴿وَهَيِّئْ لَنَا مِنْ أَمْرِنَا رَشَدًا﴾ أَيْ: وَقَدِّرْ لَنَا مِنْ أَمْرِنَا هَذَا رَشَدًا، أَيْ: اجْعَلْ عَاقِبَتَنَا رَشَدًا كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "وَمَا قَضَيْتَ لَنَا مِنْ قَضَاءٍ، فَاجْعَلْ عَاقِبَتَهُ رَشَدًا"، وَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ بُسْر بْنِ أَبِي أَرْطَاةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أنه كَانَ يَدْعُو: "اللَّهُمَّ، أَحْسِنْ عَاقِبَتَنَا فِي الْأُمُورِ كُلِّهَا، وَأَجِرْنَا مِنْ خِزْيِ الدُّنْيَا وَعَذَابِ الْآخِرَةِ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَضَرَبْنَا عَلَى آذَانِهِمْ فِي الْكَهْفِ سِنِينَ عَدَدًا﴾ أَيْ: أَلْقَيْنَا عَلَيْهِمُ النَّوْمَ حِينَ دَخَلُوا إِلَى الْكَهْفِ، فَنَامُوا سِنِينَ كَثِيرَةً ﴿ثُمَّ بَعَثْنَاهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ رَقْدَتِهِمْ تِلْكَ، وَخَرَجَ أَحَدُهُمْ بِدَرَاهِمَ مَعَهُ لِيَشْتَرِيَ لَهُمْ بِهَا طَعَامًا يَأْكُلُونَهُ، كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ وَتَفْصِيلُهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ بَعَثْنَاهُمْ لِنَعْلَمَ أَيُّ الْحِزْبَيْنِ﴾ أَيِ: الْمُخْتَلِفَيْنِ فِيهِمْ ﴿أَحْصَى لِمَا لَبِثُوا أَمَدًا﴾ قِيلَ: عَدَدًا وَقِيلَ: غَايَةً فَإِنَّ الْأَمَدَ الْغَايَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ 

سَبَقَ الجَوَاد إذَا اسْتَولى عَلَى الأمَد.

---

## 18:13-16 — verses 13-16 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It is from here that he began to elaborate the story and explain it. He, exalted, mentioned that they were fityah (young men), that is, youths, and that they are more receptive to truth and more guided to the right path than elders who have grown obstinate and hardened in false religion. This is why most of those who responded to Allah and His Messenger ﷺ were young. As for the elders of Quraysh, most of them remained on their religion, and only a few of them accepted Islam. Likewise, Allah, exalted, informed about the People of the Cave that they were young men.

Mujahid said: It has reached me that some of them had earrings in their ears, meaning rings. So Allah inspired them with their right guidance and granted them their piety. {So they believed in their Lord}, meaning: they acknowledged His oneness for Him, and testified that there is no god but He.

{And We increased them in guidance}: More than one of the imams, such as al-Bukhari and others, used this verse and similar ones as evidence for those who held that faith increases and varies in degree, and that it increases and decreases. This is why Allah, exalted, said: {And We increased them in guidance}, just as He said: {And those who are guided, He increases them in guidance and grants them their piety} [Muhammad: 17], and He said: {As for those who believe, it increased them in faith} [al-Tawbah: 124], and He said: {That they may increase in faith along with their faith} [al-Fath: 4], among other verses that indicate this.

It has been mentioned that they were upon the religion of Jesus son of Mary (peace be upon him), and Allah knows best. The apparent view is that they were entirely before the Christian religion, for if they had been upon Christianity, the rabbis of the Jews would not have concerned themselves with preserving news of them and their affair, given their divergence from them. It has already been mentioned from Ibn Abbas that Quraysh sent to the rabbis of the Jews in Madinah seeking things with which to test the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, so they sent word to them to ask him about the story of these people, and about the story of Dhu al-Qarnayn, and about the spirit. This indicates that this matter was preserved in the books of the People of the Book, and that it predates the Christian religion. And Allah knows best.

His saying: {And We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and said: Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth} means: Allah, exalted, gave them patience to oppose their people and their city, and to part with the comfortable life, happiness, and blessing in which they had been living. For more than one of the commentators among the earlier and later scholars mentioned that they were sons of the kings and nobles of Rome, and that they went out one day during one of their people's festivals. They had a yearly gathering in which they assembled on the outskirts of the town, and they used to worship idols and false deities and sacrifice to them. They had a tyrannical, obstinate king called "Decius," who commanded the people to do this, urged them to it, and called them to it. When the people went out for their gathering, and these young men went out with their fathers and their people, and they looked with the eye of insight at what their people were doing, they realized that what their people were doing, prostrating to their idols and sacrificing to them, was not fitting for anyone except Allah, who created the heavens and the earth. So each one of them began to slip away from his people, withdrawing from them and setting himself apart in a corner. The first of them to sit alone sat under the shade of a tree. Then another came and sat beside him, then another came and sat with the two of them, then another came and sat with them, then another came, then another came, then another came, and none of them knew the other. Rather, what gathered them there was that which had united their hearts upon faith, as has come in the hadith which al-Bukhari related as a mu'allaq (suspended report), from the hadith of Yahya ibn Sa'id, from Amrah, from A'ishah, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Souls are troops mustered together. Those among them that recognize one another become friendly, and those that do not recognize one another become discordant." Muslim also related it in his Sahih from the hadith of Suhayl, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ.

And people say: shared nature is the cause of joining together.

The point is that each one of them began to conceal his condition from his companions, out of fear of them, not knowing that they were like him, until one of them said: "By Allah, O my people, you know that nothing has driven you out from among your people and set you apart from them except something particular, so let each one of you reveal his affair." Another said: "As for me, by Allah, I saw what my people were upon and I recognized that it was false. Rather, the One who deserves to be worshipped alone, with nothing associated with Him, is Allah who created everything: the heavens and the earth and what is between them." Another said: "And I, by Allah, experienced the same thing." And another said likewise, until they all agreed upon a single word. So they became as one hand and true brothers. They took for themselves a place of worship in which to worship Allah. Their people came to know of them and reported their matter to their king. He summoned them before him and asked them about their affair and what they held, and they answered him with the truth and called him to Allah, mighty and majestic. This is why Allah, exalted, informed about them in His saying: {And We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and said: Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth. We will never call upon any god besides Him}. "Never" here is for the negation of eternity, meaning: this will never occur from us, for if we did that it would be false. This is why He said about them: {We would then have said an outrageous thing}, meaning: falsehood, lying, and slander.

{These, our people, have taken besides Him gods. Why do they not bring some clear authority concerning them?} meaning: why did they not establish a clear, valid proof for the correctness of what they had adopted? {So who is more unjust than one who invents a lie against Allah?} They are saying: rather, they are wrongdoers, liars in that claim of theirs. It is said that when their king called them to believe in Allah, he refused them, threatened them, and warned them, and ordered that the clothing they wore, which was the adornment of their people, be stripped from them, and he gave them a period of time to reconsider their affair, hoping that they might return to the religion they had been upon. This was a kindness from Allah toward them, for during that respite they found a way to flee from him and to escape with their religion from the trial.

This is the prescribed course when trials befall people: that the servant flee from them out of fear for his religion, as has come in the hadith: "It is nearly the case that the best wealth of one of you will be sheep which he follows to the peaks of the mountains and the places where rain falls, fleeing with his religion from the trials." In this case, withdrawal from people is prescribed, but it is not prescribed otherwise, because of what would be lost thereby, namely the abandonment of the congregational prayers and the Friday prayers.

When their resolve to go and flee from their people was settled, and Allah, exalted, chose that for them, and informed about them concerning that in His saying: {And when you have withdrawn from them and from what they worship besides Allah}, meaning: when you have separated from them and opposed them in your religion regarding their worship of other than Allah, then separate from them also with your bodies, {then take refuge in the cave; your Lord will spread over you something of His mercy}, meaning: He will extend over you a mercy by which He will conceal you from your people, {and will prepare for you a facility in your affair}, meaning the affair you are in, {mirfaqan}, meaning: something by which you may find ease. At that point they went out fleeing to the cave and took refuge in it. Their people missed them from among themselves, and the king searched for them. It is said that he did not succeed in finding them, and Allah obscured their trace from him, just as He did with His Prophet [Muhammad] ﷺ and his companion al-Siddiq, when he took refuge in the cave of Thawr, and the polytheists of Quraysh came searching, yet they were not guided to him even though they passed right by it. At that time, the Prophet ﷺ, when he saw the distress of al-Siddiq in his saying, "O Messenger of Allah, if one of them were to look at the place of his feet he would see us," said: "O Abu Bakr, what do you think of two, the third of whom is Allah?" Allah, exalted, has said: {If you do not aid him, Allah has already aided him when those who disbelieved drove him out, the second of two, when they were in the cave, when he said to his companion, 'Do not grieve, indeed Allah is with us.' Then Allah sent down His tranquility upon him and supported him with troops you did not see, and made the word of those who disbelieved the lowest, while the word of Allah is the highest, and Allah is Mighty, Wise} [al-Tawbah: 40]. So the story of this cave is nobler, greater, more magnificent, and more wondrous than the story of the People of the Cave. And it has been said that their people did succeed in finding them, and stood at the entrance of the cave which they had entered, and said: "We do not wish to inflict upon them any punishment greater than what they have already done to themselves." So the king ordered that the entrance be sealed over them so that they would perish in their place, and this was done to them. But there is something questionable in this, and Allah knows best, for Allah, exalted, has informed that the sun entered upon them in the cave morning and evening, as He, exalted, said:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

مِنْ هَاهُنَا شَرَعَ فِي بَسْطِ الْقِصَّةِ وَشَرْحِهَا، فَذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ فِتْيَةٌ -وَهُمُ الشَّبَابُ-وَهُمْ أَقْبَلُ لِلْحَقِّ، وَأَهْدَى لِلسَّبِيلِ مِنَ الشُّيُوخِ، الَّذِينَ قَدْ عَتَوْا وعَسَوا فِي دِينِ الْبَاطِلِ؛ وَلِهَذَا كَانَ أَكْثَرُ الْمُسْتَجِيبِينَ لِلَّهِ وَلِرَسُولِهِ ﷺ شَبَابًا. وَأَمَّا الْمَشَايِخُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ، فَعَامَّتُهُمْ بَقُوا عَلَى دِينِهِمْ، وَلَمْ يُسْلِمْ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا الْقَلِيلُ. وَهَكَذَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا فِتْيَةً شَبَابًا.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُ كَانَ فِي آذَانِ بَعْضْهِمُ الْقِرَطَةُ يَعْنِي: الحَلَق فَأَلْهَمَهُمُ اللَّهُ رُشْدَهُمْ وَآتَاهُمْ تَقْوَاهُمْ. فَآمَنُوا بِرَبِّهِمْ، أَيْ: اعْتَرَفُوا لَهُ بِالْوَحْدَانِيَّةِ، وَشَهِدُوا أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ.

﴿وَزِدْنَاهُمْ هُدًى﴾ : اسْتَدَلَّ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ وَأَمْثَالِهَا غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ كَالْبُخَارِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِ مِمَّنْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى زِيَادَةِ الْإِيمَانِ وَتَفَاضُلِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ يَزِيدُ وَيَنْقُصُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَزِدْنَاهُمْ هُدًى﴾ كَمَا قَالَ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ اهْتَدَوْا زَادَهُمْ هُدًى وَآتَاهُمْ تَقْوَاهُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ:١٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فَزَادَتْهُمْ إِيمَانًا﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:١٢٤] ، وَقَالَ ﴿لِيَزْدَادُوا إِيمَانًا مَعَ إِيمَانِهِمْ﴾ [الْفَتْحِ:٤] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ.

وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا عَلَى دِينِ عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَبْلَ مِلَّةِ النَّصْرَانِيَّةِ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَوْ كَانُوا عَلَى دِينِ النَّصْرَانِيَّةِ، لَمَا اعْتَنَى أَحْبَارُ الْيَهُودِ بِحِفْظِ خَبَرِهِمْ وَأَمْرِهِمْ، لِمُبَايِنَتِهِمْ لَهُمْ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّ قُرَيْشًا بَعَثُوا إِلَى أَحْبَارِ الْيَهُودِ بِالْمَدِينَةِ يَطْلُبُونَ مِنْهُمْ أَشْيَاءَ يَمْتَحِنُونَ بِهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَبَعَثُوا إِلَيْهِمْ أَنْ يَسْأَلُوهُ عَنْ خَبَرِ هَؤُلَاءِ، وَعَنْ خَبَرِ ذِي الْقَرْنَيْنِ، وَعَنِ الرُّوحِ، فَدَلَّ هَذَا عَلَى أَنَّ هَذَا أَمْرٌ مَحْفُوظٌ فِي كُتُبِ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، وَأَنَّهُ مُتَقَدِّمٌ عَلَى دِينِ النَّصْرَانِيَّةِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَرَبَطْنَا عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ إِذْ قَامُوا فَقَالُوا رَبُّنَا رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وصَبَّرناهم عَلَى مُخَالَفَةِ قَوْمِهِمْ وَمَدِينَتِهِمْ، وَمُفَارَقَةِ مَا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْعَيْشِ الرَّغِيدِ وَالسَّعَادَةِ وَالنِّعْمَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ ذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا مِنْ أَبْنَاءِ مُلُوكِ الرُّومِ وَسَادَتِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ خَرَجُوا يَوْمًا فِي بَعْضِ أَعْيَادِ قَوْمِهِمْ، وَكَانَ لَهُمْ مُجْتَمَعٌ فِي السَّنَةِ يَجْتَمِعُونَ فِيهِ فِي ظَاهِرِ الْبَلَدِ، وَكَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ الْأَصْنَامَ وَالطَّوَاغِيتَ، وَيَذْبَحُونَ لَهَا، وَكَانَ لَهُمْ مَلِكٌ جَبَّارٌ عَنِيدٌ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "دَقْيَانُوسُ"، وَكَانَ يَأْمُرُ النَّاسَ بِذَلِكَ وَيَحُثُّهُمْ عَلَيْهِ وَيَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَيْهِ. فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ النَّاسُ لِمُجْتَمَعِهِمْ ذَلِكَ، وَخَرَجَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْفِتْيَةُ مَعَ آبَائِهِمْ وَقَوْمِهِمْ، وَنَظَرُوا إِلَى مَا يَصْنَعُ قَوْمُهُمْ بِعَيْنِ بَصِيرَتِهِمْ، عَرَفُوا أَنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي يَصْنَعُهُ قَوْمُهُمْ مِنَ السُّجُودِ لِأَصْنَامِهِمْ وَالذَّبْحِ لَهَا، لَا يَنْبَغِي إِلَّا لِلَّهِ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ. فَجَعَلَ كُلُّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمْ يَتَخَلَّصُ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، وَيَنْحَازُ مِنْهُمْ وَيَتَبَرَّزُ عَنْهُمْ نَاحِيَةً. فَكَانَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ جَلَسَ مِنْهُمْ [وَحْدَهُ] أَحَدَهُمْ، جَلَسَ تَحْتَ ظِلِّ شَجَرَةٍ، فَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ فَجَلَسَ عِنْدَهُ، وَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ فَجَلَسَ إِلَيْهِمَا، وَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ فَجَلَسَ إِلَيْهِمْ، وَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ، وَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ، وَجَاءَ الْآخَرُ، وَلَا يَعْرِفُ وَاحِدٌ مِنْهُمُ الْآخَرَ، وَإِنَّمَا جَمَعَهُمْ هُنَاكَ الَّذِي جَمَعَ قُلُوبَهُمْ عَلَى الْإِيمَانِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ تَعْلِيقًا، مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ عَمْرَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الْأَرْوَاحُ جُنُودٌ مُجَنَّدة، فَمَا تَعَارَفَ مِنْهَا ائْتَلَفَ، وَمَا تَنَاكَرَ مِنْهَا اخْتَلَفَ" . وَأَخْرَجَهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُهَيْلٍ عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ .

وَالنَّاسُ يَقُولُونَ: الْجِنْسِيَّةُ عِلَّةُ الضَّمِّ.

وَالْغَرَضُ أَنَّهُ جَعَلَ كُلَّ أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ يَكْتُمُ مَا هُوَ فِيهِ عَنْ أَصْحَابِهِ، خَوْفًا مِنْهُمْ، وَلَا يَدْرِي أَنَّهُمْ مِثْلُهُ، حَتَّى قَالَ أَحَدُهُمْ: تَعْلَمُونَ -وَاللَّهِ يَا قَوْمِ-إِنَّهُ مَا أَخْرَجَكُمْ مِنْ قَوْمِكُمْ وَأَفْرَدَكُمْ عَنْهُمْ، إِلَّا شَيْءٌ فليظهر كل واحد منكم بِأَمْرِهِ. فَقَالَ آخَرُ: أَمَّا أَنَا فَإِنِّي [وَاللَّهِ] رَأَيْتُ مَا قَوْمِي عَلَيْهِ، فَعَرَفْتُ أَنَّهُ بَاطِلٌ، وَإِنَّمَا الَّذِي يَسْتَحِقُّ أَنْ يُعْبَدَ [وَحْدَهُ] وَلَا يُشْرَكَ بِهِ شَيْءٌ هُوَ اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ: السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا. وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ: وَأَنَا وَاللَّهِ وَقَعَ لِي كَذَلِكَ. وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ كَذَلِكَ، حَتَّى تَوَافَقُوا كُلُّهُمْ عَلَى كَلِمَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ، فَصَارُوا يَدًا وَاحِدَةً وَإِخْوَانَ صِدْقٍ، فَاتَّخَذُوا لَهُمْ مَعْبَدًا يَعْبُدُونَ اللَّهَ فِيهِ، فَعَرَفَ بِهِمْ قَوْمُهُمْ، فَوَشَوْا بِأَمْرِهِمْ إِلَى مَلِكِهِمْ، فَاسْتَحْضَرَهُمْ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ فَسَأَلَهُمْ عَنْ أَمْرِهِمْ وَمَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ فَأَجَابُوهُ بِالْحَقِّ، وَدَعَوْهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْهُمْ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَرَبَطْنَا عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ إِذْ قَامُوا فَقَالُوا رَبُّنَا رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ لَنْ نَدْعُوَ مِنْ دُونِهِ إِلَهًا﴾ ولن: لِنَفْيِ التَّأْبِيدِ، أَيْ: لَا يَقَعُ مِنَّا هَذَا أَبَدًا؛ لِأَنَّا لَوْ فَعَلْنَا ذَلِكَ لَكَانَ بَاطِلًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ عَنْهُمْ: ﴿لَقَدْ قُلْنَا إِذًا شَطَطًا﴾ أَيْ: باطِلا وَكَذِبًا وَبُهْتَانًا.

﴿هَؤُلاءِ قَوْمُنَا اتَّخَذُوا مِنْ دُونِهِ آلِهَةً لَوْلا يَأْتُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِسُلْطَانٍ بَيِّنٍ﴾ أَيْ: هَلا أَقَامُوا عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا ذَهَبُوا إِلَيْهِ دَلِيلًا وَاضِحًا صَحِيحًا؟! ﴿فَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا﴾ يَقُولُونَ: بَلْ هُمْ ظَالِمُونَ كَاذِبُونَ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ ذَلِكَ، فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّ مَلِكَهُمْ لَمَّا دَعَوْهُ إِلَى الْإِيمَانِ بِاللَّهِ، أَبَى عَلَيْهِمْ، وتَهَدّدهم وَتَوَعَّدَهُمْ، وَأَمَرَ بِنَزْعِ لِبَاسِهِمْ عَنْهُمُ الَّذِي كَانَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ زِينَةِ قَوْمِهِمْ، وأجَّلهم لِيَنْظُرُوا فِي أَمْرِهِمْ، لَعَلَّهُمْ يُرَاجِعُونَ دِينَهُمُ الَّذِي كَانُوا عَلَيْهِ. وَكَانَ هَذَا مِنْ لُطْفِ اللَّهِ بِهِمْ، فَإِنَّهُمْ فِي تِلْكَ النَّظْرَةِ تَوَصَّلُوا إِلَى الْهَرَبِ مِنْهُ. وَالْفِرَارِ بِدِينِهِمْ مِنَ الْفِتْنَةِ.

وَهَذَا هُوَ الْمَشْرُوعُ عِنْدَ وُقُوعِ الْفِتَنِ فِي النَّاسِ، أَنْ يَفِرَّ الْعَبْدُ مِنْهُمْ خَوْفًا عَلَى دينه، كما جاء في الْحَدِيثِ: "يُوشِكُ أَنْ يَكُونَ خيرُ مَالِ أَحَدِكُمْ غَنَمًا يَتْبَعُ بِهَا شَغَفَ الْجِبَالِ وَمَوَاقِعَ القَطْر، يَفِرُّ بِدِينِهِ مِنَ الْفِتَنِ" فَفِي هَذِهِ الْحَالِ تُشْرَعُ الْعُزْلَةُ عَنِ النَّاسِ، وَلَا تُشْرَعُ فِيمَا عَدَاهَا، لِمَا يَفُوتُ بِهَا مِنْ تَرْكِ الْجَمَاعَاتِ وَالْجُمَعِ.

فَلَمَّا وَقَعَ عَزْمُهُمْ عَلَى الذَّهَابِ وَالْهَرَبِ مِنْ قَوْمِهِمْ، وَاخْتَارَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهُمْ ذَلِكَ، وَأَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ بِذَلِكَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذِ اعْتَزَلْتُمُوهُمْ وَمَا يَعْبُدُونَ إِلا اللَّهَ﴾ أَيْ: وَإِذَا فَارَقْتُمُوهُمْ وَخَالَفْتُمُوهُمْ بِأَدْيَانِكُمْ فِي عِبَادَتِهِمْ غَيْرَ اللَّهِ، فَفَارِقُوهُمْ أَيْضًا بِأَبْدَانِكُمْ ﴿فَأْوُوا إِلَى الْكَهْفِ يَنْشُرْ لَكُمْ رَبُّكُمْ مِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: يَبْسُطْ عَلَيْكُمْ رَحْمَةً يَسْتُرُكُمْ بِهَا مِنْ قَوْمِكُمْ ﴿وَيُهَيِّئْ لَكُمْ مِنْ أَمْرِكُمْ﴾ [أَيِ] الَّذِي أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ، ﴿مِرفَقًا﴾ أَيْ: أَمْرًا تَرْتَفِقُونَ بِهِ. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ خَرَجُوا هُرابًا إِلَى الْكَهْفِ، فَأَوَوْا إِلَيْهِ، فَفَقَدَهُمْ قَوْمُهُمْ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، وتَطَلَّبهم الْمَلِكُ فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ لَمْ يَظْفَرْ بِهِمْ، وعَمَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ خَبَرَهُمْ. كَمَا فَعَلَ بِنَبِيِّهِ [مُحَمَّدٍ] ﷺ وَصَاحِبِهِ الصِّدِّيقِ، حِينَ لَجَأَ إِلَى غَارِ ثَوْرٍ، وَجَاءَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ فِي الطَّلَبِ، فَلَمْ يَهْتَدُوا إِلَيْهِ مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ يَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهِ، وَعِنْدَهَا قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ حِينَ رَأَى جَزَعَ الصِّدِّيقِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَوْ أَنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ نَظَرَ إِلَى مَوْضِعِ قَدَمَيْهِ لَأَبْصَرَنَا، فَقَالَ: "يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ، مَا ظَنُّكَ بِاثْنَيْنِ اللَّهُ ثَالِثُهُمَا؟ "، وَقَدْ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِلا تَنْصُرُوهُ فَقَدْ نَصَرَهُ اللَّهُ إِذْ أَخْرَجَهُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا ثَانِيَ اثْنَيْنِ إِذْ هُمَا فِي الْغَارِ إِذْ يَقُولُ لِصَاحِبِهِ لَا تَحْزَنْ إِنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَنَا فَأَنزلَ اللَّهُ سَكِينَتَهُ عَلَيْهِ وَأَيَّدَهُ بِجُنُودٍ لَمْ تَرَوْهَا وَجَعَلَ كَلِمَةَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا السُّفْلَى وَكَلِمَةُ اللَّهِ هِيَ الْعُلْيَا وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٤٠] فَقِصَّةُ هَذَا الْغَارِ أَشْرَفُ وَأَجَلُّ وَأَعْظَمُ وَأَعْجَبُ مِنْ قِصَّةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ، وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ قَوْمَهُمْ ظَفِرُوا بِهِمْ، وَقَفُوا عَلَى بَابِ الْغَارِ الَّذِي دَخَلُوهُ، فَقَالُوا: مَا كُنَّا نُرِيدُ مِنْهُمْ مَنِ الْعُقُوبَةِ أَكْثَرَ مِمَّا فَعَلُوا بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ. فَأَمَرَ الْمَلِكُ بِرَدْمِ بَابِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ لِيَهْلَكُوا مَكَانَهُمْ فَفُعِلَ [لَهُمْ] ذَلِكَ. وَفِي هَذَا نَظَرٌ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَدْ أَخْبَرَ أَنَّ الشَّمْسَ تَدْخُلُ عَلَيْهِمْ فِي الْكَهْفِ بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيَّةً، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى:

---

## 18:17 — verse 17

### Translation

This is evidence that the entrance of this cave faced the north, because He, Exalted is He, informed us that when the sun entered upon them at its rising, it inclined away from it, {to the right}, meaning the shadow contracted toward the right, as Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and Qatadah said: {tazawaru} means "it inclines." That is because the higher the sun rose in the horizon, its rays would contract as it rose, until nothing of it remained at midday in a place such as that. This is why He said: {and when it set, it passed beside them on the left}, meaning it entered their cave from the left side of its entrance, which is from the direction of the east. This proves the correctness of what we have said, and this is clear to whoever reflects upon it and has knowledge of astronomy and the movement of the sun, moon, and stars.

The explanation of this is that if the entrance of the cave had faced the east, nothing of the sun would have entered it at sunset. And if it had faced the direction of the qiblah, nothing would have entered it either at sunrise or at sunset, and the shadow would not have inclined either to the right or to the left. And if it had faced the west, the sun would not have entered it at the time of sunrise, but only after midday, and would have remained in it until sunset. Thus what we have stated is confirmed to be the case, and praise belongs to God.

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and Qatadah said: {taqriduhum} means "it left them alone."

God, Exalted is He, informed us of this and intended for us to understand and reflect upon it, but He did not inform us of the location of this cave, in which of the lands of the earth it was, since there is no benefit for us in that and no legislative purpose in it. Some of the commentators have nonetheless taken pains over it and mentioned various sayings about it. It was mentioned earlier from Ibn Abbas that he said: it is near Aylah. Ibn Ishaq said: it is near Nineveh. It has also been said: in the land of the Byzantines (Rum). And it has been said: in the land of al-Balqa. God knows best in which of God's lands it actually is. Had there been for us in it some benefit of religion, God and His Messenger would have guided us to it, for the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I have not left anything that would bring you closer to Paradise and take you further from the Fire, except that I have informed you of it." So He, Exalted is He, informed us of its description but did not inform us of its location. He said: {and you would see the sun, when it rose, inclining away from their cave}. Malik reported from Zayd ibn Aslam: it inclines {to the right, and when it set, it passed beside them on the left, while they were in a wide space within it}, meaning in a spacious area inside it, in a manner such that the sun did not touch them, for had it touched them it would have burned their bodies and their clothing, as Ibn Abbas said.

{That is among the signs of God}, in that He, Exalted is He, guided them to this cave in which He kept them alive, while the sun and the wind entered upon them in it so that their bodies would be preserved. This is why He said: {That is among the signs of God}.

Then He said: {Whomever God guides is the rightly guided, and whomever He leaves to stray, you will never find for him a protecting guide}, meaning He is the One who guided these youths to right guidance from among their own people, for whoever God guides is truly guided, and whoever He leads astray has no guide at all.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا دَلِيلٌ عَلَى أَنَّ بَابَ هَذَا الْكَهْفِ مِنْ نَحْوِ الشَّمَالِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى أَخْبَرَ أَنَّ الشَّمْسَ إِذَا دَخَلَتْهُ عِنْدَ طُلُوعِهَا تَزَاوَرُ عَنْهُ ﴿ذَاتَ الْيَمِينِ﴾ أَيْ: يَتَقَلَّصُ الْفَيْءُ يَمْنَةً كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ: ﴿تَزَاوَرُ﴾ أَيْ: تَمِيلُ؛ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهَا كُلَّمَا ارْتَفَعَتْ فِي الْأُفُقِ تَقَلَّصَ شُعَاعُهَا بِارْتِفَاعِهَا حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ عِنْدَ الزَّوَالِ فِي مِثْلِ ذَلِكَ الْمَكَانِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا غَرَبَتْ تَقْرِضُهُمْ ذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ﴾ أَيْ: تَدْخُلُ إِلَى غَارِهِمْ مِنْ شِمَالِ بَابِهِ، وَهُوَ مِنْ نَاحِيَةِ الْمَشْرِقِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا قُلْنَاهُ، وَهَذَا بَيِّنٌ لِمَنْ تَأَمَّلَهُ وَكَانَ لَهُ عِلْمٌ بِمَعْرِفَةِ الْهَيْئَةِ، وَسَيْرِ الشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ وَالْكَوَاكِبِ، وَبَيَانُهُ أَنَّهُ لَوْ كَانَ بَابُ الْغَارِ مِنْ نَاحِيَةِ الشَّرْقِ لَمَا دَخَلَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ عِنْدَ الْغُرُوبِ، وَلَوْ كَانَ مِنْ نَاحِيَةِ الْقِبْلَةِ لَمَا دَخَلَ مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ عِنْدَ الطُّلُوعِ وَلَا عِنْدَ الْغُرُوبِ، وَلَا تَزَاوَرَ الْفَيْءُ يَمِينًا وَلَا شِمَالًا وَلَوْ كَانَ مِنْ جِهَةِ الْغَرْبِ لَمَا دَخَلَتْهُ وَقْتَ الطُّلُوعِ، بَلْ بَعْدَ الزَّوَالِ وَلَمْ تَزَلْ فِيهِ إِلَى الْغُرُوبِ. فَتَعَيَّنَ مَا ذَكَرْنَاهُ وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ: ﴿تَقْرِضُهُمْ﴾ تَتْرُكُهُمْ.

وَقَدْ أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِذَلِكَ وَأَرَادَ مِنَّا فَهْمَهُ وَتَدَبُّرَهُ، وَلَمْ يُخْبِرْنَا بِمَكَانِ هَذَا الْكَهْفِ فِي أَيِّ الْبِلَادِ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ؛ إِذْ لَا فَائِدَةٌ لَنَا فِيهِ وَلَا قَصْدٌ شَرْعِيٌّ. وَقَدْ تَكَلَّفَ بَعْضُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ فَذَكَرُوا فِيهِ أَقْوَالًا فَتَقَدَّمَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: [هُوَ] قَرِيبٌ مِنْ أَيْلَةَ. وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُوَ عِنْدَ نِينَوَى. وَقِيلَ: بِبِلَادِ الرُّومِ. وَقِيلَ: بِبِلَادِ الْبَلْقَاءِ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِأَيِّ بِلَادِ اللَّهِ هُوَ. وَلَوْ كَانَ لَنَا فِيهِ مَصْلَحَةٌ دِينِيَّةٌ لَأَرْشَدْنَا اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ إِلَيْهِ فَقَدْ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا تَرَكْتُ شَيْئًا يُقَرِّبُكُمْ إِلَى [الْجَنَّةِ] وَيُبَاعِدُكُمْ مِنَ النَّارِ، إِلَّا وَقَدْ أَعْلَمْتُكُمْ بِهِ". فَأَعْلَمَنَا تَعَالَى بِصِفَتِهِ، وَلَمْ يُعْلِمْنَا بِمَكَانِهِ، فَقَالَ ﴿وَتَرَى الشَّمْسَ إِذَا طَلَعَتْ تَزَاوَرُ عَنْ كَهْفِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: تَمِيلُ ﴿ذَاتَ الْيَمِينِ وَإِذَا غَرَبَتْ تَقْرِضُهُمْ ذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ وَهُمْ فِي فَجْوَةٍ مِنْهُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي مُتَّسَعٍ مِنْهُ دَاخِلًا بِحَيْثُ لَا تَمَسُّهُمْ؛ إِذْ لَوْ أَصَابَتْهُمْ لَأَحْرَقَتْ أَبْدَانَهُمْ وَثِيَابَهُمْ قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ.

﴿ذَلِكَ مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ﴾ حَيْثُ أَرْشَدَهُمْ تَعَالَى إِلَى هَذَا الْغَارِ الَّذِي جَعَلَهُمْ فِيهِ أَحْيَاءً، وَالشَّمْسُ وَالرِّيحُ تَدْخُلُ عَلَيْهِمْ فِيهِ لِتَبْقَى أَبْدَانُهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ يَهْدِ اللَّهُ فَهُوَ الْمُهْتَدِ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلْ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ وَلِيًّا مُرْشِدًا﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الَّذِي أَرْشَدَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْفِتْيَةَ إِلَى الْهِدَايَةِ مِنْ بَيْنِ قَوْمِهِمْ، فَإِنَّهُ مَنْ هَدَاهُ اللَّهُ اهْتَدَى، وَمَنْ أَضَلَّهُ فَلَا هَادِيَ لَهُ.

---

## 18:18 — verse 18

### Translation

Some of the people of knowledge mentioned that when Allah struck their ears with sleep, their eyes did not close, so that decay would not hasten to them; for if they remained open to the air, that would preserve them better. This is why the Almighty said: {and you would think them awake while they are asleep}. It has been mentioned regarding the wolf that it sleeps by closing one eye and opening the other, then opens this one and closes that one while it remains asleep, as the poet said: "He sleeps with one of his eyes and guards with the other against calamities, so he is awake while asleep."

Concerning the Almighty's saying, {and We turn them over to the right side and to the left side}: some of the predecessors said they are turned over twice a year. Ibn Abbas said: had they not been turned over, the earth would have consumed them.

Concerning His saying, {and their dog was stretching out his forelegs at the threshold (al-wasid)}: Ibn Abbas, Qatadah, Mujahid, and Sa'id ibn Jubayr said that al-wasid means the courtyard (al-fina').

Ibn Abbas said: at the door. It has also been said: on the bare ground (al-sa'id), that is, the dust. The correct view is that it means the courtyard, that is, the door. This is related to the Almighty's saying, {indeed it will be closed upon them} [al-Humazah: 8], meaning shut and locked. It is said both "wasid" and "asid."

Their dog crouched at the door, as is the habit of dogs.

Ibn Jurayj said: he guarded the door for them. This was from his nature and disposition, in that he crouched at their door as though guarding them, and his sitting was outside the door, because the angels do not enter a house in which there is a dog, as has come in the authentic hadith, nor one in which there is an image, nor one in which there is a person in a state of ritual impurity (janabah), nor a disbeliever, as has come in the hasan (sound) hadith. Their blessing encompassed their dog, so that what befell them of sleep in that state befell him as well. This is the benefit of the companionship of the righteous: this dog thereby acquired mention, report, and standing.

It has been said that he was a hunting dog belonging to one of them, and this is the more likely view. It has also been said that he was the dog of the king's cook, who had agreed with them in religion, so his dog accompanied him. Allah knows best.

Al-Hafiz Ibn Asakir narrated, in the biographical entry on "Hammam ibn al-Walid al-Dimashqi": [chain] ... Sadaqah ibn Umar al-Ghassani told us, Abbad al-Minqari told us, I heard al-Hasan al-Basri, may Allah have mercy on him, say: the name of Ibrahim's ram was Jarir, the name of Sulayman's hoopoe was Anqaz, the name of the dog of the People of the Cave was Qitmir, and the name of the calf of the Children of Israel which they worshipped was Bahmut. Adam (peace be upon him) descended in India, Hawwa' in Jeddah, Iblis in the plain of Baysan, and the serpent in Isfahan.

It has already been mentioned regarding Shu'ayb al-Jubba'i that he named him Himran.

They differed regarding his color, holding various opinions that amount to nothing, have no benefit beneath them, no evidence for them, and no need for them. Rather, this is among what is forbidden, for their basis is mere conjecture about the unseen (rajm bi'l-ghayb).

Concerning the Almighty's saying, {had you looked upon them, you would have turned away from them in flight, and you would have been filled with terror of them}: that is, the Almighty cast awe over them such that no one's gaze would fall upon them without being overawed, because of the awe and dread with which they were clothed, so that no one would draw near them, nor would the hand of any toucher touch them, until the decree reached its appointed term and their sleep, which the Blessed and Almighty willed for them, came to its end, for the sake of the proof and far-reaching wisdom and vast mercy that He has in that.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ذَكَرَ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ أَنَّهُمْ لَمَّا ضَرَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَى آذَانِهِمْ بِالنَّوْمِ، لَمْ تَنْطَبِقْ أَعْيُنُهُمْ؛ لِئَلَّا يُسْرِعَ إِلَيْهَا الْبِلَى، فَإِذَا بَقِيَتْ ظَاهِرَةً لِلْهَوَاءِ كَانَ أَبْقَى لَهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَحْسَبُهُمْ أَيْقَاظًا وَهُمْ رُقُودٌ﴾ وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ عَنِ الذِّئْبِ أَنَّهُ يَنَامُ فَيُطْبِقُ عَيْنًا وَيَفْتَحُ عَيْنًا، ثُمَّ يَفْتَحُ هَذِهِ وَيُطْبِقُ هذه وهو راقد، كما قال الشاعر يَنَامُ بإحْدَى مُقْلتَيه وَيَتَّقِي ... بأخْرَى الرَّزَايَا فَهْوَ يَقْظَانُ نَائِمُ ...

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنُقَلِّبُهُمْ ذَاتَ الْيَمِينِ وَذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: يُقَلَّبُونَ فِي الْعَامِ مَرَّتَيْنِ. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: لَوْ لَمْ يُقَلَّبُوا لَأَكْلَتْهُمُ الْأَرْضُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَلْبُهُمْ بَاسِطٌ ذِرَاعَيْهِ بِالْوَصِيدِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ الْوَصِيدُ: الْفِنَاءُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: بِالْبَابِ. وَقِيلَ: بِالصَّعِيدِ، وَهُوَ التُّرَابُ. وَالصَّحِيحُ أَنَّهُ بِالْفِنَاءِ، وَهُوَ الْبَابُ، وَمِنْهُ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّهَا عَلَيْهِمْ مُؤْصَدَةٌ﴾ [الْهُمَزَةِ: ٨] أَيْ: مُطْبَقَةٌ مُغْلَقَةٌ. وَيُقَالُ: "وَصِيد" وَ "أَصِيدٌ".

رَبَضَ كَلْبُهُمْ عَلَى الْبَابِ كَمَا جَرَتْ بِهِ عَادَةُ الْكِلَابِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ يَحْرُسُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْبَابَ. وَهَذَا مِنْ سَجِيَّتِهِ وَطَبِيعَتِهِ، حَيْثُ يَرْبِضُ بِبَابِهِمْ كَأَنَّهُ يَحْرُسُهُمْ، وَكَانَ جُلُوسُهُ خَارِجَ الْبَابِ؛ لِأَنَّ الْمَلَائِكَةَ لَا تَدْخُلُ بَيْتًا فِيهِ كَلْبٌ -كَمَا وَرَدَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ -وَلَا صُورَةٌ وَلَا جُنُب وَلَا كَافِرٌ، كَمَا وَرَدَ بِهِ الْحَدِيثُ الْحَسَنُ وَشَمَلَتْ كَلْبَهُمْ بَرَكَتُهُمْ، فَأَصَابَهُ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ مِنَ النَّوْمِ عَلَى تِلْكَ الْحَالِ. وَهَذَا فَائِدَةُ صُحْبَةِ الْأَخْيَارِ؛ فَإِنَّهُ صَارَ لِهَذَا الْكَلْبِ ذِكْرٌ وَخَبَرٌ وَشَأْنٌ.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ كَلْبَ صَيْدٍ لِأَحَدِهِمْ، وَهُوَ الْأَشْبَهُ. وَقِيلَ: كَانَ كَلْبَ طَبَّاخِ الْمَلِكِ، وَقَدْ كَانَ وَافَقَهُمْ عَلَى الدِّينِ فَصَحِبَهُ كَلْبُهُ فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "هَمَّامِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ الدِّمَشْقِيِّ": حَدَّثَنَا صَدَقَة بْنُ عُمَرَ الغَسَّاني، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادٌ المِنْقَري، سَمِعْتُ الْحَسَنَ الْبَصْرِيَّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، يَقُولُ: كَانَ اسْمَ كَبْشِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: جَرِيرٌ وَاسْمَ هُدْهُدِ سُلَيْمَانَ: عَنْقَز، وَاسْمَ كَلْبِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ: قِطْمِيرٌ، وَاسْمَ عِجْلِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ الَّذِي عَبَدُوهُ: بَهْمُوتُ. وَهَبَطَ آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِالْهِنْدِ، وَحَوَّاءُ بِجُدَّةَ، وَإِبْلِيسُ بِدَسْتَ بَيْسَانَ، وَالْحَيَّةُ بِأَصْبَهَانَ 

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ عَنْ شُعَيْبٍ الْجُبَّائِيِّ أَنَّهُ سَمَّاهُ: حِمْرَانَ.

وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي لَوْنِهِ عَلَى أَقْوَالٍ لَا حَاصِلَ لَهَا، وَلَا طَائِلَ تَحْتَهَا وَلَا دَلِيلَ عَلَيْهَا، وَلَا حَاجَةَ إِلَيْهَا، بَلْ هِيَ مِمَّا يُنْهَى عَنْهُ، فَإِنَّ مُسْتَنَدَهَا رَجْمٌ بالغيب.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَوِ اطَّلَعْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ لَوَلَّيْتَ مِنْهُمْ فِرَارًا وَلَمُلِئْتَ مِنْهُمْ رُعْبًا﴾ أَيْ: أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى أَلْقَى عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَهَابَةَ بِحَيْثُ لَا يَقَعُ نَظَرُ أَحَدٍ عَلَيْهِمْ إِلَّا هَابَهُمْ؛ لِمَا أُلْبِسُوا مِنَ الْمَهَابَةِ وَالذُّعْرِ، لِئَلَّا يَدْنُوَ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدٌ وَلَا تَمَسَّهُمْ يَدُ لَامِسٍ، حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ الْكِتَابُ أَجَلَهُ، وَتَنْقَضِيَ رَقْدَتُهُمُ الَّتِي شَاءَ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى فِيهِمْ، لِمَا لَهُ فِي ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْحُجَّةِ وَالْحِكْمَةِ الْبَالِغَةِ، وَالرَّحْمَةِ الْوَاسِعَةِ.

---

## 18:19-20 — verses 19-20 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: just as We had made them sleep, We raised them up with their bodies, their hair, and their skin sound, having lost nothing of their conditions or their forms, and that was after three hundred and nine years. This is why they asked one another: {How long have you remained?} that is, how long have you slept? {They said, "We have remained a day or part of a day."} Their entering the cave had been at the beginning of the day, and their waking had been at the end of the day. This is why they corrected themselves and said: {"Or part of a day." They said, "Your Lord knows best how long you have remained,"} meaning: Allah knows best your affair. It seems some hesitation occurred to them regarding the length of their sleep, so they left it to Allah's knowledge. Then they turned to what was more important in their situation at that moment, which was their need for food and drink, so they said: {"So send one of you with this silver coin of yours"} meaning your silver, this one. That was because they had brought with them coins from their homes for their needs, and they had given some in charity and some remained. This is why they said: {"So send one of you with this silver coin of yours to the city"} meaning your city, the one you left, and the definite article here refers to something already known.

{"And let him see which of its food is purest"} meaning, most wholesome in food, similar to His saying: {And were it not for the favor of Allah upon you and His mercy, not one of you would ever have been purified} [al-Nur: 21], and His saying: {He has certainly succeeded who purifies himself} [al-A'la: 14]. From this comes zakat, which makes wealth wholesome and purifies it. It has also been said that it means more abundant in food, from which comes the zakat (increase) of crops when they become abundant, as the poet said:

Our tribes are seven and you are three, and the seven are more abundant and better than the three.

The correct view is the first one, because their purpose was only what was wholesome and lawful, whether it was little or much.

As for His saying {and let him be discreet}, meaning in his going out and his departure, in his purchasing and his return. They mean: let him move as stealthily as he is able. {And let him not make anyone aware} meaning: let him not inform {anyone about you. Indeed, if they come to know of you, they will stone you} meaning, if they learn of your location, {they will stone you or return you to their religion,} meaning the companions of Decius (Daqyanus). They feared that these people would discover their location, and that they would then continue to torment them with various kinds of torture until they forced them back into the religion they had been upon, or until they died. And if you were to yield to them regarding a return to that religion, then there would be no success for you in this world or in the Hereafter. This is why He said: {and in that case you would never succeed.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَكَمَا أَرْقَدْنَاهُمْ بَعَثْنَاهُمْ صَحِيحَةً أَبْدَانُهُمْ وَأَشْعَارُهُمْ وَأَبْشَارُهُمْ، لَمْ يَفْقِدُوا مِنْ أَحْوَالِهِمْ وَهَيْئَاتِهِمْ شَيْئًا، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَ ثَلَاثِمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ وَتِسْعِ سِنِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا تَسَاءَلُوا بَيْنَهُمْ: ﴿كَمْ لَبِثْتُمْ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: كَمْ رَقَدْتُمْ؟ ﴿قَالُوا لَبِثْنَا يَوْمًا أَوْ بَعْضَ يَوْمٍ﴾ كَانَ دُخُولُهُمْ إِلَى الْكَهْفِ فِي أَوَّلِ نَهَارٍ، وَاسْتِيقَاظُهُمْ كَانَ فِي آخِرِ نَهَارٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا اسْتَدْرَكُوا فَقَالُوا: ﴿أَوْ بَعْضَ يَوْمٍ قَالُوا رَبُّكُمْ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا لَبِثْتُمْ﴾ أَيْ: اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِأَمْرِكُمْ، وَكَأَنَّهُ حَصَلَ لَهُمْ نَوْعُ تَرَدّد فِي كَثْرَةِ نَوْمِهِمْ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، ثُمَّ عَدَلُوا إِلَى الْأَهَمِّ فِي أَمْرِهِمْ إِذْ ذَاكَ وَهُوَ احْتِيَاجُهُمْ إِلَى الطَّعَامِ وَالشَّرَابِ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿فَابْعَثُوا أَحَدَكُمْ بِوَرِقِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِضَّتِكُمْ هَذِهِ. وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَدِ اسْتَصْحَبُوا مَعَهُمْ دَرَاهِمَ مِنْ مَنَازِلِهِمْ لِحَاجَتِهِمْ إِلَيْهَا، فَتَصَدَّقُوا مِنْهَا وَبَقِيَ مِنْهَا؛ فَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿فَابْعَثُوا أَحَدَكُمْ بِوَرِقِكُمْ هَذِهِ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ﴾ أَيْ: مَدِينَتِكُمُ الَّتِي خَرَجْتُمْ مِنْهَا وَالْأَلِفُ وَاللَّامُ لِلْعَهْدِ.

﴿فَلْيَنْظُرْ أَيُّهَا أَزْكَى طَعَامًا﴾ أَيْ: أَطْيَبُ طَعَامًا، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَوْلا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَرَحْمَتُهُ مَا زَكَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ أَبَدًا﴾ [النُّورِ:٢١] وَقَوْلِهِ ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ مَنْ تَزَكَّى﴾ [الْأَعْلَى:١٤] وَمِنْهُ الزَّكَاةُ الَّتِي تُطَيب الْمَالَ وَتُطَهِّرُهُ. وَقِيلَ: أَكْثَرُ طَعَامًا، وَمِنْهُ زَكَاةُ الزَّرْعِ إِذَا كَثُرَ، قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ: 

قَبَاِئُلنا سَبْعٌ وَأَنْتُمْ ثَلاثَةٌ ... وَللسَّبْعُ أزْكَى مِنْ ثَلاثٍ وَأطْيَبُ ...

وَالصَّحِيحُ الْأَوَّلُ؛ لِأَنَّ مَقْصُودَهُمْ إِنَّمَا هُوَ الطَّيِّبُ الْحَلَالُ، سَوَاءٌ كَانَ قَلِيلًا أَوْ كَثِيرًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿وَلْيَتَلَطَّفْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي خُرُوجِهِ وَذَهَابِهِ، وَشِرَائِهِ وَإِيَابِهِ، يَقُولُونَ: وَلْيَتَخَفَّ كُلَّ مَا يَقْدِرُ عَلَيْهِ ﴿وَلا يُشْعِرَنَّ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا يُعْلِمَنَّ ﴿بِكُمْ أَحَدًا إِنَّهُمْ إِنْ يَظْهَرُوا عَلَيْكُمْ يَرْجُمُوكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: إِنْ عَلِمُوا بِمَكَانِكُمْ، ﴿يَرْجُمُوكُمْ أَوْ يُعِيدُوكُمْ فِي مِلَّتِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنُونَ أَصْحَابَ دَقْيَانُوسَ، يَخَافُونَ مِنْهُمْ أَنْ يَطَّلِعُوا عَلَى مَكَانِهِمْ، فَلَا يَزَالُونَ يُعَذِّبُونَهُمْ بِأَنْوَاعِ الْعَذَابِ إِلَى أَنْ يُعِيدُوهُمْ فِي ملتهم التي هم عليها أو يَمُوتُوا، وَإِنْ واتَوهم عَلَى الْعَوْدِ فِي الدِّينِ فَلَا فَلَاحَ لَكُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَلَا فِي الْآخِرَةِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ﴿وَلَنْ تُفْلِحُوا إِذًا أَبَدًا﴾ .

---

## 18:21 — verse 21

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And thus We made them known} that is, We caused the people to discover them, {so that they might know that the promise of Allah is true and that the Hour, there is no doubt about it}

More than one of the Salaf mentioned that the people of that time had come to have doubt about the resurrection and about the matter of the Hour. Ikrimah said: among them was a group who said, "the spirits are resurrected but the bodies are not resurrected." So Allah raised up the People of the Cave as a proof, an indication, and a sign concerning that.

They mentioned that when one of them wanted to go out to the city to buy something for them to eat, he disguised himself and went out walking on a path other than the main road, until he reached the city. They mentioned that its name was Diqsus. He thought that he had only recently left it, whereas the people had changed generation after generation, era after era, nation after nation, and the land and those upon it had changed, as the poet said:

"As for the abodes, they are indeed like their abodes, but I see the men of the encampment are not its men."

So he found that he could not see any of the landmarks of the town that he knew, nor did he recognize anyone among its people, neither its notables nor its common folk. He became bewildered within himself and said, "perhaps madness or some affliction has struck me, or I am dreaming," then he said, "by Allah, none of that is the case with me, and my knowledge of this town as of yesterday evening was different from this description." Then he said, "hastening to leave from here would be best for me." Then he approached a man selling food and gave him the money he had with him, asking him to sell him food with it. When that man saw the coin, he found it strange, and found its minting strange, so he passed it to his neighbor, and they began passing it around among themselves, saying, "perhaps this man has found a treasure." So they asked him about his situation, and where he had gotten this money, "perhaps he found it from a treasure. And who are you?" He kept saying, "I am from the people of this city, and my knowledge of it is from yesterday evening, and Daqyanus was in it." So they attributed madness to him, and carried him to the one in charge of their affairs, who questioned him about his condition and his matter until he informed them of his situation, while he himself was bewildered by his state and what he was in. When he informed them of that, they set out with him to the cave: the governor of the town and its people, until they brought him to the cave. He said, "leave me to go ahead of you in entering, so that I may inform my companions." It is said that they do not know how he went in, and Allah concealed knowledge of him from them. And it is said instead that they entered upon them, and saw them, and the king greeted them and embraced them, and he was a Muslim as it is said, and his name was Tidusis (Theodosius). They rejoiced in him and comforted him with speech, then they bade him farewell and greeted him with peace, and they returned to their resting places, and Allah, Mighty and Majestic, caused them to die. And Allah knows best.

Qatadah said: Ibn Abbas went on a military campaign with Habib ibn Maslamah, and they passed by a cave in the land of the Byzantines, and they saw bones in it.
