Someone said, "are these the bones of the People of the Cave?" Ibn Abbas said, "their bones decayed more than three hundred years ago." Narrated by Ibn Jarir.

His statement: {And thus We made them known} that is, just as We had made them sleep and awakened them in their same forms, We caused the people of that time to discover them, {so that they might know that the promise of Allah is true and that the Hour, there is no doubt about it, when they were disputing among themselves about their affair} that is, regarding the matter of the Hour, some affirming it and some denying it. So Allah made their discovery of the People of the Cave a proof for them and against them. {Then they said, build over them a structure; their Lord knows best about them} that is, seal up for them the door of their cave and leave them in their condition. {Those who prevailed in their affair said, we will surely take over them a place of worship}

Ibn Jarir related two opinions concerning who said this: one, that they were the Muslims among them; the second, that they were the polytheists among them. And Allah knows best.

The apparent view is that those who said that were the people of authority and influence. But were they praised for this or not? There is a matter to consider here, because the Prophet ﷺ said: "May Allah curse the Jews and the Christians, they took the graves of their prophets and righteous ones as places of worship," warning against what they did. It has been related to us from the Commander of the Faithful, Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, that when he found the grave of Daniel in his time in Iraq, he ordered that it be concealed from the people, and that the document found with him, which contained something of the accounts of great battles and other matters, be buried.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ أَعْثَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَطْلَعْنَا عَلَيْهِمُ النَّاسَ ﴿لِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ وَأَنَّ السَّاعَةَ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهَا﴾

ذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ أَنَّهُ كَانَ قَدْ حَصَلَ لِأَهْلِ ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ شَكٌّ فِي الْبَعْثِ وَفِي أَمْرِ الْقِيَامَةِ. وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: كَانَ مِنْهُمْ طَائِفَةٌ قَدْ قَالُوا: تُبْعَثُ الْأَرْوَاحُ وَلَا تُبْعَثُ الْأَجْسَادُ. فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ أَهْلَ الْكَهْفِ حُجَّةً وَدَلَالَةً وَآيَةً عَلَى ذَلِكَ.

وَذَكَرُوا أَنَّهُ لَمَّا أَرَادَ أَحَدُهُمُ الْخُرُوجَ لِيَذْهَبَ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، فِي شِرَاءِ شَيْءٍ لَهُمْ لِيَأْكُلُوهُ، تَنَكَّرَ وَخَرَجَ يَمْشِي فِي غَيْرِ الْجَادَّةِ، حَتَّى انْتَهَى إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، وَذَكَرُوا أَنَّ اسْمَهَا دِقْسُوسُ وَهُوَ يَظُنُّ أَنَّهُ قَرِيبُ الْعَهْدِ بِهَا، وَكَانَ النَّاسُ قَدْ تَبَدَّلُوا قَرْنًا بَعْدَ قَرْنٍ، وَجِيلًا بَعْدَ جِيلٍ، وَأُمَّةً بَعْدَ أُمَّةٍ، وَتَغَيَّرَتِ الْبِلَادُ وَمَنْ عَلَيْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ:

أَمَّا الدّيارُ فَإنَّها كَديارهِم ... وَأرَى رجالَ الحَي غَيْرَ رجَاله ...

فَجَعَلَ لَا يَرَى شَيْئًا مِنْ مَعَالِمِ الْبَلَدِ الَّتِي يَعْرِفُهَا، وَلَا يَعْرِفُ أَحَدًا مِنْ أَهْلِهَا، لَا خَوَاصِّهَا وَلَا عَوَامِّهَا، فَجَعَلَ يَتَحَيَّرُ فِي نَفْسِهِ وَيَقُولُ: لَعَلَّ بِي جُنُونًا أَوْ مَسًّا، أَوْ أَنَا حَالِمٌ، وَيَقُولُ: وَاللَّهِ مَا بِي شَيْءٌ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَإِنَّ عَهْدِي بِهَذِهِ الْبَلْدَةِ عَشِيَّةَ أَمْسٍ عَلَى غَيْرِ هَذِهِ الصِّفَةِ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: إِنَّ تَعْجِيلَ الْخُرُوجِ مِنْ هَاهُنَا لَأَوْلَى لِي. ثُمَّ عَمَدَ إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِمَّنْ يَبِيعُ الطَّعَامَ، فَدَفَعَ إِلَيْهِ مَا مَعَهُ مِنَ النَّفَقَةِ، وَسَأَلَهُ أَنْ يَبِيعَهُ بِهَا طَعَامًا. فَلَمَّا رَآهَا ذَلِكَ الرَّجُلُ أَنْكَرَهَا وَأَنْكَرَ ضَرْبها، فَدَفَعَهَا إِلَى جَارِهِ، وَجَعَلُوا يَتَدَاوَلُونَهَا بَيْنَهُمْ وَيَقُولُونَ: لَعَلَّ هَذَا قَدْ وَجَدَ كَنْزًا. فَسَأَلُوهُ عَنْ أَمْرِهِ، وَمِنْ أَيْنَ لَهُ هَذِهِ النَّفَقَةُ؟ لَعَلَّهُ وَجَدَهَا مِنْ كَنْزٍ. وَمَنْ أَنْتَ؟ فَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ: أَنَا مِنْ أَهْلِ هَذِهِ الْمَدِينَةِ وَعَهْدِي بِهَا عَشِيَّةَ أَمْسٍ وَفِيهَا دَقْيَانُوسُ. فَنَسَبُوهُ إِلَى الْجُنُونِ، فَحَمَلُوهُ إِلَى وَلِيِّ أَمْرِهِمْ، فَسَأَلَهُ عَنْ شَأْنِهِ وَعَنْ أَمْرِهِ حَتَّى أَخْبَرَهُمْ بِأَمْرِهِ، وَهُوَ مُتَحَيِّرٌ فِي حَالِهِ، وَمَا هُوَ فِيهِ. فَلَمَّا أَعْلَمَهُمْ بِذَلِكَ قَامُوا مَعَهُ إِلَى الْكَهْفِ: مُتَوَلّى الْبَلَدِ وَأَهْلُهَا، حَتَّى انْتَهَى بِهِمْ إِلَى الْكَهْفِ، فَقَالَ: دَعُونِي حَتَّى أَتَقَدَّمَكُمْ في الدخول لأعلم أصحابي، فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُمْ لَا يَدْرُونَ كَيْفَ ذَهَبَ فِيهِ، وَأَخْفَى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ خَبَرَهُ وَيُقَالُ: بَلْ دَخَلُوا عَلَيْهِمْ، وَرَأَوْهُمْ وَسَلَّمَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَلِكُ وَاعْتَنَقَهُمْ، وَكَانَ مُسْلِمًا فِيمَا قِيلَ، وَاسْمُهُ تِيدُوسِيسُ فَفَرِحُوا بِهِ وَآنَسُوهُ بِالْكَلَامِ، ثُمَّ وَدَّعُوهُ وَسَلَّمُوا عَلَيْهِ، وَعَادُوا إِلَى مَضَاجِعِهِمْ، وَتَوَفَّاهُمُ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: غَزَا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ مَعَ حَبِيبِ بْنِ مَسْلَمَةَ، فَمَرُّوا بِكَهْفٍ فِي بِلَادِ الرُّومِ، فَرَأَوْا فِيهِ عِظَامًا، فَقَالَ قَائِلٌ: هَذِهِ عِظَامُ أَهْلِ الْكَهْفِ؟ فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: لَقَدْ بَلِيَتْ عِظَامُهُمْ مِنْ أَكْثَرِ مِنْ ثَلَاثِمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ أَعْثَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أي: كما أرقدناهم وأيقظناهم بهيآتهم، أَطْلَعْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ أَهْلَ ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ ﴿لِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ وَأَنَّ السَّاعَةَ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهَا إِذْ يَتَنَازَعُونَ بَيْنَهُمْ أَمْرَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي أَمْرِ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَمِنْ مُثْبِتٍ لَهَا وَمِنْ مُنْكِرٍ، فَجَعَلَ اللَّهُ ظُهُورَهُمْ عَلَى أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ حُجَّةً لَهُمْ وَعَلَيْهِمْ ﴿فَقَالُوا ابْنُوا عَلَيْهِمْ بُنْيَانًا رَبُّهُمْ أَعْلَمُ بِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: سُدُّوا عَلَيْهِمْ بَابَ كَهْفِهِمْ، وَذَرُوهُمْ عَلَى حَالِهِمْ ﴿قَالَ الَّذِينَ غَلَبُوا عَلَى أَمْرِهِمْ لَنَتَّخِذَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ مَسْجِدًا﴾

حَكَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي الْقَائِلِينَ ذَلِكَ قَوْلَيْنِ: أَحَدُهُمَا: إِنَّهُمُ الْمُسْلِمُونَ مِنْهُمْ. وَالثَّانِي: أَهْلُ الشِّرْكِ مِنْهُمْ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ 

وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا ذَلِكَ هُمْ أَصْحَابُ الْكَلِمَةِ وَالنُّفُوذِ. وَلَكِنْ هَلْ هُمْ مَحْمُودُونَ أَمْ لَا؟ فِيهِ نَظَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَعَنَ اللَّهُ الْيَهُودَ وَالنَّصَارَى، اتَّخَذُوا قُبُورَ أَنْبِيَائِهِمْ وَصَالِحِيهِمْ مَسَاجِدَ" يُحَذِّرُ مَا فَعَلُوا. وَقَدْ رُوِّينَا عَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ لَمَّا وَجَدَ قَبْرَ دَانْيَالَ فِي زَمَانِهِ بِالْعِرَاقِ، أَمَرَ أَنْ يُخْفَى عَنِ النَّاسِ، وَأَنْ تُدْفَنَ تِلْكَ الرُّقْعَةُ الَّتِي وَجَدُوهَا عِنْدَهُ، فِيهَا شَيْءٌ مِنَ الْمَلَاحِمِ وَغَيْرِهَا.

---

## 18:22 — verse 22

### Translation

The Almighty is speaking, reporting the disagreement among people about the number of the People of the Cave. He related three sayings, which indicates that no one held a fourth. He weakened the first two sayings by His statement: {a guess about the unseen}, meaning a statement made without knowledge, like one who throws toward a place he does not know, for he can hardly hit it, and if he does hit it, it is without intention. Then He related the third and remained silent about it, or rather affirmed it by His statement: {and the eighth of them was their dog}, which indicates its soundness, and that it is what actually occurred.

His statement: {Say: My Lord knows best their number} is guidance that the best course in such a matter is to refer the knowledge back to Allah, the Almighty, since there is no need to delve into such a matter without knowledge. But if He informs us of something, we say it, and otherwise we stop where we stop.

His statement: {none knows them except a few} means, of the people. Qatadah said: Ibn Abbas said, "I am among the few whom Allah, Mighty and Majestic, excepted. They were seven." Ibn Jurayj likewise narrated from Ata al-Khurasani, from him, that he used to say: "I am among those whom Allah excepted," and he would say, "Their number was seven."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Bashshar told us, Abd al-Rahman told us, Isra'il told us, from Simak, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: {none knows them except a few}, he said: "I am among the few, they were seven."

These are sound chains of transmission back to Ibn Abbas that they were seven, and this agrees with what we presented before.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar said, from Abdullah ibn Abi Najih, from Mujahid, who said: "I was told that one of them, because of his young age, had a mark of silver on him." Ibn Abbas said: "They remained thus, night and day, in worship of Allah, weeping and seeking help from Allah. They were eight persons: Makslamina, who was the eldest of them and the one who spoke to the king on their behalf, Majsimilinina, Tamlikha, Martunis, Kashtunis, Bayrunis, Dimus, Yatunis, and Qalush."

This is how it occurs in this report, and it is possible that this comes from the words of Ibn Ishaq himself, or from someone between him and Ibn Abbas, for what is sound from Ibn Abbas is that they were seven, and this is also the apparent meaning of the verse. It was mentioned earlier from Shu'ayb al-Jabba'i that the name of their dog was Himran. There is doubt about the soundness of naming them with these names and naming their dog, and Allah knows best, for most of that is taken from the People of the Book. The Almighty has said: {So do not dispute concerning them except with an outward disputation}, meaning easy and gentle, for there is no great benefit resulting from knowing that precisely. {And do not inquire about them from any of them}, meaning, for they have no knowledge of that except what they say from their own selves, a guess about the unseen, that is, without relying on infallible speech. Allah has brought you, O Muhammad, the truth about which there is no doubt and no uncertainty, and it takes precedence and stands as judge over everything that came before it, of books and sayings.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ اخْتِلَافِ النَّاسِ فِي عِدَّةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ، فَحَكَى ثَلَاثَةَ أَقْوَالٍ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَا قَائِلَ بِرَابِعٍ، وَلِمَا ضَعَّف الْقَوْلَيْنِ الْأَوَّلَيْنِ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿رَجْمًا بِالْغَيْبِ﴾ أَيْ: قَوْلًا بِلَا عِلْمٍ، كَمَنْ يَرْمِي إِلَى مَكَانٍ لَا يَعْرِفُهُ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَكَادُ يُصِيبُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَ فَبِلَا قَصْدٍ، ثُمَّ حَكَى الثَّالِثَ وَسَكَتَ عَلَيْهِ أَوْ قَرَّرَهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَثَامِنُهُمْ كَلْبُهُمْ﴾ فَدَلَّ عَلَى صِحَّتِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ هُوَ الْوَاقِعُ فِي نَفْسِ الْأَمْرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ رَبِّي أَعْلَمُ بِعِدَّتِهِمْ﴾ إِرْشَادٌ إِلَى أَنَّ الْأَحْسَنَ فِي مِثْلِ هَذَا الْمَقَامِ رَدُّ الْعِلْمِ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، إِذْ لَا احْتِيَاجَ إِلَى الْخَوْضِ فِي مِثْلِ ذَلِكَ بِلَا عِلْمٍ، لَكِنْ إِذَا أَطْلَعَنَا عَلَى أَمْرٍ قُلْنَا بِهِ، وَإِلَّا وَقَفْنَا حَيْثُ وَقَفْنَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا يَعْلَمُهُمْ إِلا قَلِيلٌ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ النَّاسِ. قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَا مِنَ الْقَلِيلِ الَّذِي اسْتَثْنَى اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، كَانُوا سَبْعَةً. وَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ عَنْهُ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَقُولُ: أَنَا مِمَّنِ اسْتَثْنَى اللَّهُ، وَيَقُولُ: عَدَّتُهُمْ سَبْعَةٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّارٍ حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿مَا يَعْلَمُهُمْ إِلا قَلِيلٌ﴾ قَالَ: أَنَا مِنَ الْقَلِيلِ، كَانُوا سَبْعَةً.

فَهَذِهِ أَسَانِيدُ صَحِيحَةٌ إِلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا سَبْعَةً، وَهُوَ مُوَافِقٌ لِمَا قَدَّمْنَاهُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَار عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: لَقَدْ حُدّثتُ أَنَّهُ كَانَ عَلَى بَعْضِهِمْ مِنْ حَدَاثَةِ سِنِّهِ وَضَح الوَرِق. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَكَانُوا كَذَلِكَ لَيْلَهُمْ وَنَهَارَهُمْ فِي عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ، يَبْكُونَ وَيَسْتَغِيثُونَ بِاللَّهِ، وَكَانُوا ثَمَانِيَةَ نَفَرٍ: مَكْسَلْمِينَا وَكَانَ أَكْبَرَهُمْ وَهُوَ الَّذِي كَلَّمَ الْمَلِكَ عَنْهُمْ، وَمَجْسِيمِيلِنِينَا وَتِمْلِيخَا وَمَرْطُونَسُ، وَكَشْطُونَسُ، وَبَيْرُونَسُ، وَدِيمُوسُ، وَيَطُونَسُ وَقَالُوشُ.

هَكَذَا وَقَعَ فِي هَذِهِ الرِّوَايَةِ، وَيُحْتَمَلُ هَذَا مِنْ كَلَامِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، وَمِنْ بَيْنِهِ وَبَيْنَهُ، فَإِنَّ الصَّحِيحَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا سَبْعَةً، وَهُوَ ظَاهِرُ الْآيَةِ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ عَنْ شُعَيْبٍ الْجَبَّائِيِّ أَنَّ اسْمَ كَلْبِهِمْ حِمْرَانُ ، وَفِي تَسْمِيَتِهِمْ بِهَذِهِ الْأَسْمَاءِ وَاسْمِ كَلْبِهِمْ نَظَرٌ فِي صِحَّتِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ؛ فَإِنَّ غَالِبَ ذَلِكَ مُتَلَقَّى مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، وَقَدْ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلا تُمَارِ فِيهِمْ إِلا مِرَاءً ظَاهِرًا﴾ أَيْ: سَهْلًا هَيِّنًا؛ فَإِنَّ الْأَمْرَ فِي مَعْرِفَةِ ذَلِكَ لَا يَتَرَتَّبُ عَلَيْهِ كَبِيرُ فَائِدَةٍ ﴿وَلا تَسْتَفْتِ فِيهِمْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا﴾ أَيْ: فَإِنَّهُمْ لَا عِلْمَ لَهُمْ بِذَلِكَ إِلَّا مَا يَقُولُونَهُ مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ رَجْمًا بِالْغَيْبِ، أَيْ مِنْ غَيْرِ اسْتِنَادٍ إِلَى كَلَامٍ مَعْصُومٍ، وَقَدْ جَاءَكَ اللَّهُ يَا مُحَمَّدُ بِالْحَقِّ الَّذِي لَا شَكَّ فِيهِ وَلَا مِرْيَةَ، فَهُوَ الْمُقَدِّمُ الْحَاكِمُ عَلَى كُلِّ مَا تَقَدَّمُهُ مِنَ الْكُتُبِ وَالْأَقْوَالِ.

---

## 18:23-24 — verses 23-24 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is guidance from God to His Messenger ﷺ, regarding proper conduct when he resolves to do something in the future: that he should refer that back to the will of God, mighty and majestic, the Knower of the unseen, who knows what has been and what will be, and what has not been, how it would have been if it had been, as is established in the two Sahihs on the authority of Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: Sulayman ibn Dawud (peace be upon them both) said, "I will surely go around tonight to seventy women," and in another narration, "ninety women," and in another narration, "one hundred women," "each of whom will bear a boy who will fight in the way of God." It was said to him, and in another narration, the angel said to him, "Say: If God wills." But he did not say it. So he went around to them, and none of them bore a child except one woman, who bore half a person. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, had he said 'if God wills,' he would not have broken his oath, and it would have been a means of attaining what he sought." In another narration: "and they would all have fought as horsemen in the way of God."

The reason for the revelation of this verse was mentioned earlier at the beginning of the surah, regarding the statement of the Prophet ﷺ when he was asked about the story of the People of the Cave: "Tomorrow I will answer you." Then revelation was delayed for fifteen days. We have mentioned this at length at the beginning of the surah, so there is no need to repeat it here.

Concerning His saying, {And remember your Lord when you forget}: it was said that its meaning is, when you forget to say the exception (the words "if God wills"), then say it whenever you remember it. This was stated by Abu al-Aliyah and al-Hasan al-Basri.

Hushaym said, from al-A'mash, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas, regarding a man who swears an oath: he said that he may make the exception even after a year has passed, and he used to cite {And remember your Lord when you forget} in this regard. Al-A'mash was asked, "Did you hear this from Mujahid?" He said, "Layth ibn Abi Sulaym narrated it to me," meaning he doubted its authenticity, for Layth would even see this cloak of mine as gold.

Al-Tabarani related it through the hadith of Abu Mu'awiyah, from al-A'mash, with the same chain.

The meaning of Ibn Abbas's statement, "he may make the exception even after a year," is: if he forgets to say in his oath or speech "if God wills," and then remembers, even after a year, then it is the recommended practice (sunnah) for him to say it, so that he fulfills the practice of making the exception, even if this is after he has already broken the oath. Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him, stated this explicitly, meaning that it does not remove the breaking of the oath or nullify the expiation required. What Ibn Jarir said, may God have mercy on him, is correct, and it is the most fitting interpretation to place upon Ibn Abbas's words, and God knows best.

Ikrimah said: {And remember your Lord when you forget} means, when you become angry. This is an interpretation by way of a necessary consequence (tafsir bi'l-lazim).

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, regarding {And do not say of anything, "Indeed, I will do that tomorrow," except [when adding], "If God wills." And remember your Lord when you forget}, meaning that you should say "if God wills." This too is an interpretation by way of necessary consequence.

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying: {And do not say of anything, "Indeed, I will do that tomorrow," except [when adding], "If God wills." And remember your Lord when you forget}, meaning that you should say "if God wills."

Al-Tabarani also related from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying {And remember your Lord when you forget}: the exception, so make the exception whenever you remember it. He said: this is specific to the Messenger of God ﷺ, and none of us is permitted to make the exception except in connection with his oath. Then he said: al-Walid narrated it alone, from Abd al-Aziz ibn al-Husayn.

Another interpretation of the verse is possible: that God, mighty and majestic, guided whoever forgets something in his speech to the remembrance of God the Exalted, because forgetfulness originates from Satan, as the young companion of Musa said: {And none made me forget it except Satan, so that I would mention it} [al-Kahf: 63]. The remembrance of God the Exalted repels Satan, and when Satan departs, forgetfulness departs, so the remembrance of God is a cause for remembering. This is why He said: {And remember your Lord when you forget}.

As for His saying, {And say, "Perhaps my Lord will guide me to what is nearer than this to right guidance"}: this means, when you are asked about something you do not know, ask God concerning it, and turn to Him so that He may grant you success in reaching what is correct and rightly guided in that matter. Other interpretations of it have also been given, and God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِرْشَادٌ مِنَ الله لرسوله الله صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، إِلَى الْأَدَبِ فِيمَا إِذَا عَزَمَ عَلَى شَيْءٍ لِيَفْعَلَهُ فِي الْمُسْتَقْبَلِ، أَنْ يَرُدَّ ذَلِكَ إِلَى مَشِيئَةِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَلَّامِ الْغُيُوبِ، الَّذِي يَعْلَمُ مَا كَانَ وَمَا يَكُونُ، وَمَا لَمْ يَكُنْ لَوْ كَانَ كَيْفَ كَانَ يَكُونُ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أنه [قَالَ] قَالَ سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ: لأطوفن الليلة على سَبْعِينَ امْرَأَةً -وَفِي رِوَايَةِ تِسْعِينَ امْرَأَةً. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: مِائَةِ امْرَأَةٍ-تَلِدُ كُلُّ امْرَأَةٍ مِنْهُنَّ غُلَامًا يُقَاتِلُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، فَقِيلَ لَهُ -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: فَقَالَ لَهُ الْمَلَكُ-قُلْ: إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ. فَلَمْ يَقُلْ فَطَافَ بِهِنَّ فَلَمْ يَلِدْ مِنْهُنَّ إِلَّا امْرَأَةٌ وَاحِدَةٌ نِصْفَ إِنْسَانٍ"، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَوْ قَالَ: "إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ" لَمْ يَحْنَثْ، وَكَانَ دَرْكًا لِحَاجَتِهِ"، وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "وَلَقَاتَلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ فُرْسَانًا أَجْمَعُونَ 

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ ذِكْرُ سَبَبِ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ فِي قَوْلِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، لَمَّا سُئِلَ عَنْ قِصَّةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ: "غَدًا أُجِيبُكُمْ". فَتَأَخَّرَ الْوَحْيُ خَمْسَةَ عَشَرَ يَوْمًا، وَقَدْ ذَكَرْنَاهُ بِطُولِهِ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ، فَأَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ قِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ إِذَا نَسِيتَ الِاسْتِثْنَاءَ، فَاسْتَثْنِ عِنْدَ ذِكْرِكَ لَهُ. قَالَهُ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ.

وَقَالَ هُشَيْمٌ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي الرَّجُلِ يَحْلِفُ؟ قَالَ: لَهُ أَنْ يَسْتَثْنِيَ وَلَوْ إِلَى سَنَةٍ، وَكَانَ يَقُولُ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ فِي ذَلِكَ. قِيلَ لِلْأَعْمَشِ: سَمِعْتَهُ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ؟ قَالَ حَدَّثَنِي بِهِ لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، يَرَى ذَهَبَ كِسَائِي هَذَا.

وَرَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ .

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: "أَنَّهُ يَسْتَثْنِي وَلَوْ بَعْدَ سَنَةٍ" أَيْ: إِذَا نَسِيَ أَنْ يَقُولَ فِي حَلِفِهِ أَوْ كَلَامِهِ "إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ" وَذَكَرَ وَلَوْ بَعْدَ سَنَةٍ، فالسُّنة لَهُ أَنْ يَقُولَ ذَلِكَ، لِيَكُونَ آتِيًا بسُنَّة الِاسْتِثْنَاءِ، حَتَّى وَلَوْ كَانَ بَعْدَ الْحِنْثِ، قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَنَصَّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، لَا أَنْ يَكُونَ [ذَلِكَ] رَافِعًا لِحِنْثِ الْيَمِينِ وَمُسْقِطًا لِلْكَفَّارَةِ. وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، هُوَ الصَّحِيحُ، وَهُوَ الْأَلْيَقُ بِحَمْلِ كَلَامِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ عَلَيْهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا غَضِبْتَ. وَهَذَا تَفْسِيرٌ بِاللَّازِمِ.

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ يَحْيَى الحُلْواني، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ عَبَّادُ بْنُ الْعَوَّامِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ حُسَيْنٍ، عَنْ يَعْلَى بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلا تَقُولَنَّ لِشَيْءٍ إِنِّي فَاعِلٌ ذَلِكَ غَدًا إِلا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ أَنْ تَقُولَ: إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ [وَهَذَا تَفْسِيرٌ بِاللَّازِمِ] .

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ الجُبيلي حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ حُصَيْن، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا تَقُولَنَّ لِشَيْءٍ إِنِّي فَاعِلٌ ذَلِكَ غَدًا إِلا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ أَنْ تَقُولَ: إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ.

وَرَوَى الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، أَيْضًا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ الِاسْتِثْنَاءَ، فَاسْتَثْنِ إِذَا ذَكَرْتَ. وَقَالَ: هِيَ خَاصَّةٌ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَلَيْسَ لِأَحَدٍ مِنَّا أَنْ يَسْتَثْنِيَ إِلَّا فِي صِلَةٍ مِنْ يَمِينِهِ ثُمَّ قَالَ: تَفَرَّد بِهِ الْوَلِيدُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ الْحُصَيْنِ .

وَيَحْتَمِلُ فِي الْآيَةِ وَجْهٌ آخَرُ، وَهُوَ أَنْ يَكُونَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، قَدْ أَرْشَدَ مَنْ نَسِيَ الشَّيْءَ فِي كَلَامِهِ إِلَى ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى؛ لِأَنَّ النِّسْيَانَ مَنْشَؤُهُ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ فَتَى مُوسَى: ﴿وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهُ إِلا الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٦٣] وَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى يَطْرُدُ الشَّيْطَانَ، فَإِذَا ذَهَبَ الشَّيْطَانُ ذَهَبَ النِّسْيَانُ، فَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ سَبَبٌ لِلذِّكْرِ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ إِذَا نَسِيتَ﴾ .

وقوله: ﴿وَقُلْ عَسَى أَنْ يَهْدِيَنِ رَبِّي لأقْرَبَ مِنْ هَذَا رَشَدًا﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا سئُلت عَنْ شَيْءٍ لَا تَعْلَمُهُ، فَاسْأَلِ اللَّهَ فِيهِ، وَتَوَجَّهَ إِلَيْهِ فِي أَنْ يُوَفِّقَكَ لِلصَّوَابِ وَالرَّشَدِ [فِي ذَلِكَ] وقيل في تفسيره غَيْرُ ذَلِكَ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 18:25-26 — verses 25-26 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report from God, exalted is He, to His Messenger ﷺ concerning the length of time that the People of the Cave remained in their cave, from when God put them to sleep until He raised them and the people of that later age happened upon them. This period was three hundred years and nine years by the lunar reckoning, which is three hundred years by the solar reckoning, for the difference between every hundred lunar years and solar years is three years. This is why, after mentioning three hundred, He said: {and added nine}.

And His saying: {Say: God knows best how long they remained} means: if you are asked about how long they stayed and you have no knowledge of it and no instruction from God, mighty and majestic is He, then do not proceed to say anything about it. Rather say, regarding a matter like this: {God knows best how long they remained. To Him belongs the unseen of the heavens and the earth}, meaning: none knows that except Him, or one whom God has informed of it among His creation. This is what we have stated, and it is held by more than one of the scholars of tafsir, such as Mujahid, and by more than one of the earlier and later generations.

Qatadah said regarding His saying: {And they remained in their cave three hundred years and added nine}: this is the statement of the People of the Book, and God, exalted is He, refuted it by His saying: {Say: God knows best how long they remained}. He said: and in the reading of Abdullah [ibn Mas'ud] it is "and they said: and they remained," meaning that it was the people who said it.

Mutarrif ibn Abdullah said the same as Qatadah said.

There is a difficulty in what Qatadah claimed, for what is in the hands of the People of the Book is that they remained three hundred years without the nine, meaning by the solar reckoning. Had God been relating their statement, He would not have said: {and added nine}. The apparent sense of the verse is that it is a report from God, not a relation of their statement. This is the choice of Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him. Qatadah's report of Ibn Mas'ud's reading is disconnected (munqati'), and moreover it is anomalous (shadhdh) in relation to the reading of the majority, so it cannot be used as evidence. And God knows best.

His saying: {How seeing is He and how hearing} means: He indeed sees them and hears them.

Ibn Jarir said: this is in the sense of exaggeration in praise, as if it were said: how well He sees and how well He hears. The meaning of the statement is: how well God sees every existing thing, and how well He hears everything that can be heard; nothing of that is hidden from Him.

It is then reported from Qatadah regarding His saying {How seeing is He and how hearing}: none sees better than God nor hears better.

Ibn Zayd said: {How seeing is He and how hearing} means He sees their deeds and hears them from them, being All-Hearing, All-Seeing.

And His saying: {They have no guardian besides Him, and He shares His judgment with no one} means: He, exalted is He, is the One to whom belong creation and command, whose judgment none can overturn. He has no minister, no helper, no partner, and no counselor, exalted and sanctified is He.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا خبَر مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ ﷺ بِمِقْدَارِ مَا لَبِثَ أَصْحَابُ الْكَهْفِ فِي كَهْفِهِمْ، مُنْذُ أَرْقَدَهُمُ اللَّهُ إِلَى أَنْ بَعَثَهُمْ وَأَعْثَرَ عَلَيْهِمْ أَهْلُ ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ، وَأَنَّهُ كَانَ مِقْدَارُهُ ثَلَاثَمِائَةِ [سَنَةٍ] وَتِسْعَ سِنِينَ بِالْهِلَالِيَّةِ، وَهِيَ ثَلَاثُمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ بِالشَّمْسِيَّةِ، فَإِنَّ تَفَاوُتَ مَا بَيْنِ كُلِّ مِائَةِ [سَنَةٍ] بِالْقَمَرِيَّةِ إِلَى الشَّمْسِيَّةِ ثَلَاثُ سِنِينَ؛ فَلِهَذَا قَالَ بَعْدَ الثَّلَاثِمِائَةٍ: ﴿وَازْدَادُوا تِسْعًا﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلِ اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا لَبِثُوا﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا سُئِلْتَ عَنْ لَبْثِهِمْ وَلَيْسَ عِنْدَكَ [عِلْمٌ] فِي ذَلِكَ وَتَوْقِيفٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فَلَا تَتَقَدَّمْ فِيهِ بِشَيْءٍ، بَلْ قُلْ فِي مِثْلِ هَذَا: ﴿اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا لَبِثُوا لَهُ غَيْبُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَعْلَمُ ذَلِكَ إِلَّا هُوَ أَوْ مَنْ أَطْلَعَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ خَلْقه، وَهَذَا الَّذِي قُلْنَاهُ، عَلَيْهِ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ التَّفْسِيرِ كَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَبِثُوا فِي كَهْفِهِمْ ثَلاثَ مِائَةٍ سِنِينَ وَازْدَادُوا تِسْعًا﴾ هَذَا قَوْلُ أهل الكتاب، وَقَدْ رَدَّهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قُلِ اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا لَبِثُوا﴾ قَالَ: وَفِي قِرَاءَةِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ: "وَقَالُوا: وَلَبِثُوا"، يَعْنِي أَنَّهُ قَالَهُ النَّاسُ 

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ -كَمَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ-مُطرَف بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ.

وَفِي هَذَا الَّذِي زَعَمَهُ قَتَادَةُ نَظَرٌ، فَإِنَّ الَّذِي بِأَيْدِي أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ أَنَّهُمْ لَبِثُوا ثَلَاثَمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ مِنْ غَيْرِ تِسْعٍ، يَعْنُونَ بِالشَّمْسِيَّةِ، وَلَوْ كَانَ اللَّهُ قَدْ حَكَى قَوْلَهُمْ لَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَازْدَادُوا تِسْعًا﴾ وَظَاهِرٌ مِنَ الْآيَةِ إِنَّمَا هُوَ إِخْبَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، لَا حِكَايَةَ عَنْهُمْ. وَهَذَا اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ. وَرِوَايَةُ قَتَادَةَ قِرَاءَةُ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ مُنْقَطِعَةٌ، ثُمَّ هِيَ شَاذَّةٌ بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى قِرَاءَةِ الْجُمْهُورِ فَلَا يُحْتَجُّ بِهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَبْصِرْ بِهِ وَأَسْمِعْ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّهُ لَبَصِيرٌ بِهِمْ سَمِيعٌ لَهُمْ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَذَلِكَ فِي مَعْنَى الْمُبَالَغَةِ فِي الْمَدْحِ، كَأَنَّهُ قِيلَ: مَا أَبْصَرَهُ وَأَسْمَعَهُ، وَتَأْوِيلُ الْكَلَامِ: مَا أَبْصَرَ اللَّهَ لِكُلِّ مَوْجُودٍ، وَأَسْمَعَهُ لِكُلِّ مَسْمُوعٍ، لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ شَيْءٌ.

ثُمَّ رُوِيَ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَبْصِرْ بِهِ وَأَسْمِعْ﴾ فَلَا أَحَدَ أَبْصَرُ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَلَا أَسْمَعُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: ﴿أَبْصِرْ بِهِ وَأَسْمِعْ﴾ يَرَى أَعْمَالَهُمْ، وَيَسْمَعُ ذَلِكَ مِنْهُمْ سَمِيعًا بَصِيرًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِهِ مِنْ وَلِيٍّ وَلا يُشْرِكُ فِي حُكْمِهِ أَحَدًا﴾ أَيْ: أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى هُوَ الَّذِي لَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالْأَمْرُ، الَّذِي لَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، وَلَيْسَ لَهُ وَزِيرٌ وَلَا نَصِيرٌ وَلَا شَرِيكٌ وَلَا مُشِيرٌ، تَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ.

---

## 18:27-28 — verses 27-28 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, commanding His Messenger [upon him be prayer and peace] to recite His mighty Book and to convey it to the people: {No one can alter His words} meaning, no one changes them, distorts them, or reinterprets them.

Concerning His saying {and you will never find besides Him a refuge}, [from Mujahid: he said "malja'an" (a refuge) means a place of shelter; and from Qatadah: "neither a protector nor a patron"], Ibn Jarir said: "He says: if you, O Muhammad, do not recite what has been revealed to you from your Lord's Book, then there will be no refuge for you from Allah." This is as the Almighty said: {O Messenger, convey what has been revealed to you from your Lord, and if you do not do so, then you have not conveyed His message. And Allah will protect you from the people} [al-Ma'idah: 67]. And He, the Almighty, said: {Indeed, He who has made the Qur'an obligatory upon you will surely bring you back to a place of return} [al-Qasas: 85], meaning: He will question you concerning what He made obligatory upon you of conveying the message.

Concerning His saying {And keep yourself patient with those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening, seeking His Face}, meaning: sit with those among Allah's servants who remember Allah, proclaim His oneness, praise Him, glorify Him, and magnify Him, calling upon Him morning and evening, whether they be poor or rich, strong or weak. It is said that this was revealed concerning the nobles of Quraysh, when they asked the Prophet ﷺ to sit with them alone and not to sit together with them in the company of his weaker companions such as Bilal, Ammar, Suhayb, [Khabbab], and Ibn Mas'ud, and that he should hold a separate gathering for those others. Allah forbade him from that, saying: {And do not drive away those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening} [al-An'am: 52] to the end of the verse, and He commanded him to be patient in sitting with these people, saying: {And keep yourself patient with those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening, seeking His Face}.

Muslim said in his Sahih: [chain] Sa'd, that is Ibn Abi Waqqas, said: "We were with the Prophet ﷺ, six men, and the polytheists said to the Prophet ﷺ: 'Drive these away, so that they do not grow bold against us!'" He said: "I was among them, along with Ibn Mas'ud, a man from Hudhayl, Bilal, and two men whose names I have forgotten. Something came into the mind of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, as Allah willed it to come, and he spoke to himself about it. Then Allah, Mighty and Sublime, revealed: {And do not drive away those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening, seeking His Face}." Muslim alone reported this, not al-Bukhari.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu al-Ja'd narrating from Abu Umamah, who said: "The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came upon a storyteller who was giving a sermon, and he stopped. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: 'Continue your sermon, for that I should sit from early morning until the sun rises is dearer to me than that I should free four slaves.'"

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Kurdus ibn Qays, who was the public storyteller of Kufa, said: "A man from among the Companions of Badr informed me that he heard the Prophet ﷺ say: 'That I should sit in a gathering like this one is dearer to me than that I should free four slaves.'" Shu'bah said: "So I asked, 'Which gathering?' He said: 'It was a storyteller's gathering.'"

Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said in his Musnad: [chain] Anas said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "That I should sit with a people who remember Allah from the dawn prayer until sunrise is dearer to me than all that the sun rises upon, and that I should remember Allah from the afternoon prayer until sunset is dearer to me than that I should free eight of the descendants of Isma'il, the blood price of each of them being twelve thousand." We calculated their blood prices while we were in the gathering of Anas, and it came to ninety-six thousand. And here there is someone who says "four of the descendants of Isma'il," but by Allah, he said nothing but "eight," the blood price of each of them being twelve thousand.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] al-Aghar Abu Muslim, who was from Kufah, reported that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by a man reciting Surat al-Kahf, and when he saw the Prophet ﷺ he fell silent. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "This is the gathering with which I have been commanded to keep myself patient."

Thus Abu Ahmad narrated it, from Amr ibn Thabit, from Ali ibn al-Aqmar, from al-Aghar, as a mursal (a report missing its Companion link) report. And it was also narrated to us by Yahya ibn al-Mu'alla, from Mansur, [chain] from Abu Hurayrah and Abu Sa'id, who said: "The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came while a man was reciting Surat al-Hijr or Surat al-Kahf, and he fell silent. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: 'This is the gathering with which I have been commanded to keep myself patient.'"

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Maymun ibn Siyah, from Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "There is no people who gather to remember Allah, seeking thereby nothing but His Face, except that a caller calls out to them from the heavens: 'Rise up, forgiven, for your evil deeds have been changed into good deeds.'" Ahmad alone reported this, may Allah have mercy on him.

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] Abd al-Rahman ibn Sahl ibn Hunayf said: "There was revealed to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, while he was in one of his houses, {And keep yourself patient with those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening, seeking His Face}. So he went out seeking them, and found a group of people remembering Allah the Almighty, among them one with disheveled hair, one with rough skin, and one with a single garment. When he saw them, he sat with them and said: 'Praise be to Allah, who has placed within my community those with whom Allah has commanded me to keep myself patient.'"

This Abd al-Rahman was mentioned by Abu Bakr ibn Abi Dawud among the Companions. As for his father, he was among the leading Companions, may Allah be pleased with them.

Concerning His saying {And let not your eyes pass beyond them, desiring the adornment of the worldly life}, Ibn Abbas said: "Do not pass beyond them to others," meaning: seeking in their place people of rank and wealth.

{And do not obey one whose heart We have made heedless of Our remembrance} meaning: one who has been diverted from religion and the worship of his Lord by the worldly life, {and follows his own desire, and whose affair is ever in reckless excess} meaning: his deeds and actions are folly, negligence, and waste. Do not be obedient to him, nor a lover of his way, nor envious of him for what he possesses, as the Almighty said: {And do not extend your eyes toward that which We have given certain groups of them to enjoy, the splendor of the worldly life, that We may test them thereby. And the provision of your Lord is better and more lasting} [Ta Ha: 131].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا رَسُولَهُ [عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ] بِتِلَاوَةِ كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ وَإِبْلَاغِهِ إِلَى النَّاسِ: ﴿لَا مُبَدِّلَ لِكَلِمَاتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا مُغَيِّرَ لَهَا وَلَا مُحَرِّفَ وَلَا مُؤَوِّلَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَنْ تَجِدَ مِنْ دُونِهِ مُلْتَحَدًا﴾ [عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿مُلْتَحَدًا﴾ قَالَ: مَلْجَأً. وَعَنْ قَتَادَةَ: وَلِيًّا وَلَا مَوْلًى] قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: يَقُولُ إِنْ أَنْتَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ لَمْ تَتْلُ مَا أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ كِتَابِ رَبِّكَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا مَلْجَأَ لَكَ مِنَ اللَّهِ". كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الرَّسُولُ بَلِّغْ مَا أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلْ فَمَا بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَتَهُ وَاللَّهُ يَعْصِمُكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٦٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِي فَرَضَ عَلَيْكَ الْقُرْآنَ لَرَادُّكَ إِلَى مَعَادٍ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٨٥] أَيْ: سَائِلُكَ عَمَّا فَرَضَ عَلَيْكَ مِنْ إِبْلَاغِ الرسالة.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاصْبِرْ نَفْسَكَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ يُرِيدُونَ وَجْهَهُ﴾ أَيْ: اجْلِسْ مَعَ الَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ وَيُهَلِّلُونَهُ، وَيَحْمَدُونَهُ وَيُسَبِّحُونَهُ وَيَكْبُرُونَهُ، وَيَسْأَلُونَهُ بِكُرَةً وَعَشِيًّا مِنْ عِبَادِ اللَّهِ، سَوَاءً كَانُوا فُقَرَاءَ أَوْ أَغْنِيَاءَ أَوْ أَقْوِيَاءَ أَوْ ضُعَفَاءَ. يُقَالُ: إِنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي أَشْرَافِ قُرَيْشٍ، حِينَ طَلَبُوا مِنَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنْ يَجْلِسَ مَعَهُمْ وَحْدَهُ وَلَا يُجَالِسَهُمْ بِضُعَفَاءِ أَصْحَابِهِ كَبِلَالٍ وَعَمَّارٍ وَصُهَيْبٍ [وَخَبَّابٍ] وَابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، وَلْيُفْرِدْ أُولَئِكَ بِمَجْلِسٍ عَلَى حِدَةٍ. فَنَهَاهُ اللَّهُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا تَطْرُدِ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٥٢] الْآيَةَ، وَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يُصَبِّرَ نَفْسَهُ فِي الْجُلُوسِ مَعَ هَؤُلَاءِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَاصْبِرْ نَفْسَكَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ يُرِيدُونَ وَجْهَهُ﴾

وَقَالَ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْأَسَدِيُّ، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنِ الْمِقْدَامِ بْنِ شُرَيْح، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ سَعْدٍ -هُوَ ابْنُ أَبِي وَقَاصٍّ-قَالَ: كُنَّا مَعَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ سِتَّةَ نَفَرٍ، فَقَالَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ: اطْرُدْ هَؤُلَاءِ لَا يَجْتَرِئُونَ عَلَيْنَا!. قَالَ: وَكُنْتُ أَنَا وَابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، وَرَجُلٌ مِنْ هُذَيْلٍ، وَبِلَالٌ وَرَجُلَانِ نَسِيتُ اسْمَيْهِمَا فَوَقَعَ فِي نَفْسِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَقَعَ، فَحَدَّثَ نَفْسَهُ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَلا تَطْرُدِ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ يُرِيدُونَ وَجْهَهُ﴾ انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ دُونَ الْبُخَارِيِّ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي التَّيَّاح قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا الْجَعْدِ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ قَالَ: خَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَى قَاصٍّ يَقُصُّ، فَأَمْسَكَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "قُص، فَلِأَنْ أَقْعُدَ غُدْوَةً إِلَى أَنْ تُشْرِقَ الشَّمْسُ، أَحَبُّ إليَّ مِنْ أَنْ أُعْتِقَ أَرْبَعَ رِقَابٍ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمٌ حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ مَيْسَرة قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ كُرْدُوس بْنَ قَيْسٍ -وَكَانَ قَاصَّ الْعَامَّةِ بِالْكُوفَةِ-يَقُولُ: أَخْبَرَنِي رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابٍ بَدْرٍ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "لِأَنْ أَقْعُدَ فِي مِثْلِ هَذَا الْمَجْلِسِ أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْ أَنْ أَعْتِقَ أَرْبَعَ رِقَابٍ". قَالَ شُعْبَةُ: فَقُلْتُ: أَيُّ مَجْلِسٍ؟ قَالَ: كَانَ قَاصًّا 

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدٌ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ أَبَانٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَأَنْ أُجَالِسَ قَوْمًا يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ مِنْ صَلَاةِ الْغَدَاةِ إِلَى طُلُوعِ الشَّمْسِ، أحَبّ إِلَيَّ مِمَّا طَلَعَتْ عَلَيْهِ الشَّمْسُ، وَلَأَنْ أَذْكُرَ اللَّهَ مِنْ صَلَاةِ الْعَصْرِ إِلَى غُرُوبِ الشَّمْسِ أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْ أَنْ أعتق ثَمَانِيَةً مِنْ وَلَدِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ دِيَةُ كُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمُ اثْنَا عَشَرَ أَلْفًا". فَحَسِبْنَا دِيَّاتِهِمْ وَنَحْنُ فِي مَجْلِسِ أَنَسٍ، فَبَلَغَتْ سِتَّةً وَتِسْعِينَ أَلْفًا، وَهَاهُنَا مَنْ يَقُولُ: "أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنْ وَلَدِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ" وَاللَّهِ مَا قَالَ إِلَّا ثَمَانِيَةً، دِيَةُ كُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمُ اثْنَا عَشَرَ أَلْفًا 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ الْأَهْوَازِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أَحْمَدَ الزُّبَيْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بن ثابت، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْأَقْمَرِ، عَنِ الْأَغَرِّ أَبِي مُسْلِمٍ -وَهُوَ الْكُوفِيُّ-أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَرَّ بِرَجُلٍ يَقْرَأُ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ سَكَتَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "هَذَا الْمَجْلِسُ الَّذِي أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أُصَبِّرَ نَفْسِي مَعَهُمْ".

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو أَحْمَدَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْأَقْمَرِ، عَنِ الْأَغَرِّ مُرْسَلًا. وَحَدَّثْنَاهُ يَحْيَى بْنُ الْمُعَلَّى، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الصَّلْتِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْأَقْمَرِ، عَنِ الْأَغَرِّ أَبِي مُسْلِمٍ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ وَأَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَا جَاءَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَرَجُلٌ يَقْرَأُ سُورَةَ الحِجْر أَوْ سُورَةَ الْكَهْفِ، فَسَكَتَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "هَذَا الْمَجْلِسُ الَّذِي أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أُصَبِّرَ نَفْسِي مَعَهُمْ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَكْرٍ حَدَّثَنَا مَيْمُونٌ المَرئي، حَدَّثَنَا مَيْمُونُ بْنُ سِيَاه، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ قَوْمٍ اجْتَمَعُوا يُذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ، لَا يُرِيدُونَ بِذَلِكَ إِلَّا وَجْهَهُ، إِلَّا نَادَاهُمْ مُنَادٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ: أَنْ قُومُوا مَغْفُورًا لَكُمْ، قَدْ بُدِّلت سيئاتُكُم حَسَنَاتٍ" تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ أُسَامَةَ بْنِ زَيْدٍ عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ سَهْلِ بْنِ حُنيف قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهُوَ فِي بَعْضِ أَبْيَاتِهِ: ﴿وَاصْبِرْ نَفْسَكَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ يُرِيدُونَ وَجْهَهُ﴾ فَخَرَجَ يَلْتَمِسُهُمْ، فَوَجَدَ قَوْمًا يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى، مِنْهُمْ ثَائِرُ الرَّأْسِ، وَجَافِي الْجِلْدِ وَذُو الثَّوْبِ الْوَاحِدِ، فَلَمَّا رَآهُمْ جَلَسَ مَعَهُمْ وَقَالَ: "الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي جَعَلَ فِي أُمَّتِي مَنْ أَمَرَنِي اللَّهُ أَنَّ أُصَبِّرَ نَفْسِي مَعَهُمْ" 

عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ هَذَا، ذَكَرَهُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي دَاوُدَ فِي الصَّحَابَةِ وَأَمَّا أبوه فمن سادات الصحابة، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تَعْدُ عَيْنَاكَ عَنْهُمْ تُرِيدُ زِينَةَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَلَا تُجَاوِزْهُمْ إِلَى غَيْرِهِمْ: يَعْنِي: تَطْلُبُ بَدَلَهُمْ أَصْحَابَ الشَّرَفِ وَالثَّرْوَةِ.

﴿وَلا تُطِعْ مَنْ أَغْفَلْنَا قَلْبَهُ عَنْ ذِكْرِنَا﴾ أَيْ: شُغِلَ عَنِ الدِّينِ وَعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِ بِالدُّنْيَا ﴿ [وَاتَّبَعَ هَوَاهُ] وَكَانَ أَمْرُهُ فُرُطًا﴾ أَيْ: أَعْمَالُهُ وَأَفْعَالُهُ سَفَهٌ وَتَفْرِيطٌ وَضَيَاعٌ، وَلَا تَكُنْ مُطِيعًا لَهُ وَلَا مُحِبًّا لِطَرِيقَتِهِ، وَلَا تَغْبِطْهُ بِمَا هُوَ فِيهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَمُدَّنَّ عَيْنَيْكَ إِلَى مَا مَتَّعْنَا بِهِ أَزْوَاجًا مِنْهُمْ زَهْرَةَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا لِنَفْتِنَهُمْ فِيهِ وَرِزْقُ رَبِّكَ خَيْرٌ وَأَبْقَى﴾ [طَه:١٣١]

---

## 18:29 — verse 29

### Translation

The Exalted says to His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ: Say, O Muhammad, to the people: this which I have brought to you from your Lord is the truth, in which there is no doubt and no uncertainty. {So whoever wills, let him believe, and whoever wills, let him disbelieve.} This is of the nature of threat and severe warning. That is why He said: {Indeed, We have prepared}, meaning We have made ready, {for the wrongdoers}, who are those who disbelieve in Allah, His Messenger, and His Book, {a fire whose walls (suradiq) will surround them}, meaning its enclosing wall.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "The suradiq (enclosing wall) of the Fire has four walls, the thickness of each wall being a distance of forty years."

Al-Tirmidhi reported it in "The Description of the Fire" and Ibn Jarir in his tafsir, from the hadith of Darraj Abu al-Samh, with this chain.

[Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said regarding {a fire whose walls will surround them}: he said, a wall of fire.]

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Ya'la ibn Umayyah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The sea, it is Hell (Jahannam)." He said: So it was said to him: [How is that?] So he recited this verse, or read this verse: {a fire whose walls will surround them}, then he said: "By Allah, I will never enter it, or: as long as I live, and not a single drop of it will touch me."

Regarding His saying: {And if they call for relief, they will be relieved with water like murky oil that scalds the faces. Wretched is the drink, and evil is the resting place}, Ibn Abbas said: "al-muhl" (murky oil) is a thick water like the dregs of olive oil.

Mujahid said: it is like blood and pus. Ikrimah said: it is that thing whose heat has reached its utmost. Others said: it is everything that has been melted.

Qatadah said: Ibn Mas'ud melted some gold in a trench, and when it dissolved and frothed, he said: this is the closest thing to al-muhl.

Al-Dahhak said: the water of Jahannam is black, and it (the fire) is black, and its people are black.

None of these statements negates the others, for al-muhl combines all these vile qualities together: it is black, foul-smelling, thick, and hot. That is why He said: {that scalds the faces}, meaning from its heat. When the disbeliever wants to drink it and brings it close to his face, it scalds him until the skin of his face falls into it, as has come in the hadith which Imam Ahmad related with the chain mentioned above regarding the suradiq of the Fire, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "water like al-muhl." He said: like the dregs of olive oil, and when he brings it close to himself, the skin of his face falls into it. Al-Tirmidhi likewise related it in "The Description of the Fire" in his Jami', from the hadith of Rishdin ibn Sa'd, from Amr ibn al-Harith, from Darraj, with this chain, then he said: we do not know it except from the hadith of "Rishdin," and there has been some discussion of him regarding his memory. This is what he said, but Imam Ahmad related it, as mentioned before, from Hasan al-Ashyab, from Ibn Lahi'ah, from Darraj. And Allah knows best.

Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak and Baqiyyah ibn al-Walid said, from Safwan ibn Amr, from Abdullah ibn Busr, from Abu Umamah, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding His saying: {and he is given to drink from purulent water which he sips little by little} [Ibrahim 14:16-17], he said: "It is brought close to him and he finds it repugnant, and when it is brought close to him it scalds his face and the skin of his head falls off, and when he drinks it, it cuts his intestines into pieces. Allah the Exalted says: {And if they call for relief, they will be relieved with water like murky oil that scalds the faces. Wretched is the drink.}"

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: when the people of the Fire become hungry, they call for relief with the tree of Zaqqum, and they eat from it, and it strips away the skins of their faces, so that if a passerby who knew them were to pass by them, he would recognize the skins of their faces within it. Then thirst is poured upon them and they call for relief. So they are relieved with water like al-muhl, which is that whose heat has reached its utmost, and when they bring it close to their mouths, the flesh of their faces, from which the skin has already fallen, is scalded by its heat.

That is why the Exalted, after describing this drink with these blameworthy, hideous qualities, said: {Wretched is the drink}, meaning wretched is this drink, just as He said in another verse: {and they were given scalding water to drink which cut their intestines into pieces} [Muhammad 47:15]. And the Exalted said: {given to drink from a boiling spring} [al-Ghashiyah 88:5], meaning hot, just as He said: {and between scalding water, heated to boiling} [al-Rahman 55:44]. {and evil is the resting place}, meaning and evil is the Fire as a dwelling, a place of rest, a gathering place, and a place of comfort, just as He said in another verse: {indeed it is evil as a settlement and residence} [al-Furqan 25:66].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ: وَقُلْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ لِلنَّاسِ: هَذَا الَّذِي جِئْتُكُمْ بِهِ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ هُوَ الْحَقُّ الذِي لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ وَلَا شَكَّ ﴿فَمَنْ شَاءَ فَلْيُؤْمِنْ وَمَنْ شَاءَ فَلْيَكْفُرْ﴾ هَذَا مِنْ بَابِ التَّهْدِيدِ وَالْوَعِيدِ الشَّدِيدِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّا أَعْتَدْنَا﴾ أَيْ: أَرْصَدْنَا ﴿لِلظَّالِمِينَ﴾ وَهُمُ الْكَافِرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ وَكِتَابِهِ ﴿نَارًا أَحَاطَ بِهِمْ سُرَادِقُهَا﴾ أَيْ: سُورُهَا.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهيعة، حَدَّثَنَا دَرَّاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "لسُرَادِق النَّارِ أَرْبَعَةُ جُدُر، كَثَافَةُ كُلِّ جِدَارٍ مَسَافَةَ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً".

وَأَخْرَجَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي "صِفَةِ النَّارِ" وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ دَرَّاجٍ أَبِي السَّمح بِهِ 

[وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَحَاطَ بِهِمْ سُرَادِقُهَا﴾ قَالَ: حَائِطٌ مِنْ نَارٍ] 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ نَصْرٍ وَالْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ حُيَيِّ بْنِ يَعْلَى، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ يَعْلَى، عَنْ يَعْلَى بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الْبَحْرُ هُوَ جَهَنَّمُ" قَالَ: فَقِيلَ لَهُ: [كَيْفَ ذَلِكَ؟] فَتَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ -أَوْ: قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ-: ﴿نَارًا أَحَاطَ بِهِمْ سُرَادِقُهَا﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ: "وَاللَّهِ لَا أَدْخُلُهَا أَبَدًا أَوْ: مَا دُمْتُ حَيًّا -وَلَا تُصِيبُنِي مِنْهَا قَطْرَةٌ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ يَسْتَغِيثُوا يُغَاثُوا بِمَاءٍ كَالْمُهْلِ يَشْوِي الْوُجُوهَ بِئْسَ الشَّرَابُ وَسَاءَتْ مُرْتَفَقًا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: "الْمُهْلُ": مَاءٌ غَلِيظٌ مِثْلُ دُرْدِيِّ الزَّيْتِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هُوَ كَالدَّمِ وَالْقَيْحِ. وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: هُوَ الشَّيْءُ الَّذِي انْتَهَى حَرّه: وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: هُوَ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ أُذِيبَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَذَابَ ابنُ مَسْعُودٍ شَيْئًا مِنَ الذَّهَبِ فِي أُخْدُودٍ، فَلَمَّا انْمَاعَ وَأَزْبَدَ قَالَ: هَذَا أَشْبَهُ شَيْءٍ بِالْمُهْلِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: مَاءُ جَهَنَّمَ أَسْوَدُ، وَهِيَ سَوْدَاءُ وَأَهْلُهَا سُودٌ.

وَهَذِهِ الْأَقْوَالُ لَيْسَ شَيْءٌ مِنْهَا يَنْفِي الْآخَرَ، فَإِنَّ الْمُهْلَ يَجْمَعُ هَذِهِ الْأَوْصَافَ الرَّذِيلَةَ كُلَّهَا، فَهُوَ أَسْوَدُ مُنْتِنٌ غَلِيظٌ حَارٌّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَشْوِي الْوُجُوهَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ حَرِّهِ، إِذَا أَرَادَ الْكَافِرُ أَنْ يَشْرَبَهُ وقَرّبه مِنْ وَجْهِهِ، شَوَاهُ حَتَّى يَسْقُطَ جِلْدُ وَجْهِهِ فِيهِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بِإِسْنَادِهِ الْمُتَقَدِّمِ فِي سُرادِق النَّارِ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "مَاءٍ كَالْمُهْلِ". قَالَ كَعَكْرِ الزَّيْتِ فَإِذَا قَرَّبَهُ إِلَيْهِ سَقَطَتْ فَرْوَةُ وَجْهِهِ فِيهِ" وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي "صِفَةِ النَّارِ" مِنْ جَامِعِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ رِشْدِين بْنِ سَعْدٍ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ دَرَّاجٍ، بِهِ ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ "رِشْدِينَ"، وَقَدْ تُكُلِّمَ فِيهِ مِنْ قِبَلِ حِفْظِهِ،، هَكَذَا قَالَ، وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ عَنْ حَسَنٍ الْأَشْيَبِ، عَنِ ابْنِ لَهِيعة، عَنْ دَرّاج، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، وبَقِيَّة بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ بُسْر، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَيُسْقَى مِنْ مَاءٍ صَدِيدٍ يَتَجَرَّعُهُ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ:١٦، ١٧] قَالَ: "يُقَرَّبُ إِلَيْهِ فيَتَكرّهه، فَإِذَا قُرِّبَ مِنْهُ شَوَى وجهَه وَوَقَعَتْ فروةُ رَأْسِهِ، فَإِذَا شَرِبَهُ قَطَّعَ أَمْعَاءَهُ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ يَسْتَغِيثُوا يُغَاثُوا بِمَاءٍ كَالْمُهْلِ يَشْوِي الْوُجُوهَ بِئْسَ الشَّرَابُ﴾ .

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: إِذَا جَاعَ أَهْلُ النَّارِ اسْتَغَاثُوا بِشَجَرَةِ الزَّقُّومِ، فَأَكَلُوا مِنْهَا فَاخْتَلَسَتْ جُلُودَ وُجُوهِهِمْ، فَلَوْ أَنَّ مَارًّا مَرَّ بِهِمْ يَعْرِفُهُمْ، لَعَرَفَ جُلُودَ وُجُوهِهِمْ فِيهَا. ثُمَّ يَصُبُّ عَلَيْهِمُ الْعَطَشَ فَيَسْتَغِيثُونَ. فَيُغَاثُونَ بِمَاءٍ كَالْمُهْلِ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي قَدِ انْتَهَى حَرُّهُ، فَإِذَا أَدْنَوْهُ مِنْ أَفْوَاهِهِمُ اشْتَوَى مِنْ حَرِّهِ لُحُومُ وُجُوهِهِمُ الَّتِي قَدْ سَقَطَتْ عَنْهَا الْجُلُودُ.

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى بَعْدَ وَصْفِهِ هَذَا الشَّرَابَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ [الذَّمِيمَةِ] الْقَبِيحَةِ: ﴿بِئْسَ الشَّرَابُ﴾ أَيْ: بِئْسَ هَذَا الشَّرَابُ كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَسُقُوا مَاءً حَمِيمًا فَقَطَّعَ أَمْعَاءَهُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ:١٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿تُسْقَى مِنْ عَيْنٍ آنِيَةٍ﴾ [الْغَاشِيَةِ:٥] أَيْ: حَارَّةٍ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَبَيْنَ حَمِيمٍ آنٍ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٤٤] ﴿وَسَاءَتْ مُرْتَفَقًا﴾ [أَيْ: وَسَاءَتِ النَّارُ] مَنْزِلًا ومَقِيلا وَمُجْتَمَعًا وَمَوْضِعًا لِلِارْتِفَاقِ كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿إِنَّهَا سَاءَتْ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَمُقَامًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٦٦]

---

## 18:30-31 — verses 30-31 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the state of the wretched, He followed it by mentioning the fortunate ones, those who believed in Allah and confirmed the messengers in what they brought, and acted upon the righteous deeds they commanded them to do. So for them are {Gardens of Eden}, and al-Adn (Eden) means permanent residence.

{Beneath them rivers flow}, meaning beneath their chambers and dwellings. Pharaoh said [to them]: {And these rivers flowing beneath me} [al-Zukhruf: 51].

{They will be adorned}, that is, with ornaments, {therein with bracelets of gold}. And He said in another place: {and pearls, and their garments therein will be silk} [al-Hajj: 23]. Here He detailed it, saying: {and they will wear green garments of sundus (fine silk) and istabraq (thick brocade)}. As for sundus, it is a garment of thin, fine fabric like shirts and similar things, while istabraq is thick brocade that has a sheen in it.

Regarding His saying: {reclining therein on couches}, it is said that al-ittika' (reclining) means lying down, and it is also said that it means sitting cross-legged, and this latter meaning is closer to what is intended here. From this comes the hadith in the Sahih: "As for me, I do not eat reclining," in which both interpretations apply.

Al-ara'ik (couches) is the plural of arikah, which is a bed set beneath a canopy (hajalah). The hajalah, as people of our time recognize it, is what is called al-bashkhanah (a curtained bridal enclosure). And Allah knows best.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from Qatadah, regarding {on couches}, he said: they are the canopies. Ma'mar said: and someone other than him said: they are beds within the canopies.

Regarding His saying: {Excellent is the reward, and good is the resting place}, meaning: excellent is Paradise as a reward for their deeds, and {good is the resting place}, meaning good as a dwelling, a place of repose, and a station, just as He said concerning the Fire: {Wretched is the drink, and evil is the resting place} [al-Kahf: 29]. Thus He contrasted the two similarly in Surat al-Furqan, in His saying: {Indeed, it is evil as a settlement and residence} [al-Furqan: 66]. Then He mentioned the qualities of the believers, saying: {Those will be rewarded with the highest chamber for what they patiently endured, and they will be met therein with greeting and peace, abiding therein eternally. Good it is as a settlement and residence} [al-Furqan: 75-76].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى حَالَ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ، ثَنَّى بِذِكْرِ السُّعَدَاءِ، الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بالله وصدقوا المرسلين فيما جاؤوا بِهِ، وَعَمِلُوا بِمَا أَمَرُوهُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ الصَّالِحَةِ، فَلَهُمْ ﴿جَنَّاتُ عَدْنٍ﴾ وَالْعَدْنُ: الْإِقَامَةُ.

﴿تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهِمُ الأنْهَارُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ تَحْتِ غُرَفِهِمْ وَمَنَازِلِهِمْ، قَالَ [لَهُمْ] فِرْعَوْنُ: ﴿وَهَذِهِ الأنْهَارُ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِي﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٥١] .

﴿يُحَلَّوْنَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْحِلْيَةِ ﴿فِيهَا مِنْ أَسَاوِرَ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ﴾ وَقَالَ فِي الْمَكَانِ الْآخَرِ: ﴿وَلُؤْلُؤًا وَلِبَاسُهُمْ فِيهَا حَرِيرٌ﴾ [الْحَجِّ:٢٣] وَفَصَّلَهُ هَاهُنَا فَقَالَ: ﴿وَيَلْبَسُونَ ثِيَابًا خُضْرًا مِنْ سُنْدُسٍ وَإِسْتَبْرَقٍ﴾ فالسندس: لباس رقاع رقاق كَالْقُمْصَانِ وَمَا جَرَى مَجْرَاهَا، وَأَمَّا الْإِسْتَبْرَقُ فَغَلِيظُ الدِّيبَاجِ وَفِيهِ بَرِيقٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مُتَّكِئِينَ فِيهَا عَلَى الأرَائِكِ﴾ الِاتِّكَاءُ قِيلَ: الِاضْطِجَاعُ وَقِيلَ التَّرَبُّعُ فِي الْجُلُوسِ. وَهُوَ أَشْبَهُ بِالْمُرَادِ هَاهُنَا وَمِنْهُ الْحَدِيثُ [فِي] الصَّحِيحِ: "أَمَّا أَنَا فَلَا آكُلُ مُتَّكِئًا " فِيهِ الْقَوْلَانِ.

وَالْأَرَائِكُ: جَمَعَ أَرِيكَةٍ، وَهِيَ السَّرِيرُ تَحْتَ الحَجَلة، وَالْحَجَلَةُ كَمَا يَعَرِّفُهُ النَّاسُ فِي زَمَانِنَا هَذَا بِالْبَاشخَانَاه، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَرُ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: ﴿عَلَى الأرَائِكِ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ الْحِجَالُ. قَالَ مَعْمَرٌ: وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: السّرُر فِي الْحِجَالِ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿نِعْمَ الثَّوَابُ وَحَسُنَتْ مُرْتَفَقًا﴾ [أَيْ: نِعْمَتِ الْجَنَّةُ ثَوَابًا عَلَى أَعْمَالِهِمْ ﴿وَحَسُنَتْ مُرْتَفَقًا﴾ أَيْ: حَسُنَتْ مَنْزِلًا وَمَقِيلًا وَمَقَامًا، كَمَا قَالَ فِي النَّارِ: ﴿بِئْسَ الشَّرَابُ وَسَاءَتْ مُرْتَفَقًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ:٢٩] ، وَهَكَذَا قَابَلَ بَيْنَهُمَا فِي سُورَةِ الْفُرْقَانِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّهَا سَاءَتْ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَمُقَامًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٦٦] ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ صِفَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فَقَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ يُجْزَوْنَ الْغُرْفَةَ بِمَا صَبَرُوا وَيُلَقَّوْنَ فِيهَا تَحِيَّةً وَسَلامًا خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا حَسُنَتْ مُسْتَقَرًّا وَمُقَامًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٧٦، ٧٥] .

---

## 18:32-36 — verses 32-36 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah Most High says, after mentioning the polytheists who disdained sitting with the weak and the poor among the Muslims and boasted over them with their wealth and lineage, that He struck for them a parable of two men. Allah made {for one of them two gardens}, that is, two orchards of grapevines, hedged about with date palms encircling their sides, with crops growing in between them, and each of the trees and crops was fruitful and thriving in the utmost degree of abundance. It is for this reason that He said: {Both gardens brought forth their produce}, meaning they yielded their fruit, {and withheld nothing thereof}, meaning it did not fall short in anything, {and We caused a river to flow between them}, meaning rivers ran through them here and there.

{And he had fruit} (thamar): it was said that what is meant by it is wealth. This was reported from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and Qatadah. And it was said that it means fruits, and this is the more evident meaning here, and it is supported by another reading, "wa kana lahu thumr" with the tha' vowelled with damma and the mim vowelled with sukun, in which case it would be the plural of thamarah (fruit), like khashabah and khushub. Others read it as {thamarun} with the tha' and mim both vowelled with fatha.

So he, that is the owner of these two gardens, said {to his companion while conversing with him}, meaning while disputing and arguing with him, boasting over him and lording it over him: {I have more wealth than you and am mightier in respect of men}, meaning more numerous in servants, retainers, and children.

Qatadah said: That, by Allah, is the aspiration of the wicked person: abundance of wealth and might of following.

And His saying: {And he entered his garden while he was wronging himself}, meaning through his disbelief, his rebelliousness, his arrogance, his tyranny, and his denial of the resurrection, {he said, I do not think that this will ever perish}. This was a delusion on his part; when he saw the crops, fruits, trees, and the flowing rivers running along its sides and expanses, he supposed that it would never perish, never run out, never be destroyed, and never be spoiled. That was due to the weakness of his reason, the feebleness of his certainty in Allah, his infatuation with worldly life and its adornment, and his disbelief in the Hereafter. It is for this reason that he said: {And I do not think the Hour will come to pass}, meaning that it will occur, {and even if I am returned to my Lord, I will surely find something better than this in return}, meaning: even if there is a resurrection, a return, and a going-back to Allah, then I will surely have there something better than this, because I am favored with my Lord, and were it not for my esteemed standing with Him, He would not have given me this. As He said in another verse: {And if I am returned to my Lord, indeed I will have with Him the best} [Fussilat: 50], and He said: {Have you seen the one who disbelieved in Our signs and said, I will surely be given wealth and children} [Maryam: 77], meaning in the abode of the Hereafter, swearing an oath against Allah, Mighty and Majestic. The occasion of the revelation of this verse concerned al-'Aas ibn Wa'il, as will be explained in its place, if Allah Most High wills, and in Him is trust.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بَعْدَ ذِكْرِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ الْمُسْتَكْبِرِينَ عَنْ مُجَالَسَةِ الضُّعَفَاءِ وَالْمَسَاكِينِ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، وَافْتَخَرُوا عَلَيْهِمْ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَحْسَابِهِمْ، فَضَرَبَ لَهُمْ مَثَلًا بِرَجُلَيْنِ، جَعَلَ اللَّهُ ﴿لأحَدِهِمَا جَنَّتَيْنِ﴾ أَيْ: بُسْتَانَيْنِ مِنْ أَعْنَابٍ، مَحْفُوفَتَيْنِ بِالنَّخْلِ الْمُحْدِقَةِ فِي جَنْبَاتِهِمَا، وَفِي خِلَالِهِمَا الزُّرُوعُ، وَكُلٌّ مِنَ الْأَشْجَارِ وَالزُّرُوعِ مُثْمِرٌ مُقبلٌ فِي غَايَةِ الْجُودِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كِلْتَا الْجَنَّتَيْنِ آتَتْ أُكُلَهَا﴾ أَيْ: خَرَجَتْ ثَمَرُهَا ﴿وَلَمْ تَظْلِمْ مِنْهُ شَيْئًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَمْ تَنْقُصْ مِنْهُ شَيْئًا ﴿وَفَجَّرْنَا خِلالَهُمَا نَهَرًا﴾ أَيْ: وَالْأَنْهَارُ تَتَخَرِقُ فِيهِمَا هَاهُنَا وَهَاهُنَا.

﴿وَكَانَ لَهُ ثَمَرٌ﴾ قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِهِ: الْمَالُ. رُوي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَقَتَادَةَ. وَقِيلَ: الثِّمَارُ وَهُوَ أَظْهَرُ هَاهُنَا، وَيُؤَيِّدُهُ الْقِرَاءَةُ الْأُخْرَى: "وَكَانَ لَهُ ثُمْر" بِضَمِّ الثَّاءِ وَتَسْكِينِ الْمِيمِ، فَيَكُونُ جَمْعَ ثَمَرَة، كَخَشَبَة وخُشب، وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: ﴿ثَمَرٌ﴾ بِفَتْحِ الثَّاءِ وَالْمِيمِ.

فَقَالَ -أَيْ صَاحِبُ هَاتَيْنِ [الْجَنَّتَيْنِ] - ﴿لِصَاحِبِهِ وَهُوَ يُحَاوِرُهُ﴾ أَيْ: يُجَادِلُهُ وَيُخَاصِمُهُ، يَفْتَخِرُ عَلَيْهِ وَيَتَرَأَّسُ: ﴿أَنَا أَكْثَرُ مِنْكَ مَالا وَأَعَزُّ نَفَرًا﴾ أَيْ: أَكْثَرُ خَدَمًا وَحَشَمًا وَوَلَدًا.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: تِلْكَ -وَاللَّهِ-أُمْنِيَةُ الْفَاجِرِ: كَثْرَةُ الْمَالِ وَعِزَّةُ النَّفَرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَدَخَلَ جَنَّتَهُ وَهُوَ ظَالِمٌ لِنَفْسِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِكُفْرِهِ وَتَمَرُّدِهِ وَتَكَبُّرِهِ وَتَجَبُّرِهِ وَإِنْكَارِهِ الْمَعَادَ ﴿قَالَ مَا أَظُنُّ أَنْ تَبِيدَ هَذِهِ أَبَدًا﴾ وَذَلِكَ اغْتِرَارٌ مِنْهُ، لَمَّا رَأَى فِيهَا مِنَ الزُّرُوعِ وَالثِّمَارِ وَالْأَشْجَارِ وَالْأَنْهَارِ الْمُطَّرِدَةِ فِي جَوَانِبِهَا وَأَرْجَائِهَا، ظَنَّ أَنَّهَا لَا تَفْنَى وَلَا تَفْرَغُ وَلَا تَهْلَكُ وَلَا تُتْلَفُ وَذَلِكَ لِقِلَّةِ عَقْلِهِ، وَضَعْفِ يَقِينِهِ بِاللَّهِ، وَإِعْجَابِهِ بِالْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتِهَا، وَكُفْرِهِ بِالْآخِرَةِ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا أَظُنُّ السَّاعَةَ قَائِمَةً﴾ أَيْ: كَائِنَةً ﴿وَلَئِنْ رُدِدْتُ إِلَى رَبِّي لأجِدَنَّ خَيْرًا مِنْهَا مُنْقَلَبًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَئِنْ كَانَ مَعَادٌ وَرَجْعَةٌ وَمَرَدٌّ إِلَى اللَّهِ، ليكونَنّ لِي هُنَاكَ أَحْسَنَ مِنْ هَذَا لِأَنِّي مُحظى عِنْدَ رَبِّي، وَلَوْلَا كَرَامَتِي عَلَيْهِ مَا أَعْطَانِي هَذَا، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَلَئِنْ رُجِعْتُ إِلَى رَبِّي إِنَّ لِي عِنْدَهُ لَلْحُسْنَى﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ:٥٠] ، وَقَالَ ﴿أَفَرَأَيْتَ الَّذِي كَفَرَ بِآيَاتِنَا وَقَالَ لأوتَيَنَّ مَالا وَوَلَدًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ:٧٧] أَيْ: فِي الدار الآخرة، تألى على الله، عز وَجَلَّ، وَكَانَ سَبَبُ نُزُولِهَا فِي الْعَاصِ بْنِ وَائِلٍ، كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ فِي مَوْضِعِهِ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ.

---

## 18:37-41 — verses 37-41 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing of how his believing companion answered him, admonishing him and restraining him from the disbelief in Allah and the delusion he was in: {Have you disbelieved in the One who created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then fashioned you into a man?} This is a repudiation and an expression of how grave was the denial he had fallen into, of his Lord, who created him and began the creation of mankind from clay, that being Adam, then made his progeny from an extract of despised fluid, as the Exalted said: {How can you disbelieve in Allah when you were dead and He gave you life, then He will cause you to die, then He will bring you to life} [al-Baqarah: 28], meaning: how can you deny your Lord when the proof of Him upon you is manifest and clear, known to every person from within himself. For there is no one among created beings but knows that he was once nonexistent and then came into existence, and that his existence was not from himself, nor dependent upon anything else among created things, since that thing would be in the same position as himself. Thus it is known that his coming into existence must be attributed to his Creator, who is Allah, there is no god but He, Creator of all things. That is why he said: {But as for me, He is Allah, my Lord}, meaning: I do not say what you say, rather I acknowledge for Allah His lordship and His oneness, {and I do not associate anyone with my Lord}, meaning: rather He alone is Allah, the One worshipped, with no partner.

Then he said: {And why, when you entered your garden, did you not say: What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah? Though you see me as less than you in wealth and children.} This is an incitement and encouragement toward that, meaning: why did you not, when it impressed you as you entered it and looked upon it, praise Allah for what He had favored you with, and for what He had given you of wealth and children that He had not given to others, and say: {What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah}? For this reason some of the Salaf (early generations) said: whoever is impressed by something of his state, his wealth, or his children, let him say: {What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah}. This is taken from this noble verse. A marfu' (elevated) hadith has been reported concerning it, recorded by the Hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili in his Musnad:

[chain] Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah never bestows upon a servant a favor of family, wealth, or children, and the servant says: {What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah}, but he is protected from every affliction short of death." And he used to interpret this in light of this verse: {And why, when you entered your garden, did you not say: What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah?}

Hafiz Abu al-Fath al-Azdi said: Isa ibn Awn, from Abd al-Malik ibn Zurarah, from Anas: his hadith is not sound.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "Shall I not direct you to a treasure among the treasures of Paradise? There is no power except by Allah." Ahmad alone transmitted this.

It is established in the Sahih, on the authority of Abu Musa, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to him: "Shall I not direct you to a treasure among the treasures of Paradise? There is no power and no strength except by Allah."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Amr ibn Maymun said: Abu Hurayrah said: The Prophet of Allah ﷺ said to me: "O Abu Hurayrah, shall I direct you to a treasure among the treasures of Paradise, beneath the Throne?" He said: I said: Yes, may my father and mother be ransomed for you. He said: "That you say: there is no power except by Allah." Abu Balj said: and I think he said: "For Allah says: My servant has submitted and surrendered." He said: I said to Amr, Abu Balj said: Amr said: I said to Abu Hurayrah: "There is no might and no power except by Allah"? He said: No, it is in Surat al-Kahf: {And why, when you entered your garden, did you not say: What Allah wills, there is no power except by Allah?}

His saying: {It may be that my Lord will give me something better than your garden}, meaning: in the Hereafter, {and send upon it}, meaning upon your garden in this world which you supposed would never perish or come to an end, {a calamity from the sky}. Ibn Abbas, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, and Malik, from al-Zuhri, said: meaning a punishment from the sky.

The apparent meaning is that it is a mighty, devastating rain that uproots its crops and trees. That is why He said: {so that it becomes a bare slippery ground}, meaning barren, smooth soil in which no foot can find footing.

Ibn Abbas said: like a barren wasteland that grows nothing.

His saying: {or its water becomes sunken}, meaning sinking into the earth, the opposite of a spring whose surface is sought at the top of the ground. What is sunken is sought at its depths, as the Exalted said: {Say: have you considered, if your water were to become sunken, who then could bring you flowing water?} [al-Mulk: 30], meaning flowing and running. Here He says: {or its water becomes sunken, so you would never be able to seek it out}. Ghawr (sunken) is a verbal noun with the meaning of gha'ir (sinking), and it is more emphatic than that form, as the poet said:

"Its steeds remain mourning over him, arrayed, their reins draped upon them,"

meaning: wailing over him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَمَّا أَجَابَهُ صَاحِبُهُ الْمُؤْمِنُ، وَاعِظًا لَهُ وَزَاجِرًا عَمَّا هُوَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ بِاللَّهِ وَالِاغْتِرَارِ: ﴿أَكَفَرْتَ بِالَّذِي خَلَقَكَ مِنْ تُرَابٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ ثُمَّ سَوَّاكَ رَجُلا﴾ ؟ وَهَذَا إِنْكَارٌ وَتَعْظِيمٌ لِمَا وَقَعَ فِيهِ مِنْ جُحُودِ رَبِّهِ، الَّذِي خَلَقَهُ وَابْتَدَأَ خَلْقَ الْإِنْسَانِ مَنْ طِينٍ وَهُوَ آدَمُ، ثُمَّ جَعَلَ نَسْلَهُ مِنْ سُلَالَةٍ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَيْفَ تَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَكُنْتُمْ أَمْوَاتًا فَأَحْيَاكُمْ ثُمَّ يُمِيتُكُمْ ثُمَّ يُحْيِيكُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٢٨٠] أَيْ: كَيْفَ تجحَدُون رَبَّكُمْ، وَدَلَالَتُهُ عَلَيْكُمْ ظَاهِرَةٌ جَلِيَّةٌ، كُلُّ أَحَدٍ يَعْلَمُهَا مِنْ نَفْسِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ مَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ مِنَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ إِلَّا وَيَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ كَانَ مَعْدُومًا ثُمَّ وُجِدَ، وَلَيْسَ وُجُودُهُ مِنْ نَفْسِهِ وَلَا مُسْتَنِدًا إِلَى شَيْءٍ مِنَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ بِمَثابَتِهِ فَعُلِمَ إِسْنَادُ إِيجَادِهِ إِلَى خَالِقِهِ، وَهُوَ اللَّهُ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، خَالِقُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ؛ وَلِذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَكِنَّا هُوَ اللَّهُ رَبِّي﴾ أَيْ: أَنَا لَا أَقُولُ بِمَقَالَتِكَ، بَلْ أَعْتَرِفُ لِلَّهِ بِالرُّبُوبِيَّةِ وَالْوَحْدَانِيَّةِ ﴿وَلا أُشْرِكُ بِرَبِّي أَحَدًا﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ هُوَ اللَّهُ الْمَعْبُودُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْلا إِذْ دَخَلْتَ جَنَّتَكَ قُلْتَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ إِنْ تَرَنِ أَنَا أَقَلَّ مِنْكَ مَالا وَوَلَدًا﴾ هَذَا تَحْضِيضٌ وَحَثٌّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، أَيْ: هَلَّا إِذَا أَعْجَبَتْكَ حِينَ دَخَلْتَهَا وَنَظَرْتَ إِلَيْهَا حَمِدْتَ اللَّهَ عَلَى مَا أَنْعَمَ به عليك، وأعطاك من المال والولد مَا لَمْ يُعْطَهُ غَيْرُكَ، وَقُلْتَ: ﴿مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ بَعْضَ السَّلَفِ: مَنْ أَعْجَبَهُ شَيْءٌ مِنْ حَالِهِ أَوْ مَالِهِ أَوْ وَلَدِهِ أَوْ مَالِهِ، فَلْيَقُلْ: ﴿مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ وَهَذَا مَأْخُوذٌ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ. وَقَدْ رُوِيَ فِيهِ حَدِيثٌ مَرْفُوعٌ أَخْرَجَهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ:

حَدَّثَنَا جَرَّاح بْنُ مَخْلَد، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا عِيسَى بْنُ عَوْن، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ زُرَارَة، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَى عَبْدٍ نِعْمَةً مِنْ أَهْلٍ أَوْ مَالٍ أَوْ وَلَدٍ، فَيَقُولُ: ﴿مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ فَيَرَى فِيهِ آفَةً دُونَ الْمَوْتِ". وَكَانَ يَتَأَوَّلُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَلَوْلا إِذْ دَخَلْتَ جَنَّتَكَ قُلْتَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ .

قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْفَتْحِ الْأَزْدِيُّ: عِيسَى بْنُ عَوْنٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ زُرَارَةَ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ: لَا يَصِحُّ حَدِيثُهُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ وَحَجَّاجٌ، حَدَّثَنِي شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ عُبَيْدٍ مَوْلَى أَبِي رُهْم، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "أَلَّا أَدُلُّكَ عَلَى كَنْزٍ مِنْ كُنُوزِ الْجَنَّةِ؟ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ 

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ لَهُ: "أَلَّا أَدُلُّكَ عَلَى كَنْزٍ مِنْ كُنُوزِ الْجَنَّةِ؟ لَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا بَكْرُ بْنُ عِيسَى، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عَنْ أَبِي بَلَج، عَنْ عَمْرو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ قَالَ: قَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: قَالَ لِي نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَا أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ، أَدُلُّكَ عَلَى كَنْزٍ مِنْ كُنُوزِ الْجَنَّةِ تَحْتَ الْعَرْشِ؟ ". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ، فِدَاكَ أَبِي وَأُمِّي. قَالَ: "أَنْ تَقُولَ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ" قَالَ أَبُو بَلْج: وَأَحْسَبُ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: أَسْلَمَ عَبْدِي وَاسْتَسْلَمَ". قَالَ: فَقُلْتُ لِعَمْرٍو -قَالَ أَبُو بَلْج: قَالَ عَمْرو: قُلْتُ لِأَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ: لَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ؟ فَقَالَ: لَا إِنَّهَا فِي سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ: ﴿وَلَوْلا إِذْ دَخَلْتَ جَنَّتَكَ قُلْتَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلا بِاللَّهِ﴾ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَعَسَى رَبِّي أَنْ يُؤْتِيَنِ خَيْرًا مِنْ جَنَّتِكَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ ﴿وَيُرْسِلَ عَلَيْهَا﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى جَنَّتِكَ فِي الدُّنْيَا الَّتِي ظَنَنْتَ أَنَّهَا لَا تَبِيدُ وَلَا تَفْنَى ﴿حُسْبَانًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَمَالِكٌ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ: أَيْ عَذَابًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ.

وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ مَطَرٌ عَظِيمٌ مُزْعِجٌ، يُقْلِعُ زَرْعَهَا وَأَشْجَارَهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَتُصْبِحَ صَعِيدًا زَلَقًا﴾ أَيْ: بَلْقَعًا تُرَابًا أَمْلَسَ، لَا يَثْبُتُ فِيهِ قَدم.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كالجُرز الَّذِي لَا يُنْبِتُ شَيْئًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوْ يُصْبِحَ مَاؤُهَا غَوْرًا﴾ أَيْ: غَائِرًا فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَهُوَ ضِدُّ النَّابِعِ الَّذِي يُطْلَبُ وَجْهَ الْأَرْضِ، فَالْغَائِرُ يُطْلَبُ أَسْفَلَهَا كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ أَصْبَحَ مَاؤُكُمْ غَوْرًا فَمَنْ يَأْتِيكُمْ بِمَاءٍ مَعِينٍ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:٣٠] أَيْ: جَارٍ وَسَائِجٍ. وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿أَوْ يُصْبِحَ مَاؤُهَا غَوْرًا فَلَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ لَهُ طَلَبًا﴾ وَالْغَوْرُ: مَصْدَرٌ بِمَعْنَى غَائِرٍ، وَهُوَ أَبْلَغُ مِنْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ 

تَظَلّ جيّادُهُ نَوْحًا عَلَيه ... تُقَلّدُهُ أعنَّتَها صُفُوفا ...

بمعنى نائحات عليه.

---

## 18:42-44 — verses 42-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says: {and his fruit was encompassed} meaning his wealth, or his fruits according to the other view. The point is that what the believer had warned this disbeliever about befell him: the sending down of a calamity upon his garden, which he had been deceived by and which had distracted him from Allah, mighty and majestic is He. {So he began to turn his hands about over what he had spent on it}. Qatadah said: he claps his hands together, grieving and lamenting over the wealth that had been destroyed upon him, {and he says: would that I had not associated anyone with my Lord, and he had no group} meaning kinsmen or offspring, as he had boasted of them and sought strength through them, {to help him besides Allah, nor could he defend himself. There, all protection belongs to Allah, the True}.

The reciters differ here. Some of them pause at His saying: {nor could he defend himself, there} meaning, in that place where Allah's punishment descended upon him, there was no rescuer from it. Then they begin with {al-wilayah belongs to Allah, the True}. Others pause at {nor could he defend himself}, and begin with {there, al-wilayah belongs to Allah, the True}.

Then they further differ regarding the recitation of {al-wilayah}. Some read the waw with fatha, so the meaning becomes: there, allegiance belongs to Allah, meaning that there, every person, whether believer or disbeliever, returns to Allah and to allegiance to Him and submission to Him when the punishment occurs, just as He says: {But when they saw Our punishment, they said: we believe in Allah alone and we disbelieve in what we used to associate with Him} [Ghafir: 84], and as He says, reporting concerning Pharaoh: {Until, when drowning overtook him, he said: I believe that there is no god except He in whom the Children of Israel believe, and I am of those who submit. Now? And you had disobeyed before and were among the corrupters} [Yunus: 90, 91].

Others read the waw of {al-wilayah} with kasra, meaning: there, judgment belongs to Allah, the True.

Then among these, some read {al-Haqq} in the nominative as a description of al-wilayah, as in His saying: {Sovereignty on that day, the true one, belongs to the Most Merciful, and it will be a difficult day for the disbelievers} [al-Furqan: 26].

Others read the qaf with a genitive ending, making it a description of Allah, mighty and majestic is He, as in His saying: {Then they are returned to Allah, their true Protector. Unquestionably, His is the judgment, and He is the swiftest of accountants} [al-An'am: 62]. For this reason the Exalted says: {He is better in reward} meaning recompense, {and better in outcome}, meaning that the deeds which are done for Allah, mighty and majestic is He, their reward is good and their outcome is praiseworthy and rightly guided, all of it good.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأُحِيطَ بِثَمَرِهِ﴾ بِأَمْوَالِهِ، أَوْ بِثِمَارِهِ عَلَى الْقَوْلِ الْآخَرِ. وَالْمَقْصُودُ أَنَّهُ وَقَعَ بِهَذَا الْكَافِرِ مَا كَانَ يَحْذَرُ، مِمَّا خَوَّفه بِهِ الْمُؤْمِنُ مِنْ إِرْسَالِ الْحُسْبَانِ عَلَى جَنَّتِهِ، الَّتِي اغْتَرَّ بِهَا وَأَلْهَتْهُ عَنِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ ﴿فَأَصْبَحَ يُقَلِّبُ كَفَّيْهِ عَلَى مَا أَنْفَقَ فِيهَا﴾ وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: يُصفّق كَفَّيْهِ مُتَأَسِّفًا مُتَلَهِّفًا عَلَى الْأَمْوَالِ الَّتِي أَذْهَبَهَا عَلَيْهِ ﴿وَيَقُولُ يَا لَيْتَنِي لَمْ أُشْرِكْ بِرَبِّي أَحَدًا وَلَمْ تَكُنْ لَهُ فِئَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَشِيرَةٌ أَوْ وَلَدٌ، كَمَا افْتَخَرَ بِهِمْ وَاسْتَعَزَّ ﴿يَنْصُرُونَهُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَمَا كَانَ مُنْتَصِرًا هُنَالِكَ الْوَلايَةُ لِلَّهِ الْحَقِّ﴾ اخْتَلَفَ الْقُرَّاءُ هَاهُنَا، فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقِفُ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ مُنْتَصِرًا هُنَالِكَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي ذَلِكَ الْمَوْطِنِ الَّذِي حَلَّ بِهِ عَذَابُ اللَّهِ، فَلَا مُنْقِذَ مِنْهُ. وَيَبْتَدِئُ [بِقَوْلِهِ] ﴿الْوَلايَةُ لِلَّهِ الْحَقِّ﴾ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقِفُ عَلَى: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ مُنْتَصِرًا﴾ وَيَبْتَدِئُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿هُنَالِكَ الْوَلايَةُ لِلَّهِ الْحَقِّ﴾ .

ثُمَّ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي قِرَاءَةِ ﴿الْوَلايَةُ﴾ فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَتَحَ الْوَاوَ، فَيَكُونُ الْمَعْنَى: هُنَالِكَ الْمُوَالَاةُ لِلَّهِ، أَيْ: هُنَالِكَ كُلُّ أَحَدٍ مِنْ مُؤْمِنٍ أَوْ كَافِرٍ يَرْجِعُ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَإِلَى مُوَالَاتِهِ وَالْخُضُوعِ لَهُ إِذَا وَقَعَ الْعَذَابُ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَلَمَّا رَأَوْا بَأْسَنَا قَالُوا آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ وَكَفَرْنَا بِمَا كُنَّا بِهِ مُشْرِكِينَ﴾ [غَافِرَ:٨٤] وَكَقَوْلِهِ إِخْبَارًا عَنْ فِرْعَوْنَ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا أَدْرَكَهُ الْغَرَقُ قَالَ آمَنْتُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا الَّذِي آمَنَتْ بِهِ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ وَأَنَا مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ آلآنَ وَقَدْ عَصَيْتَ قَبْلُ وَكُنْتَ مِنَ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ [يُونُسَ:٩١، ٩٠]

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ كَسَرَ الْوَاوَ مِنْ ﴿الْوَلايَةُ﴾ أَيْ: هُنَالِكَ الْحُكْمُ لِلَّهِ الْحَقِّ.

ثُمَّ مِنْهُمْ مَنْ رَفَعَ ﴿الْحَقِّ﴾ عَلَى أَنَّهُ نَعْتٌ لِلْوَلَايَةِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿الْمُلْكُ يَوْمَئِذٍ الْحَقُّ لِلرَّحْمَنِ وَكَانَ يَوْمًا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ عَسِيرًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٢٦]
