His saying {But when they reached the junction between them, they forgot their fish} is because Musa had been commanded to carry a salted fish with him, and he had been told: wherever you lose the fish, that is the place. So they travelled until they reached the junction of the two seas. There was a spring there called "the spring of life." They slept there, and some of the spray of that water touched the fish, so it stirred. It had been in a basket with Yushu' (peace be upon him), and it leapt from the basket into the sea. Yushu' (peace be upon him) awoke, and the fish had fallen into the sea and began to swim through it, with the water forming around it like an archway that did not close up behind it. This is why He said: {so it took its way into the sea, as a tunnel}, meaning like a tunnel in the earth.

Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said: its trace became as if it were stone.

Al-'Awfi related from Ibn Abbas: the fish did not touch anything of the sea without it drying up until it became rock.

Muhammad bin Ishaq related, from al-Zuhri, from Ubaydullah bin Abdullah, from Ibn Abbas, from Ubayy bin Ka'b, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, when he mentioned the account of this: "No water has ever parted since mankind existed except that one, the place of the fish stayed fixed within it, and it parted like a window, until Musa returned to it and saw its passage." So he said: {That is what we were seeking}.

Qatadah said: it was a tunnel from the land until it reached the sea, then it travelled through it, and it did not travel any path in it without that path becoming solidified water.

His saying {But when they had passed beyond} means: the place where they had forgotten the fish. The forgetting is attributed to both of them even though it was Yushu' who forgot it, just as in His statement {From them both come forth pearl and coral} [al-Rahman: 22], when in fact, according to one of the two opinions, they come forth only from the salty one.

When they had gone a stage's distance beyond the place where they had forgotten it, {Musa said} to his young companion, {Bring us our morning meal, indeed we have encountered exhaustion from this journey of ours}, meaning: from the distance they had travelled past that place, {exhaustion}, meaning fatigue. He said: {Do you recall when we took shelter at the rock? I indeed forgot the fish, and nothing made me forget it except Satan, that I should remember it}. Qatadah said: Ibn Mas'ud read it: "and nothing made me forget it, that I should remember it, except Satan." This is why He said {and it took its way} meaning its path {into the sea in a wondrous manner. He said: that is what we were seeking}, meaning: this is what we sought. {So they turned back}, meaning: they returned, {upon their tracks}, meaning: their path, {retracing}, meaning: they retraced the trail of their walking and followed their own footsteps back.

{Then they found a servant among Our servants, to whom We had given mercy from Us, and whom We had taught knowledge from Our presence}. This is al-Khidr (peace be upon him), as indicated by the authentic hadiths from the Messenger of God ﷺ. Al-Bukhari said regarding this:

[chain] Al-Humaydi told us, Sufyan told us, Amr bin Dinar told us, Sa'id bin Jubayr informed me, saying: I said to Ibn Abbas: Nawf al-Bikali claims that the Musa who was the companion of al-Khidr is not the Musa of the Children of Israel. Ibn Abbas said: the enemy of God has lied. Ubayy bin Ka'b, may God be pleased with him, told us that he heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "Musa stood up to give a sermon among the Children of Israel and was asked: who among people is most knowledgeable? He said: I am. So God reproached him for not attributing knowledge back to Him, and God revealed to him: I have a servant at the junction of the two seas who is more knowledgeable than you. Musa said: O Lord, how can I reach him? He said: take a fish with you, put it in a basket, and wherever you lose the fish, that is the place. So he took a fish and put it in a basket, then set out, and his young companion Yushu' bin Nun (peace be upon them both) went with him, until when they came to the rock, they laid their heads down and slept. The fish stirred in the basket and came out of it, and fell into the sea, and took its way into the sea as a tunnel. God held back the flow of water from the fish, so it became like an archway over it. When he awoke, his companion forgot to tell him about the fish, so they went on for the rest of that day and night, until the next morning Musa said to his young companion: {Bring us our morning meal, indeed we have encountered exhaustion from this journey of ours}. Musa did not feel fatigue until they had passed beyond the place which God had commanded him to. His young companion said to him: {Do you recall when we took shelter at the rock? I indeed forgot the fish, and nothing made me forget it except Satan, that I should remember it, and it took its way into the sea in a wondrous manner}." He said: "So it was a tunnel for the fish, and a wonder for Musa and his young companion." He said: {That is what we were seeking. So they turned back upon their tracks, retracing}." He said: "So they went back, retracing their trail, until they reached the rock, and there was a man wrapped in a garment. Musa greeted him with salam, and al-Khidr said: how is there salam in your land? He said: I am Musa. He said: the Musa of the Children of Israel? He said: yes, I have come to you so that you may teach me some of the right guidance you have been taught. {He said: indeed you will not be able to have patience with me}. O Musa, I have knowledge from God's knowledge that He has taught me, which you do not know, and you have knowledge from God's knowledge that God has taught you, which I do not know. Musa said: {You will find me, if God wills, patient, and I will not disobey you in any matter}. Al-Khidr said to him: {If you follow me, then do not ask me about anything until I myself mention it to you}.

So they set off walking along the shore of the sea. A ship passed by and they spoke to its people to carry them. They recognized al-Khidr, so they carried them without charge. When they had boarded the ship, suddenly al-Khidr had pulled out a plank from the ship's planks with an adze. Musa said to him: they carried us without charge, yet you have gone and made a hole in their ship in order to drown its people? You have indeed done a monstrous thing. {He said: did I not say that you would not be able to have patience with me? He said: do not take me to task for what I forgot, and do not press me hard with difficulty in my affair}." He said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "the first was from Musa forgetfulness." He said: then a sparrow came and landed on the edge of the ship and pecked at the sea once, or twice, and al-Khidr said to him: my knowledge and your knowledge, compared to God's knowledge, are only like what this sparrow has diminished from this sea.

Then they left the ship, and while they were walking along the shore, al-Khidr saw a boy playing with other boys, and al-Khidr took hold of his head with his hand and pulled it off, killing him. Musa said to him: {Have you killed an innocent soul who has killed no one? You have indeed done a horrible thing! He said: did I not tell you that you would not be able to have patience with me?} He said: "and this was more severe than the first." {He said: if I ask you about anything after this, do not keep me as a companion. You have indeed reached the limit of excuse from me. So they went on until, when they came to the people of a town, they asked its people for food, but they refused to host them. Then they found in it a wall about to collapse}, he said: leaning. Then al-Khidr set it upright with his hand, {so he set it up straight}. Musa said: these are people we came to, and they did not feed us or host us, {had you wished, you could have taken a wage for it. He said: this is the parting between me and you. I will inform you of the interpretation of that which you could not have patience with}." The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "We wished that Musa had been patient so that God might have related to us more of their story."

Sa'id bin Jubayr said: Ibn Abbas used to read it: "and ahead of them was a king who seized every good ship by force," and he used to read: "as for the boy, he was an unbeliever, and his parents were believers."

Then al-Bukhari related it from Qutaybah, from Sufyan bin Uyaynah...

He mentioned something similar, and in it: "So Musa went out, and with him his young companion Yusha' ibn Nun, and with them both was the fish, until they reached the rock, and they stopped there. He said: Musa laid down his head and slept." Sufyan said: "And in the hadith of someone other than 'Amr, he said: At the base of the rock there was a spring called al-Hayat (Life), no water of it touched anything except that it came to life. So some of the water of that spring touched the fish." He said, "It stirred and slipped out of the basket, and entered the sea. When Musa awoke, he said to his young companion: {Bring us our morning meal}." He said it thus, and continued the hadith. A sparrow landed on the edge of the ship and dipped its beak into the sea, and al-Khidr said to Musa: "My knowledge and your knowledge and the knowledge of all creation, compared to the knowledge of Allah, is only like the amount that this sparrow has dipped its beak from the sea." He mentioned the rest similarly.

Al-Bukhari also said: Ibrahim ibn Musa told us, Hisham ibn Yusuf told us, that Ibn Jurayj informed them, saying: Ya'la ibn Muslim and 'Amr ibn Dinar informed me, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, one of them adding more than the other, and others besides them whom I have heard narrating from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: We were with Ibn 'Abbas in his house when he said, "Ask me." I said, "O Abu al-'Abbas, may Allah make me a ransom for you, there is a man in Kufa, a storyteller, called Nawf, who claims that he is not the Musa of the Children of Israel." As for 'Amr, he said to me that Ibn 'Abbas said: "The enemy of Allah has lied!" As for Ya'la, he said to me that Ibn 'Abbas said: "Ubayy ibn Ka'b told me, saying: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: 'Musa, the Messenger of Allah, was reminding the people one day, until when eyes overflowed with tears and hearts softened, he turned away. A man caught up with him and said: O Messenger of Allah, is there anyone on earth more knowledgeable than you? He said: No. So Allah reproached him for not attributing the knowledge to Allah. It was said (to him): Yes indeed (there is). He said: O my Lord, and where? He said: At the junction of the two seas. He said: O my Lord, grant me a sign by which I will know that.'" 'Amr said to me: He said, "Where the fish parts from you." And Ya'la said to me: "Take a dead fish; the place where life is breathed into it (is the place)." So he took a fish and put it in a basket, and said to his young companion: "I ask nothing of you except that you tell me where the fish leaves you." He said, "You have not asked a great thing." That is the meaning of His saying: {And when Musa said to his young companion} Yusha' ibn Nun, this is not from Sa'id ibn Jubayr's account. He said: "While he was in the shade of a rock in a moist place, the fish thrashed about, and Musa was asleep, and his young companion said, I will not wake him, until when he awoke he forgot to tell him. The fish thrashed until it entered the sea, and Allah held back the flow of water from it until its trace was like in a rock." [He said: 'Amr said to me: like this, as if its trace was in stone], and he made a circle with his thumb and the finger next to it. {Indeed, we have suffered much fatigue in this, our journey}. He said, "Allah had already removed fatigue from you." This is not from Sa'id's account, he was told, and they went back and found Khidr. He said: 'Uthman ibn Abi Sulayman said: "Upon a green cushion in the middle of the sea." Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: "Covered with a garment, having placed one end of it under his feet and the other end under his head." Musa greeted him with peace, and he uncovered his face and said: "Is there peace in this land? Who are you?" He said, "I am Musa." He said, "The Musa of the Children of Israel?" He said, "Yes." He said, "What is your purpose?" He said, "I have come to you so that you may teach me of what you have been taught, guidance." He said, "The Torah in your hand should be enough for you, and the revelation that comes to you! O Musa, I have knowledge that it is not fitting for you to know, and you have knowledge that it is not fitting for me to know." Then a bird took with its beak from the sea [and he said: By Allah, my knowledge and your knowledge compared to the knowledge of Allah is nothing but like what this bird has taken with its beak from the sea]. Until when they boarded the ship, they found small ferries carrying the people of this shore to the other shore, and they recognized him, and said, "The righteous servant of Allah?" He (the narrator) said: We said to Sa'id, "Khidr?" He said, "Yes. We will not carry him for a fare." So he made a hole in it, and drove in a peg. Musa said: {Have you made a hole in it to drown its people? You have certainly done a grave thing}.

Mujahid said: (meaning) as a denunciation. He said: {Did I not say that you would never be able to have patience with me?} The first (objection) was out of forgetfulness, the middle one was a stipulated condition, and the third was deliberate. {He said: Do not seize me for what I forgot, and do not overburden me with difficulty in my affair. So they set out} until they met a boy and he killed him. Ya'la said that Sa'id said: He found boys playing, and he took hold of a clever disbelieving boy, laid him down, then slaughtered him with a knife. Musa said: {Have you killed a pure soul} that had not committed any sin. Ibn 'Abbas read it as "zakiyyah" (pure), meaning submissive (Muslim), just as you would say "a pure boy". So they set out, and they found a wall about to collapse, and he set it upright. [Sa'id] said with his hand like this, and he raised his hand and it stood straight. Ya'la said: I think Sa'id said, "He wiped it with his hand and it became upright." He said: {If you had wished, you could have taken payment for it}. Sa'id said: payment which we could eat. {And there was behind them a king}, that is, ahead of them. Ibn 'Abbas read it as "ahead of them was a king." They claim, on authority other than Sa'id, that he was Hudad ibn Budad, and that the killed boy's name was, they claim, Jaysur. {A king who seizes every ship by force}. So I intended, when it passed by him, that it be left with its defect, so that when it had passed him they would repair it and benefit from it. Some say: they sealed it with a bottle. Others say: with tar. {And his parents were believers}, while he was a disbeliever. {So we feared that he would overburden them with transgression and disbelief}, meaning that his love would carry them to follow him in his religion. {So we intended that their Lord should substitute for them one better than him in purity}, as in His saying {Have you killed a pure soul}. {And nearer in mercy}: the two of them would be more merciful toward this one than they had been toward the first one whom Khidr killed. Someone other than Sa'id ibn Jubayr claimed that they were given a girl in exchange. As for Dawud ibn Abi 'Asim, he said, on the authority of more than one person, that it was a girl.

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from Abu Ishaq, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: Musa (peace be upon him) addressed the Children of Israel and said, "No one is more knowledgeable of Allah and His affair than I am." So he was commanded to meet this man. He then mentioned something similar to what preceded, with some additions and omissions, and Allah knows best.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from al-Hasan ibn 'Umara, from al-Hakam ibn 'Utaybah, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: I sat with Ibn 'Abbas, and with him were a group of the People of the Book, and one of them said, "O Abu al-'Abbas, Nawf, the son of Ka'b's wife, claims on the authority of Ka'b that the Musa the prophet who sought the knowledgeable one was actually Musa ibn Misha." Sa'id said: Ibn 'Abbas said, "Does Nawf say this?" Sa'id said: I said to him, "Yes, I heard Nawf say that." He said, "You heard him yourself, O Sa'id?" He said: I said, "Yes." He said, "Nawf has lied." Then Ibn 'Abbas said: "Ubayy ibn Ka'b told me, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: that Musa of the Children of Israel asked his Lord, saying: O my Lord, if among Your servants there is one more knowledgeable than I, then show him to me. He said to him: Yes, among My servants there is one more knowledgeable than you. Then He described his place to him and gave him permission to meet him. So Musa set out, and with him his young companion, and with him a salted fish. It had been said to him: When this fish comes back to life in a certain place, then your companion is there, and you have attained your goal. So Musa set out, and with him his young companion, and with him that fish, the two of them carrying it. He traveled until the journey wearied him, and he reached the rock and that water, and that water was the water of life: whoever drinks from it lives forever, and nothing dead comes near it except that it comes back to life. When they stopped there and the fish touched the water, it came to life, {and it took its way into the sea, slipping away}. They went on, and when he had passed beyond the place where it had turned back, Musa said to his young companion: {Bring us our morning meal, indeed we have suffered much fatigue in this, our journey}." The young man said, and he mentioned: {Do you recall when we took shelter at the rock? Indeed I forgot the fish, and none but Satan made me forget to mention it. It took its way into the sea in a wondrous manner}. Ibn 'Abbas said: Musa then went on top of the rock, and when they reached it, there was a man wrapped in a cloak of his. Musa greeted him with peace, and the knowledgeable one returned the greeting, then said to him, "What has brought you here, when surely you have work to do among your people?" Musa said to him, "I have come to you so that you may teach me of what you have been taught, guidance." {He said: Indeed, you will not be able to have patience with me}, for he was a man who knew the knowledge of the unseen, having been taught that. Musa said, "Yes indeed (I will be patient)." He said: {And how could you have patience for that of which you have no comprehensive knowledge?} That is: you only know the outward aspect of what you see of justice, and you have no comprehensive knowledge of what I know of the unseen. {He said: You will find me, if Allah wills, patient, and I will not disobey you in any matter}.

And if I see something that contradicts me, he said: {But if you follow me, then do not ask me about anything} [and if you deny it/reject it] {until I make mention of it to you}: so the two of them set off walking along the seashore, offering themselves to the people, seeking someone who would carry them, until a new, sturdy ship passed by them, no ship better, more complete, or sturdier than it had passed by them. They asked its people to carry them, and they carried them. When they had settled in it and it had gone out into the deep sea with its people, he took out an adze and a mallet, then went to a section of it and struck it with the adze until he had made a hole in it. Then he took a plank and fitted it over the hole, then sat upon it patching it. Musa said to him, having seen a matter that appalled him: {"Have you made a hole in it to drown its people? You have certainly done a grave thing." He said, "Did I not say that you would never be able to have patience with me?" He said, "Do not take me to task for what I forgot"}, meaning: for what I neglected of your covenant, {"and do not burden me with difficulty in my affair."}

Then the two of them left the ship and went on, until they came to the people of a town, and there were boys playing behind it, among them a boy who was more charming, more well-off, and more handsome than any of the other boys. He took him by the hand, and took a stone and struck his head with it until he crushed his skull and killed him. He said: Musa saw a grave matter that could not be borne, a small child killed with no sin of his own, so he said: {"Have you killed a pure soul}, meaning a young one, {who had killed no one? You have certainly done a horrible thing." He said, "Did I not tell you that you would never be able to have patience with me?" He said, "If I ask you about anything after this, then do not keep me as a companion. You have certainly reached an excuse from me"}, meaning: you have now excused yourself regarding my conduct.

{So they set off until, when they came to the people of a town, they asked its people for food, but they refused to host them. Then they found in it a wall about to collapse}, and he tore it down, then sat rebuilding it. Musa grew weary at what he saw him doing of this burdensome task, something for which he had no patience, and he said: {"If you had wished, you could have taken a payment for it,"} meaning: we asked them for food and they did not feed us, we sought their hospitality and they did not host us, yet you sat working without any favor owed to them, and if you had wished, you could have been given a wage for your work?

He said: {"This is the parting between me and you. I will inform you of the interpretation of that which you could not have patience with. As for the ship, it belonged to poor men who worked upon the sea, and I wished to cause a defect in it, for behind them was a king who seized every ship by force"} (and in the reading of Ubayy ibn Ka'b: "every sound ship") "I only put a defect in it so that I might turn him away from it, and it was preserved when he saw the defect I had made in it. {As for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared that he would burden them with rebellion and disbelief, so we wished that their Lord should replace him for them with one better than him in purity and closer in mercy. And as for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the town, and beneath it was a treasure belonging to them, and their father had been righteous, so your Lord wished that they should reach their maturity and extract their treasure, as a mercy from your Lord. And I did not do it of my own accord"}, meaning: I did not do it of my own initiative, {"That is the interpretation of that which you could not have patience with."} Ibn 'Abbas used to say: the treasure was nothing other than knowledge.

Al-'Awfi reported, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: when Musa and his people prevailed over Egypt, he settled his people there, and when their dwelling had become established, Allah revealed to him that he should remind them of the days of Allah. So he addressed his people, and mentioned to them the good and the blessing Allah had given them, and reminded them of how Allah had saved them from the House of Pharaoh, and reminded them of the destruction of their enemy, and of how Allah had made them successors in the land. And he said: Allah spoke to your prophet directly, and He chose me for Himself, and sent down upon me a love from Him, and Allah has given you everything you asked for; so your prophet is the most excellent of the people of the earth, and you read the Torah. He did not leave out any blessing Allah had bestowed upon them without making it known to them. Then a man from the Children of Israel said to him: they are indeed as you say, O Prophet of Allah, we know what you say, but is there on earth anyone more knowledgeable than you, O Prophet of Allah? He said: No. So Allah sent Jibril to Musa, peace be upon both of them, and he said: Allah, Mighty and Majestic, says: and how do you know where I place My knowledge? Indeed. There is on the shore of the sea a man who is more knowledgeable than you, Ibn 'Abbas said: he is al-Khidr, so Musa asked his Lord to show him to him, and He revealed to him: go to the sea, for you will find on the shore of the sea a fish; take it and give it to your servant, then stay by the shore of the sea, and when you forget the fish and it disappears from you, there you will find the righteous servant whom you seek.

When the journey of Musa, the Prophet of Allah, grew long and he grew weary in it, he asked his servant about the fish, and his servant, who was his young companion, said to him: {"Do you recall when we took shelter at the rock? Indeed, I forgot the fish, and none made me forget to mention it to you except Satan."} The young man said: I saw the fish when it took its way into the sea as a passage, and this astonished Musa, so he went back until he came to the rock, and found the fish, and the fish went on moving through the sea and Musa followed it, and Musa held his staff before him, parting the water with it, following the fish, and the fish did not touch anything of the sea without it drying up, until it became like rock. The Prophet of Allah was amazed at this, until the fish brought him to an island among the islands of the sea, and there he met al-Khidr and greeted him with peace. Al-Khidr said: and upon you be peace, but how can there be peace in this land? And who are you? He said: I am Musa. Al-Khidr said: the companion of the Children of Israel? [He said: Yes] So he welcomed him and said: what has brought you? He said, I have come to you {"so that you might teach me from what you have been taught, right guidance." He said, "Indeed, you will never be able to have patience with me,"} meaning: you will not be able to bear that. Musa said: {"You will find me, if Allah wills, patient, and I will not disobey you in any matter."} He said: so he set off with him, and said to him: do not ask me about anything I do until I explain its matter to you, and that is his statement: {until I make mention of it to you.}

Al-Zuhri reported, from 'Ubaydullah ibn 'Abdullah ibn 'Utba ibn Mas'ud, from Ibn 'Abbas: that he disputed, he and al-Hurr ibn Qays ibn Hisn al-Fazari, about the companion of Musa, and Ibn 'Abbas said: he is al-Khidr. Then Ubayy ibn Ka'b passed by them, and Ibn 'Abbas called him and said: I have disputed with this companion of mine about the companion of Musa who asked for the way to meet him, so have you heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ mention his matter? He said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "While Musa was among a gathering of the Children of Israel, a man came to him and said: do you know the whereabouts of a man more knowledgeable than you? He said: No; so Allah revealed to Musa: indeed, Our servant al-Khidr. So Musa asked for the way to meet him, and Allah made the fish a sign for him, and it was said to him: when you lose the fish [for it will be there], go back, for you will meet him. So Musa was following the trail of the fish in the sea. His young companion said to him: {"Do you recall when we took shelter at the rock? Indeed, I forgot the fish."} Musa said: {"That is what we were seeking. So they returned, retracing their footsteps."} And they found Our servant al-Khidr, and what happened between the two of them was as narrated in the Book of Allah.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

سَبَبُ قَوْلِ مُوسَى [عليه السلام] لفتاه -وهو يُشوع بْنُ نُون-هَذَا الْكَلَامَ: أَنَّهُ ذَكَرَ لَهُ أَنَّ عَبْدًا مِنْ عِبَادِ اللَّهِ بِمَجْمَعِ الْبَحْرَيْنِ، عِنْدَهُ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ مَا لَمْ يُحِطْ بِهِ مُوسَى، فَأَحَبَّ الذَّهَابَ إِلَيْهِ، وَقَالَ لِفَتَاهُ ذَلِكَ: ﴿لَا أَبْرَحُ حَتَّى أَبْلُغَ مَجْمَعَ الْبَحْرَيْنِ﴾ أَيْ لَا أَزَالُ سَائِرًا حَتَّى أَبْلُغَ هَذَا الْمَكَانَ الذي فيه مجمع البحرين، قال الفرزدق: فَمَا بَرحُوا حَتَّى تَهَادَتْ نسَاؤهُم ... بِبَطْحَاء ذِي قَارٍ عيابَ اللطَائم 

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: وَهُمَا بَحْرُ فَارِسَ مِمَّا يَلِي الْمَشْرِقَ، وَبَحْرُ الرُّومِ مِمَّا يَلِي الْمَغْرِبَ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرظي: مَجْمَعُ الْبَحْرَيْنِ عِنْدَ طَنْجَةَ، يَعْنِي فِي أَقْصَى بِلَادِ الْمَغْرِبِ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوْ أَمْضِيَ حُقُبًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَوْ أَنِّي أَسِيرُ حُقُبًا مِنَ الزَّمَانِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: ذَكَرَ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ بِكَلَامِ الْعَرَبِ أَنَّ الحُقُب فِي لُغَةِ قَيْسٍ : سَنَةٌ. ثُمَّ قَدْ رُوِيَ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو أَنَّهُ قَالَ: الحُقُب ثَمَانُونَ سَنَةً. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: سَبْعُونَ خَرِيفًا. وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوْ أَمْضِيَ حُقُبًا﴾ قَالَ: دَهْرًا. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ، مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلَمَّا بَلَغَا مَجْمَعَ بَيْنِهِمَا نَسِيَا حُوتَهُمَا﴾ ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ قَدْ أُمِرَ بِحَمْلِ حُوتٍ مَمْلُوحٍ مَعَهُ، وَقِيلَ لَهُ: مَتَى فقدتَ الْحُوتَ فَهُوَ ثَمّة. فَسَارَا حَتَّى بَلَغَا مَجْمَعَ الْبَحْرَيْنِ؛ وَهُنَاكَ عَيْنٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا: "عَيْنُ الْحَيَاةِ"، فَنَامَا هُنَالِكَ، وَأَصَابَ الْحُوتُ مِنْ رَشَاشِ ذَلِكَ الْمَاءِ فَاضْطَرَبَ ، وَكَانَ فِي مِكْتَلٍ مَعَ يُوشَعَ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] ، وطَفَر مِنَ المَكْتل إِلَى الْبَحْرِ، فَاسْتَيْقَظَ يُوشع، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَسَقَطَ الْحُوتُ فِي الْبَحْرِ وَجَعَلَ يَسِيرُ فِيهِ، وَالْمَاءُ لَهُ مِثْلُ الطَّاقِ لَا يَلْتَئِمُ بَعْدَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ سَرَبًا﴾ أَيْ: مِثْلَ السَرَب في الأرض.

قال ابن جريح : قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: صَارَ أَثَرُهُ كَأَنَّهُ حَجَر.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: جَعَلَ الْحُوتُ لَا يَمَسُّ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْبَحْرِ إِلَّا يَبِسَ حتى يكون صخرة .

وقال محمد -[هو] بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ-عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُبيد اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَاسٍ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حِينَ ذَكَرَ حَدِيثَ ذَلِكَ: "مَا انْجَابَ مَاءٌ مُنْذُ كَانَ النَّاسُ غَيْرُهُ ثَبَتَ مَكَانَ الْحُوتِ الَّذِي فِيهِ، فَانْجَابَ كالكُوّة حَتَّى رَجَعَ إِلَيْهِ مُوسَى فَرَأَى مَسْلَكَهُ"، فَقَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ مَا كُنَّا نَبْغِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: سَرب مِنَ الْبَرِّ ، حَتَّى أَفْضَى إِلَى الْبَحْرِ، ثُمَّ سَلَكَ فِيهِ فَجَعَلَ لَا يَسْلُكُ فِيهِ طَرِيقًا إِلَّا جُعِلَ مَاءً جَامِدًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلَمَّا جَاوَزَا﴾ أَيِ: الْمَكَانَ الَّذِي نَسِيَا الْحُوتَ فِيهِ، ونُسب النسيان إليهما وإن كان يُوشَع هُوَ الَّذِي نَسِيَهُ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَخْرُجُ مِنْهُمَا اللُّؤْلُؤُ وَالْمَرْجَانُ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٢٢] ، وَإِنَّمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنَ الْمَالِحِ فِي أَحَدِ الْقَوْلَيْنِ.

فَلَمَّا ذَهَبَا عَنِ الْمَكَانِ الَّذِي نَسَيَاهُ فِيهِ مَرْحَلَةً ﴿قَالَ﴾ مُوسَى ﴿لِفَتَاهُ آتِنَا غَدَاءَنَا لَقَدْ لَقِينَا مِنْ سَفَرِنَا هَذَا نَصَبًا [نَصَبًا] ﴾ أَيْ: الَّذِي جَاوَزَا فِيهِ الْمَكَانَ ﴿نَصَبًا﴾ يَعْنِي: تَعَبًا. قَالَ: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ أَوَيْنَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ فَإِنِّي نَسِيتُ الْحُوتَ وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهُ إِلا الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَقَرَأَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: ["وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهِ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ إِلَّا الشَّيْطَانُ] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ﴾ أَيْ: طَرِيقَهُ ﴿فِي الْبَحْرِ عَجَبًا قَالَ ذَلِكَ مَا كُنَّا نَبْغِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا الَّذِي نَطْلُبُ ﴿فَارْتَدَّا﴾ أَيْ: رَجَعَا ﴿عَلَى آثَارِهِمَا﴾ أَيْ: طَرِيقِهِمَا ﴿قَصَصًا﴾ أَيْ: يَقُصَّانِ أَثَرَ مَشْيِهِمَا، وَيَقْفُوَانِ أَثَرَهُمَا.

﴿فَوَجَدَا عَبْدًا مِنْ عِبَادِنَا آتَيْنَاهُ رَحْمَةً مِنْ عِنْدِنَا وَعَلَّمْنَاهُ مِنْ لَدُنَّا عِلْمًا﴾ وَهَذَا هُوَ الْخَضِرُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَمَا دَلَّتْ عَلَيْهِ الْأَحَادِيثُ الصَّحِيحَةُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. بِذَلِكَ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا الْحُمَيْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: قُلْتُ لِابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّ نَوْفًا البِكَالِيّ يَزْعُمُ أَنَّ مُوسَى صَاحِبَ الْخَضِرِ لَيْسَ هُوَ مُوسَى صَاحِبَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَذِبَ عَدُوّ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ مُوسَى قَامَ خَطِيبًا فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ فَسُئل: أَيُّ النَّاسِ أَعْلَمُ؟ قَالَ: أَنَا. فَعَتَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ إِذْ لَمْ يَرُدّ الْعِلْمَ إِلَيْهِ، فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ: إِنَّ لِي عَبْدًا بِمَجْمَعِ الْبَحْرَيْنِ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ. فَقَالَ مُوسَى: يَا رَبِّ، وَكَيْفَ لِي بِهِ؟ قَالَ: تَأْخُذُ مَعَكَ حُوتًا، تَجْعَلُهُ بِمِكْتَلٍ، فَحَيْثُمَا فَقَدْتَ الْحُوتَ فَهُوَ ثَمَّ. فَأَخَذَ حُوتًا، فَجَعَلَهُ بِمِكْتَلٍ ثُمَّ انْطَلَقَ وَانْطَلَقَ مَعَهُ بِفَتَاهُ يُوشع بْنِ نُونٍ عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، حَتَّى إِذَا أتيا الصخرة وضعا رؤوسهما فَنَامَا، وَاضْطَرَبَ الْحُوتُ فِي الْمِكْتَلِ، فَخَرَجَ مِنْهُ، فَسَقَطَ فِي الْبَحْرِ وَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ سَرَبًا، وَأَمْسَكَ اللَّهُ عَنِ الْحُوتِ جِريةَ الْمَاءِ، فَصَارَ عَلَيْهِ مِثْلَ الطَّاقِ. فَلَمَّا اسْتَيْقَظَ نَسِيَ صَاحِبُهُ أَنْ يُخْبِرَهُ بِالْحُوتِ، فَانْطَلَقَا بَقِيَّةَ يَوْمِهِمَا وَلَيْلَتِهِمَا، حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ مِنَ الْغَدِ قَالَ مُوسَى لِفَتَاهُ: ﴿آتِنَا غَدَاءَنَا لَقَدْ لَقِينَا مِنْ سَفَرِنَا هَذَا نَصَبًا﴾ وَلَمْ يَجِدْ مُوسَى النَّصَب حَتَّى جاوَزَا الْمَكَانَ الَّذِي أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ. قَالَ لَهُ فَتَاهُ : ﴿أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ أَوَيْنَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ فَإِنِّي نَسِيتُ الْحُوتَ وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهُ إِلا الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ وَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ عَجَبًا﴾ قَالَ: "فَكَانَ لِلْحُوتِ سَرَبًا وَلِمُوسَى وَفَتَاهُ عَجَبًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ مَا كُنَّا نَبْغِ فَارْتَدَّا عَلَى آثَارِهِمَا قَصَصًا﴾ . قَالَ: "فَرَجَعَا يَقُصَّانِ أَثَرَهُمَا حَتَّى انْتَهَيَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ، فَإِذَا رَجُلٌ مُسجّى بِثَوْبٍ، فَسَلَّمَ عَلَيْهِ مُوسَى، فَقَالَ الخَضِر: وَأنّى بِأَرْضِكَ السَّلَامُ!. قَالَ: أَنَا مُوسَى. قَالَ: مُوسَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، أَتَيْتُكَ لِتُعَلِّمَنِي مِمَّا عُلِّمت رُشْدًا. ﴿قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ ، يَا مُوسَى إِنِّي عَلَى عِلْمٍ مَنْ عِلْمِ اللَّهِ عَلَّمَنِيهِ، لَا تَعْلَمُهُ أَنْتَ، وَأَنْتَ عَلَى عِلْمٍ مَنْ عِلْمِ اللَّهِ عَلَّمَكَه اللَّهُ لا أَعْلَمُهُ. فَقَالَ مُوسَى: ﴿سَتَجِدُنِي إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ صَابِرًا وَلا أَعْصِي لَكَ أَمْرًا﴾ قَالَ لَهُ الْخَضِرُ: ﴿فَإِنِ اتَّبَعْتَنِي فَلا تَسْأَلْنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ حَتَّى أُحْدِثَ لَكَ مِنْهُ ذِكْرًا﴾ .

فَانْطَلَقَا يَمْشِيَانِ عَلَى سَاحِلِ الْبَحْرِ، فَمَرَّتْ سَفِينَةٌ فَكَلَّمُوهُمْ أَنْ يَحْمِلُوهُ ، فَعَرَفُوا الْخَضِرَ، فَحَمَلُوهُمْ بِغَيْرِ نَوْلٍ، فَلَمَّا رَكِبَا فِي السَّفِينَةِ لَمْ يَفْجَأْ إِلَّا وَالْخَضِرُ قَدْ قَلَعَ لَوْحًا مِنْ أَلْوَاحِ السَّفِينَةِ بِالْقَدُومِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: قَدْ حَمَلُونَا بِغَيْرِ نَوْلٍ، فَعَمَدْتَ إِلَى سَفِينَتِهِمْ فَخَرَقْتَهَا لِتُغْرِقَ أَهْلَهَا؟ لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا إِمْرًا. ﴿قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا * قَالَ لَا تُؤَاخِذْنِي بِمَا نَسِيتُ وَلا تُرْهِقْنِي مِنْ أَمْرِي عُسْرًا﴾ قَالَ: وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كَانَتِ الْأُولَى مِنْ مُوسَى نِسْيَانًا". قَالَ: وَجَاءَ عُصْفُورٌ فَنَزَلَ عَلَى حَرْفِ السَّفِينَةِ فَنَقَرَ فِي الْبَحْرِ نَقْرة، [أَوْ نَقْرَتَيْنِ] فَقَالَ لَهُ الْخَضِرُ: مَا عِلْمِي وَعِلْمُكَ فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ إِلَّا مِثْلُ مَا نَقَصَ هَذَا الْعُصْفُورُ مِنْ هَذَا الْبَحْرِ.

ثُمَّ خَرَجَا مِنَ السَّفِينَةِ، فَبَيْنَمَا هُمَا يَمْشِيَانِ عَلَى السَّاحِلِ إِذْ أَبْصَرَ الْخَضِرُ غُلَامًا يَلْعَبُ مَعَ الْغِلْمَانِ، فَأَخَذَ الْخَضِرُ رَأْسَهُ [بِيَدِهِ] فَاقْتَلَعَهُ بِيَدِهِ فَقَتَلَهُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: ﴿أَقَتَلْتَ نَفْسًا زَكِيَّةً بِغَيْرِ نَفْسٍ لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا نُكْرًا * قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ لَكَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ ؟! قَالَ: "وَهَذِهِ أَشَدُّ مِنَ الْأُولَى"، ﴿قَالَ إِنْ سَأَلْتُكَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ بَعْدَهَا فَلا تُصَاحِبْنِي قَدْ بَلَغْتَ مِنْ لَدُنِّي عُذْرًا * فَانْطَلَقَا حَتَّى إِذَا أَتَيَا أَهْلَ قَرْيَةٍ اسْتَطْعَمَا أَهْلَهَا فَأَبَوْا أَنْ يُضَيِّفُوهُمَا فَوَجَدَا فِيهَا جِدَارًا يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَنْقَضَّ ﴾ قَالَ: مَائِلٌ. فَقَالَ الْخَضِرُ بِيَدِهِ: ﴿فَأَقَامَهُ﴾ ، فَقَالَ مُوسَى: قَوْمٌ أَتَيْنَاهُمْ فَلَمْ يُطْعِمُونَا وَلَمْ يُضَيِّفُونَا، ﴿لَوْ شِئْتَ لاتَّخَذْتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا قَالَ هَذَا فِرَاقُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنِكَ سَأُنَبِّئُكَ بِتَأْوِيلِ مَا لَمْ تَسْتَطِعْ عَلَيْهِ صَبْرًا﴾ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَدِدْنَا أَنَّ مُوسَى كَانَ صَبَرَ حَتَّى يَقُصَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْنَا مِنْ خَبَرِهِمَا".

قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: كَانَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقْرَأُ: "وَكَانَ أَمَامَهُمْ مَلِكٌ يَأْخُذُ كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ صَالِحَةٍ غَصْبًا" وَكَانَ يَقْرَأُ: "وَأَمَّا الْغُلَامُ فَكَانَ كَافِرًا وَكَانَ أَبَوَاهُ مُؤْمِنَيْنِ" .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ قُتَيْبَةَ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيينة ... فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ ، وَفِيهِ: "فَخَرَجَ مُوسَى وَمَعَهُ فَتَاهُ يُوشع بْنُ نُونٍ، وَمَعَهُمَا الْحُوتُ حَتَّى انْتَهَيَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ، فَنَزَلَا عِنْدَهَا -قَالَ: فَوَضَعَ مُوسَى رَأْسَهُ فَنَامَ-قَالَ سُفْيَانُ: وَفِي حَدِيثِ غَيْرِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: وَفِي أَصْلِ الصَّخْرَةِ عَيْنٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا: الْحَيَاةُ، لَا يُصِيبُ مِنْ مَائِهَا شَيْءٌ إِلَّا حُيِيَ: فَأَصَابَ الْحُوتَ مِنْ مَاءِ تِلْكَ الْعَيْنِ، قَالَ، فَتَحَرَّكَ وَانْسَلَّ مِنَ الْمِكْتَلِ، فَدَخَلَ الْبَحْرَ، فَلَمَّا اسْتَيْقَظَ قَالَ مُوسَى لِفَتَاهُ: ﴿آتِنَا غَدَاءَنَا﴾ كَذَا قَالَ: وَسَاقَ الْحَدِيثَ. وَوَقَعَ عُصْفُورٌ عَلَى حَرْفِ السَّفِينَةِ، فَغَمَسَ مِنْقَارَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ، فَقَالَ الْخَضِرُ لِمُوسَى: مَا علمي وَعِلْمُكَ وَعِلْمُ الْخَلَائِقِ فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ إِلَّا مقدارُ مَا غَمَسَ هَذَا الْعُصْفُورُ مِنْقَارَهُ وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَهُ بِنَحْوِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ يُوسُفَ، أَنَّ ابْنَ جُرَيج أَخْبَرَهُمْ قَالَ: أَخْبَرَنِي يَعْلَى بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ وَعَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ -يَزِيدُ أَحَدُهُمَا عَلَى صَاحِبِهِ-وَغَيْرُهُمَا قَدْ سَمِعْتُهُ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: إِنَّا لَعِنْدَ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي بَيْتِهِ، إِذْ قَالَ: سَلُونِي. فَقُلْتُ: أَيْ أَبَا عَبَّاسٍ، جَعَلَنِي اللَّهُ فِدَاكَ، بِالْكُوفَةِ رَجُلٌ قَاصٌّ، يُقَالُ لَهُ: "نَوْفٌ" يَزْعُمُ أَنَّهُ لَيْسَ بِمُوسَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ -أَمَّا عَمْرٌو فَقَالَ لِي: قَالَ : كَذِبَ عَدُوُّ اللَّهِ! وَأَمَّا يَعْلَى فَقَالَ لِي: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: حَدَّثَنِي أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مُوسَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، ذكَّر النَّاسَ يَوْمًا، حَتَّى إِذَا فَاضَتِ الْعُيُونُ، وَرَقَّتِ الْقُلُوبُ، وَلَّى فَأَدْرَكَهُ رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: أَيْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ فِي الْأَرْضِ أَحَدٌ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ؟ قَالَ: لَا. فَعَتَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ إِذْ لَمْ يَرُدَّ الْعِلْمَ إِلَى اللَّهِ، قِيلَ: بَلَى قَالَ: أَيْ رَبِّ، وَأَيْنَ؟ قَالَ: بِمَجْمَعِ الْبَحْرَيْنِ. قَالَ: أَيْ رَبِّ، اجْعَلْ لِي عِلْمًا أَعْلَمُ ذَلِكَ بِهِ". قَالَ لِي عَمْرٌو: قَالَ: حَيْثُ يُفَارِقُكَ الْحُوتُ، وَقَالَ لِي يَعْلَى: خُذْ حُوتًا مَيْتًا حَيْثُ يُنْفَخُ فِيهِ الرُّوحُ. فَأَخَذَ حُوتًا فَجَعَلَهُ فِي مِكْتَلٍ، فَقَالَ لِفَتَاهُ: لَا أُكَلِّفُكَ إِلَّا أَنْ تُخْبِرَنِي حَيْثُ يُفَارِقُكَ الْحُوتُ، قَالَ مَا كَلَّفْتَ كَبِيرًا. فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالَ مُوسَى لِفَتَاهُ﴾ يُوشَعَ بْنِ نُونٍ، لَيْسَتْ عِنْدَ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، قَالَ: "فَبَيْنَا هُوَ فِي ظِلِّ صَخْرَةٍ فِي مَكَانٍ ثَرْيَانَ إِذْ تَضَرَّب الْحُوتُ وَمُوسَى نَائِمٌ فَقَالَ فَتَاهُ: لَا أُوقِظُهُ، حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْقَظَ نَسِيَ أَنْ يُخْبِرَهُ، وَتَضَرَّبَ الْحُوتُ حَتَّى دَخَلَ الْبَحْرَ، فَأَمْسَكَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ جَرْيَة الْمَاءِ حَتَّى كَأَنَّ أَثَرَهُ فِي حَجَرٍ". [قَالَ: فَقَالَ لِي عَمْرٌو: هَكَذَا كَأَنَّ أَثَرَهُ فِي حَجَرٍ] ، وَحَلَّقَ بَيْنَ إِبْهَامَيْهِ وَالَّتِي تَلِيهِمَا: ﴿لَقَدْ لَقِينَا مِنْ سَفَرِنَا هَذَا نَصَبًا﴾ قَالَ: "وَقَدْ قَطَعَ اللَّهُ عَنْكَ النَّصَبَ" لَيْسَتْ هَذِهِ عِنْدَ سَعِيدٍ -أَخْبَرَهُ، فَرَجَعَا فَوَجَدَا خَضرًا. قَالَ: قَالَ عُثْمَانُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ: عَلَى طِنْفِسَة خَضْرَاءَ عَلَى كبِد الْبَحْرِ. قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: مُسَجى بِثَوْبٍ، قَدْ جَعَلَ طَرَفَهُ تَحْتَ رِجْلَيْهِ، وَطَرَفَهُ تَحْتَ رَأْسِهِ، فَسَلَّمَ عَلَيْهِ مُوسَى، فَكَشَفَ عَنْ وَجْهِهِ، وَقَالَ: هَلْ بِأَرْضٍ مِنْ سَلَامٍ؟ مَنْ أَنْتَ؟ قَالَ أَنَا مُوسَى. قَالَ: مُوسَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: فَمَا شَأْنُكَ؟ قَالَ: جِئْتُكَ لِتُعَلِّمَنِي مِمَّا عُلِّمْتُ رُشْدًا. قَالَ: يَكْفِيكَ التَّوْرَاةُ بِيَدِكَ، وَأَنَّ الْوَحْيَ يَأْتِيكَ!. يَا مُوسَى، إِنَّ لِي عِلْمًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لَكَ أَنْ تَعْلَمَهُ، وَإِنَّ لَكَ عِلْمًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لِي أَنْ أَعْلَمَهُ. فَأَخَذَ طَائِرٌ بِمِنْقَارِهِ مِنَ الْبَحْرِ [فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهُ مَا عِلْمِي وَعِلْمُكَ فِي جَنْبِ عِلْمِ اللَّهِ إِلَّا كَمَا أَخَذَ هَذَا الطَّائِرُ بِمِنْقَارِهِ مِنَ الْبَحْرِ] ، حَتَّى إِذَا رَكِبَا فِي السَّفِينَةِ وَجَدَا مَعَابِرَ صِغَارًا تَحْمِلُ أَهْلَ هَذَا السَّاحِلِ إِلَى هَذَا السَّاحِلِ الْآخَرِ عَرَفُوهُ، فَقَالُوا: عَبْدُ اللَّهِ الصَّالِحُ؟. قَالَ فَقُلْنَا لِسَعِيدٍ: خَضِرٌ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. لَا نَحْمِلُهُ بِأَجْرٍ. فَخَرَقَهَا، وَوَتَدَ فِيهَا وَتَدًا. قَالَ مُوسَى: ﴿أَخَرَقْتَهَا لِتُغْرِقَ أَهْلَهَا لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا إِمْرًا﴾ .

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: مُنْكِرًا. قَالَ: ﴿أَلَمْ أَقُلْ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ كَانَتِ الْأُولَى نِسْيَانًا، وَالْوُسْطَى شَرْطًا، وَالثَّالِثَةُ عَمْدًا ﴿قَالَ لَا تُؤَاخِذْنِي بِمَا نَسِيتُ وَلا تُرْهِقْنِي مِنْ أَمْرِي عُسْرًا. فَانْطَلَقَا﴾ . حَتَّى لَقِيَا غُلَامًا فَقَتَلَهُ. قَالَ يَعْلَى: قَالَ سَعِيدٌ، وَجَدَ غِلْمَانًا يَلْعَبُونَ، فَأَخَذَ غُلَامًا كَافِرًا ظَرِيفًا فَأَضْجَعَهُ، ثُمَّ ذَبَحَهُ بِالسِّكِّينِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَقَتَلْتَ نَفْسًا زَكِيَّةً﴾ لَمْ تَعْمَلْ بِالْحِنْثِ . وَابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ قَرَأَهَا ﴿زَكِيَّةً﴾ -" زَاكِيَة " مُسْلمَة، كَقَوْلِكَ : غُلَامًا زَكِيًّا فَانْطَلَقَا، فَوَجَدَا جِدَارًا يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَنْقَضَّ فَأَقَامَهُ، قَالَ [سَعِيدٌ] بِيَدِهِ هَكَذَا، وَرَفَعَ يَدَهُ فَاسْتَقَامَ -قَالَ يَعْلَى: حَسِبْتُ أَنَّ سَعِيدًا قَالَ: فَمَسْحَهُ بِيَدِهِ فَاسْتَقَامَ -قَالَ: ﴿لَوْ شِئْتَ لاتَّخَذْتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا﴾ قَالَ سَعِيدٌ: أَجْرًا نَأْكُلُهُ ﴿وَكَانَ وَرَاءَهُمْ مَلِكٌ﴾ وَكَانَ أَمَامَهُمْ، قَرَأَهَا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: "أَمَامَهُمْ مَلِكٌ" يَزْعُمُونَ عَنْ غَيْرِ سَعِيدٍ أَنَّهُ هُدَدُ بْنُ بُدَدَ، وَالْغُلَامُ الْمَقْتُولُ اسْمُهُ -يَزْعُمُونَ-جَيسُور ﴿مَلِكٌ يَأْخُذُ كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ غَصْبًا﴾ فَأَرَدْتُ إِذَا هِيَ مَرَّتْ بِهِ أَنْ يَدَعَهَا بِعَيْبِهَا، فَإِذَا جَاوَزَهُ أَصْلَحُوهَا فَانْتَفَعُوا بِهَا. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقُولُ: سَدُّوهَا بِقَارُورَةٍ. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقُولُ: بِالْقَارِ. ﴿فَكَانَ أَبَوَاهُ مُؤْمِنَيْنِ﴾ وَكَانَ كَافِرًا، ﴿فَخَشِينَا أَنْ يُرْهِقَهُمَا طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا﴾ . أَنْ يَحْمِلَهُمَا حُبّه عَلَى أَنْ يُتَابِعَاهُ عَلَى دِينِهِ ﴿فَأَرَدْنَا أَنْ يُبْدِلَهُمَا رَبُّهُمَا خَيْرًا مِنْهُ زَكَاةً﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَقَتَلْتَ نَفْسًا زَكِيَّةً﴾ ، ﴿وَأَقْرَبَ رُحْمًا﴾ : هُمَا بِهِ أَرْحَمُ مِنْهُمَا بِالْأَوَّلِ الَّذِي قَتَلَ خَضِرٌ. وَزَعَمَ غَيْرُ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ أَنَّهُمَا أُبْدِلَا جَارِيَةً. وَأَمَّا دَاوُدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَاصِمٍ فَقَالَ عَنْ غَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ: إِنَّهَا جَارِيَةٌ .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: خَطَبَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ فَقَالَ: مَا أَحَدٌ أَعْلَمُ بِاللَّهِ وَبِأَمْرِهِ مِنِّي. فَأمرَ أَنْ يَلْقَى هَذَا الرَّجُلَ. فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ بِزِيَادَةٍ وَنُقْصَانٍ ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عُمَارَةَ، عَنِ الْحَكَمِ بْنِ عُتَيْبَةَ ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: جَلَسْتُ عِنْدَ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَعِنْدَهُ نَفَرٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: يَا أَبَا الْعَبَّاسِ، إِنَّ نَوْفًا ابْنَ امْرَأَةِ كَعْبٍ، يَزْعُمُ عَنْ كَعْبٍ أَنَّ مُوسَى النَّبِيَّ الَّذِي طَلَبَ الْعَالَمَ إِنَّمَا هُوَ مُوسَى بْنُ مِيشَا؟ قَالَ سَعِيدٌ: فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أنوفٌ يَقُولُ هَذَا؟ قَالَ سَعِيدٌ: فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: نَعَمْ، أَنَا سَمِعْتُ نَوْفًا يَقُولُ ذَلِكَ. قَالَ: أَنْتِ سَمِعْتَهُ يَا سَعِيدُ؟ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: كَذَبَ نَوْفٌ. ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: حَدَّثَنِي أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنْ مُوسَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ سَأَلَ رَبَّهُ فَقَالَ: أَيْ رَبِّ، إِنْ كَانَ فِي عِبَادِكَ أَحَدٌ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ مِنِّي، فَدُلَّنِي عَلَيْهِ. فَقَالَ لَهُ: نَعَمْ، فِي عِبَادِي مَنْ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ. ثُمَّ نَعَتَ لَهُ مَكَانَهُ وَأَذِنَ لَهُ فِي لُقِيِّهِ. فَخَرَجَ مُوسَى وَمَعَهُ فَتَاهُ، وَمَعَهُ حُوتٌ مَلِيحٌ، قَدْ قِيلَ لَهُ: إِذَا حَيِيَ هَذَا الْحُوتُ فِي مَكَانٍ، فَصَاحِبُكَ هُنَالِكَ، وَقَدْ أَدْرَكْتَ حَاجَتَكَ. فَخَرَجَ مُوسَى وَمَعَهُ فَتَاهُ، وَمَعَهُ ذَلِكَ الْحُوتُ يَحْمِلَانِهِ، فَسَارَ حَتَّى جَهَدَهُ السَّيْرُ، وَانْتَهَى إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ وَإِلَى ذَلِكَ الْمَاءِ، وَذَلِكَ الْمَاءُ مَاءُ الْحَيَاةِ، من شَرِبَ مِنْهُ خُلِّدَ، وَلَا يُقَارِبُهُ شَيْءٌ مَيْتٌ إِلَّا حَيِيَ. فَلَمَّا نَزَلَا وَمَسَّ الْحُوتُ الْمَاءَ حَيِيَ ﴿فَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ سَرَبًا﴾ فَانْطَلَقَا فَلَمَّا جَاوَزَ مُنْقَلَبَه قَالَ: مُوسَى لِفَتَاهُ: ﴿آتِنَا غَدَاءَنَا لَقَدْ لَقِينَا مِنْ سَفَرِنَا هَذَا نَصَبًا﴾ قَالَ الْفَتَى -وَذَكَرَ-: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ أَوَيْنَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ فَإِنِّي نَسِيتُ الْحُوتَ وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهُ إِلا الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ وَاتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ عَجَبًا﴾ . قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَظَهَرَ مُوسَى عَلَى الصَّخْرَةِ حَتَّى إِذَا انْتَهَيَا إِلَيْهَا، فَإِذَا رَجُلٌ مُتَلَفِّفٌ فِي كِسَاءٍ لَهُ، فَسَلَّمَ مُوسَى، فَرَدَّ عَلَيْهِ الْعَالِمُ ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهُ: مَا جَاءَ بِكَ إِنْ كَانَ لَكَ فِي قَوْمِكَ لَشُغل؟. قَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: جِئْتُكَ لِتُعَلِّمَنِي مِمَّا عُلِّمْتَ رُشْدًا ﴿قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ وَكَانَ رَجُلًا يَعْلَمُ عِلْمَ الْغَيْبِ قَدْ عُلِّم ذَلِكَ -فَقَالَ مُوسَى: بَلَى. قَالَ: ﴿وَكَيْفَ تَصْبِرُ عَلَى مَا لَمْ تُحِطْ بِهِ خُبْرًا﴾ ؟ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا تَعْرِفُ ظَاهِرَ مَا تَرَى مِنَ الْعَدْلِ، وَلَمْ تُحِطْ مِنْ عِلْمِ الْغَيْبِ بِمَا أَعْلَمُ. ﴿قَالَ سَتَجِدُنِي إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ صَابِرًا وَلا أَعْصِي لَكَ أَمْرًا﴾ وَإِنْ رأيتُ مَا يُخَالِفُنِي، قَالَ: ﴿فَإِنِ اتَّبَعْتَنِي فَلا تَسْأَلْنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ﴾ [وَإِنْ أَنْكَرْتَهُ] ﴿حَتَّى أُحْدِثَ لَكَ مِنْهُ ذِكْرًا﴾ : فَانْطَلَقَا يَمْشِيَانِ عَلَى سَاحِلِ الْبَحْرِ يَتَعَرَّضَانِ النَّاسَ، يَلْتَمِسَانِ مَنْ يَحْمِلُهُمَا، حَتَّى مَرَّتْ بِهِمَا سَفِينَةٌ جَدِيدَةٌ وَثِيقَةٌ، لَمْ يَمُرَّ بِهِمَا مِنَ السُّفُنِ أَحْسَنُ وَلَا أَكْمَلُ وَلَا أَوْثَقُ مِنْهَا. فَسَأَلَا أَهْلَهَا أَنْ يَحْمِلُوهُمَا، فَحَمَلُوهُمَا ، فَلَمَّا اطْمَأَنَّا فِيهَا وَلجّجَت بِهِمَا مَعَ أَهْلِهَا، أَخْرَجُ مِنْقَارًا لَهُ وَمِطْرَقَةً، ثُمَّ عَمَدَ إِلَى نَاحِيَةٍ مِنْهَا فَضَرَبَ فِيهَا بِالْمِنْقَارِ حَتَّى خَرَقَهَا. ثُمَّ أَخَذَ لَوْحًا فَطَبَّقَهُ عَلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ جَلَسَ عَلَيْهَا يُرَقِّعُهَا، فَقَالَ: لَهُ مُوسَى -وَرَأَى أَمْرًا أَفْظَعَ بِهِ-: ﴿أَخَرَقْتَهَا لِتُغْرِقَ أَهْلَهَا لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا إِمْرًا * قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا * قَالَ لَا تُؤَاخِذْنِي بِمَا نَسِيتُ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا تَرَكْتُ مِنْ عَهْدِكَ، ﴿وَلا تُرْهِقْنِي مِنْ أَمْرِي عُسْرًا﴾ . ثُمَّ خَرَجَا مِنَ السَّفِينَةِ فَانْطَلَقَا، حَتَّى أَتَيَا أَهْلَ قَرْيَةٍ، فَإِذَا غِلْمَانٌ يَلْعَبُونَ خَلْفَهَا، فِيهِمْ غُلَامٌ لَيْسَ فِي الْغِلْمَانِ غُلَامٌ أَظْرَفُ مِنْهُ وَلَا أَثْرَى وَلَا أَوْضَأُ مِنْهُ، فَأَخَذَهُ بِيَدِهِ، وَأَخَذَ حَجَرًا فَضَرَبَ بِهِ رَأْسَهُ حَتَّى دَمَغَهُ فَقَتَلَهُ، قَالَ: فَرَأَى مُوسَى أَمْرًا فَظِيعًا لَا صَبْرَ عَلَيْهِ، صَبِيٌّ صَغِيرٌ قَتَلَهُ لَا ذَنْبَ لَهُ قَالَ: ﴿أَقَتَلْتَ نَفْسًا زَكِيَّةً﴾ أَيْ: صَغِيرَةً ﴿بِغَيْرِ نَفْسٍ لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا نُكْرًا * قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ لَكَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا * قَالَ إِنْ سَأَلْتُكَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ بَعْدَهَا فَلا تُصَاحِبْنِي قَدْ بَلَغْتَ مِنْ لَدُنِّي عُذْرًا﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أعْذرتَ فِي شَأْنِي. ﴿فَانْطَلَقَا حَتَّى إِذَا أَتَيَا أَهْلَ قَرْيَةٍ اسْتَطْعَمَا أَهْلَهَا فَأَبَوْا أَنْ يُضَيِّفُوهُمَا فَوَجَدَا فِيهَا جِدَارًا يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَنْقَضَّ﴾ ، فَهَدَمَهُ ثُمَّ قَعَدَ يَبْنِيهِ، فَضَجِرَ مُوسَى مِمَّا يَرَاهُ يَصْنَعُ مِنَ التَّكْلِيفِ، وَمَا لَيْسَ عَلَيْهِ صَبْرٌ، قَالَ: ﴿لَوْ شِئْتَ لاتَّخَذْتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا﴾ أَيْ: قَدِ اسْتَطْعَمْنَاهُمْ فَلَمْ يُطْعِمُونَا، وَضِفْنَاهُمْ فَلَمْ يُضَيّفونا، ثُمَّ قَعَدْتَ تَعْمَلُ مِنْ غَيْرِ صَنِيعَةٍ، وَلَوْ شِئْتَ لَأُعْطِيتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا فِي عَمَلِهِ؟. قَالَ: ﴿هَذَا فِرَاقُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنِكَ سَأُنَبِّئُكَ بِتَأْوِيلِ مَا لَمْ تَسْتَطِعْ عَلَيْهِ صَبْرًا * أَمَّا السَّفِينَةُ فَكَانَتْ لِمَسَاكِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَأَرَدْتُ أَنْ أَعِيبَهَا وَكَانَ وَرَاءَهُمْ مَلِكٌ يَأْخُذُ كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ غَصْبًا﴾ -وَفِي قِرَاءَةِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ: "كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ صَالِحَةٍ" -وَإِنَّمَا عِبْتُهَا لِأَرُدَّهُ عَنْهَا، فَسَلِمَتْ حِينَ رَأَى الْعَيْبَ الَّذِي صَنَعْتُ بِهَا. ﴿وَأَمَّا الْغُلامُ فَكَانَ أَبَوَاهُ مُؤْمِنَيْنِ فَخَشِينَا أَنْ يُرْهِقَهُمَا طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا * فَأَرَدْنَا أَنْ يُبْدِلَهُمَا رَبُّهُمَا خَيْرًا مِنْهُ زَكَاةً وَأَقْرَبَ رُحْمًا * وَأَمَّا الْجِدَارُ فَكَانَ لِغُلامَيْنِ يَتِيمَيْنِ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ وَكَانَ تَحْتَهُ كَنز لَهُمَا وَكَانَ أَبُوهُمَا صَالِحًا فَأَرَادَ رَبُّكَ أَنْ يَبْلُغَا أَشُدَّهُمَا وَيَسْتَخْرِجَا كَنزهُمَا رَحْمَةً مِنْ رَبِّكَ وَمَا فَعَلْتُهُ عَنْ أَمْرِي﴾ أَيْ: مَا فَعَلْتُهُ عَنْ نَفْسِي، ﴿ذَلِكَ تَأْوِيلُ مَا لَمْ تَسْطِعْ عَلَيْهِ صَبْرًا﴾ وَكَانَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: مَا كَانَ الْكَنْزُ إِلَّا عِلْمًا .

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا ظَهَرَ مُوسَى وَقَوْمُهُ عَلَى مِصْرَ، أَنْزَلَ قَوْمَهُ ، فَلَمَّا اسْتَقَرَّتْ بِهِمُ الدَّارُ، أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: أَنْ ذَكِّرْهُمْ بِأَيَّامِ اللَّهِ فَخَطَبَ قَوْمَهُ، فَذَكَرَ مَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ وَالنِّعْمَةِ، وَذَكَّرَهُمْ إِذْ نَجَّاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَذَكَّرَهُمْ هَلَاكَ عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَمَا اسْتَخْلَفَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَقَالَ: كَلَّمَ اللَّهُ نَبِيَّكُمْ تَكْلِيمًا، وَاصْطَفَانِي لِنَفْسِهِ، وَأَنْزَلَ عَلَيَّ مَحَبَّةً مِنْهُ، وَآتَاكُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَا سألتموه؛ فنبيكم أفضل أهل الأرض، وأنتم تقرؤون التَّوْرَاةَ، فَلَمْ يَتْرُكْ نِعْمَةً أَنْعَمَهَا عَلَيْهِمْ إِلَّا وَعَرَّفَهُمْ إِيَّاهَا. فَقَالَ لَهُ رَجُلٌ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ: هُمْ كَذَلِكَ يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ، قَدْ عَرَفْنَا الَّذِي تَقُولُ، فَهَلْ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ أَحَدٌ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: لَا. فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ جِبْرَائِيلَ إِلَى مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ ، فَقَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] يَقُولُ: وَمَا يُدْرِيكَ أَيْنَ أَضَعُ عِلْمِي؟ بَلَى . إِنَّ عَلَى شَطِّ الْبَحْرِ رَجُلًا هُوَ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ -قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ الْخَضِرُ-فَسَأَلَ مُوسَى رَبَّهُ أَنْ يُرِيَهُ إِيَّاهُ، فَأَوْحَى إِلَيْهِ: أَنِ ائْتِ الْبَحْرَ، فَإِنَّكَ تَجِدُ عَلَى شَطِّ الْبَحْرِ حُوتًا، فَخُذْهُ فَادْفَعْهُ إِلَى فَتَاكَ، ثُمَّ الْزَمْ شَطَّ الْبَحْرِ، فَإِذَا نَسِيتَ الْحُوتَ وَهَلَكَ مِنْكَ، فَثَمَّ تَجِدُ الْعَبْدَ الصَّالِحَ الَّذِي تَطْلُبُ. فَلَمَّا طَالَ سَفَرُ مُوسَى نَبِيِّ اللَّهِ وَنَصَبَ فِيهِ، سَأَلَ فَتَاهُ عَنِ الْحُوتِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ فَتَاهُ وَهُوَ غُلَامُهُ: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ أَوَيْنَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ فَإِنِّي نَسِيتُ الْحُوتَ وَمَا أَنْسَانِيهُ إِلا الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ﴾ لَكَ، قَالَ الْفَتَى: لَقَدْ رَأَيْتُ الْحُوتَ حِينَ اتَّخَذَ سَبِيلَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ سَرَبًا فَأَعْجَبَ ذَلِكَ مُوسَى، فَرَجَعَ حَتَّى أَتَى الصَّخْرَةَ، فَوَجَدَ الْحُوتَ، فَجُعِلَ الْحُوتُ يَضْرِبُ فِي الْبَحْرِ وَيَتْبَعُهُ مُوسَى، وَجَعْلَ مُوسَى يُقَدِّمُ عَصَاهُ يُفَرِّجُ بِهَا عَنْهُ الْمَاءَ يَتْبَعُ الْحُوتَ، وَجَعَلَ الْحُوتُ لَا يَمَسُّ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْبَحْرِ إِلَّا يَبِسَ، حَتَّى يَكُونَ صَخْرَةً ، فَجَعَلَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ يَعْجَبُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، حَتَّى انْتَهَى بِهِ الْحُوتُ إِلَى جَزِيرَةٍ مِنْ جَزَائِرِ الْبَحْرِ، فَلَقِيَ الْخَضِرَ بِهَا فَسَلَّمَ عَلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ الْخَضِرُ: وَعَلَيْكَ السَّلَامُ، وَأَنَّى يَكُونُ السَّلَامُ بِهَذِهِ الْأَرْضِ؟ وَمَنْ أَنْتَ؟ قَالَ: أَنَا مُوسَى. فَقَالَ الْخَضِرُ: أَصَاحِبُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ؟ [قَالَ: نَعَمْ] فَرَحَّبَ بِهِ وَقَالَ: مَا جَاءَ بِكَ؟ قال جئتك ﴿عَلَى أَنْ تُعَلِّمَنِ مِمَّا عُلِّمْتَ رُشْدًا قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ يَقُولُ: لَا تُطِيقُ ذَلِكَ. قَالَ مُوسَى ﴿سَتَجِدُنِي إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ صَابِرًا وَلا أَعْصِي لَكَ أَمْرًا﴾ قَالَ: فَانْطَلَقَ بِهِ، وَقَالَ لَهُ: لَا تَسْأَلْنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ أَصْنَعُهُ حَتَّى أُبَيِّنَ لَكَ شَأْنَهُ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى أُحْدِثَ لَكَ مِنْهُ ذِكْرًا﴾

وَقَالَ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُتبة بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُ تَمَارَى هُوَ وَالْحُرُّ بْنُ قَيْسِ بْنِ حِصْنٍ الْفَزَارِيُّ فِي صَاحِبِ مُوسَى، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ خَضِرٌ. فَمَرَّ بِهِمَا أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ فَدَعَاهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فَقَالَ: إِنِّي تَمَارَيْتُ أَنَا وَصَاحِبِي هَذَا فِي صَاحِبِ مُوسَى الَّذِي سَأَلَ السَّبِيلَ إِلَى لُقيه، فَهَلْ سَمِعْتَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَذْكُرُ شَأْنَهُ؟ قَالَ: إِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يقول: "بَيْنَا مُوسَى فِي مَلَأٍ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ إِذْ جَاءَهُ رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: تَعْلَمُ مَكَانَ رَجُلٍ أَعْلَمَ مِنْكَ؟ قَالَ: لَا؛ فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَى مُوسَى بَلَى عَبْدُنَا خَضِرٌ. فَسَأَلَ مُوسَى السَّبِيلَ إِلَى لُقيّه فَجَعَلَ اللَّهُ لَهُ الْحُوتَ آيَةً وَقِيلَ لَهُ: إِذَا فَقَدت الْحُوتَ [فَهُوَ ثَمَّةَ] فَارْجِعْ، فَإِنَّكَ سَتَلْقَاهُ. فَكَانَ مُوسَى يَتْبَعُ أَثَرَ الْحُوتِ فِي الْبَحْرِ. فَقَالَ فَتَى مُوسَى لِمُوسَى: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ أَوَيْنَا إِلَى الصَّخْرَةِ فَإِنِّي نَسِيتُ الْحُوتَ﴾ قَالَ مُوسَى ﴿ذَلِكَ مَا كُنَّا نَبْغِ فَارْتَدَّا عَلَى آثَارِهِمَا قَصَصًا﴾ فَوَجَدَا عَبْدَنَا خَضِرًا فكان من شأنهما ما قص في الله كِتَابِهِ

---

## 18:66-70 — verses 66-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty is informing us of what Moses (peace be upon him) said to that man of knowledge, namely al-Khidr, whom Allah singled out with knowledge that He had not made known to Moses, just as He had given Moses knowledge that He had not given to al-Khidr. {Moses said to him, "Shall I follow you"} is a question posed with gentleness, not in the manner of imposition or compulsion. And this is how the question of a student to a scholar ought to be. His saying: {Shall I follow you} means: shall I accompany you and keep your company, {on condition that you teach me something of the right guidance which you have been taught} meaning: something of what Allah has taught you, by which I may seek guidance in my affairs, from beneficial knowledge and righteous action.

Thereupon al-Khidr {said} to Moses: {Indeed, you will not be able to have patience with me} meaning: you will not be able to accompany me because of what you will see from me of actions that contradict your Law. For I am upon a portion of Allah's knowledge which Allah has taught me, and you are upon a portion of Allah's knowledge which Allah has taught you. Each of us is charged with matters from Allah that the other is not charged with, and you are not able to accompany me.

{And how can you have patience about something you cannot encompass in knowledge?} That is: I know that you will object to things I do for which you have an excuse, but you have not been made aware of their inner wisdom and benefit, which I alone have been made aware of, without you.

Moses {said} to him: {You will find me, if Allah wills, patient} meaning: with what I see of your affairs, {and I will not disobey you in any order} meaning: I will not oppose you in anything. At that, al-Khidr made a condition with him, {He said, "Then if you follow me, do not ask me about anything} meaning: from the outset, {until I myself mention it to you"} meaning: until I begin to speak of it to you before you ask me.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn 'Abbas said: Moses asked his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, saying: "My Lord, which of Your servants is most beloved to You?" He said: "The one who remembers Me and does not forget Me." He said: "Then which of Your servants judges best?" He said: "The one who judges by truth and does not follow desire." He said: "My Lord, which of Your servants is most knowledgeable?" He said: "The one who seeks people's knowledge in addition to his own knowledge, hoping he may come upon a word that guides him to right guidance or turns him away from ruin." He said: "My Lord, is there anyone on Your earth more knowledgeable than I?" He said: "Yes." He said: "Who is he?" He said: "Al-Khidr." He said: "Where shall I seek him?" He said: "At the shore, by the rock where the fish slips away." He said: So Moses went out seeking him, until what Allah has mentioned came to pass, and Moses arrived at him by the rock, and each of them greeted the other with salam. Moses said to him: "I wish that you would let me accompany you." He said: "You will not be able to bear my company." He said: "Yes, I will." He said: "Then if you accompany me, {do not ask me about anything until I myself mention it to you}." He said: So he journeyed with him upon the sea until he reached the confluence of the two seas, and there is no place on earth with more water than it. He said: And Allah sent a small bird, and it began to draw water from the sea with its beak, and he said to Moses: "How much do you think this bird has diminished from this water?" He said: "How little it has diminished!" He said: "O Moses, my knowledge and your knowledge, in comparison to the knowledge of Allah, are like what this bird has drawn from this water." And Moses had said to himself that there was no one more knowledgeable than he, or had spoken it aloud, and it was for that reason that he was commanded to go to al-Khidr. And he mentioned the rest of the hadith concerning the piercing of the ship, the killing of the boy, and the repair of the wall, and its explanation to him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ قِيلِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ لِذَلِكَ [الرَّجُلِ] الْعَالِمِ، وَهُوَ الْخَضِرُ، الَّذِي خَصَّهُ اللَّهُ بِعِلْمٍ لَمْ يُطْلِعْ عَلَيْهِ مُوسَى، كَمَّا أَنَّهُ أَعْطَى مُوسَى مِنَ الْعِلْمِ مَا لَمْ يُعْطِهِ الْخَضِرَ، ﴿قَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى هَلْ أَتَّبِعُكَ﴾ سُؤَالٌ بِتَلَطُّفٍ ، لَا عَلَى وَجْهِ الْإِلْزَامِ وَالْإِجْبَارِ. وَهَكَذَا يَنْبَغِي أَنْ يَكُونَ سُؤَالُ الْمُتَعَلِّمِ مِنَ الْعَالِمِ. وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَتَّبِعُكَ﴾ أي: أصحبك وأرافقك، ﴿عَلَى أَنْ تُعَلِّمَنِ مِمَّا عُلِّمْتَ رُشْدًا﴾ أَيْ: مِمَّا عَلَّمَكَ اللَّهُ شَيْئًا، أَسْتَرْشِدُ بِهِ فِي أَمْرِي، مِنْ عِلْمٍ نَافِعٍ وَعَمَلٍ صَالِحٍ.

فَعِنْدَهَا ﴿قَالَ﴾ الْخَضِرُ لِمُوسَى: ﴿إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتَ لا تقدرأن تُصَاحِبَنِي لِمَا تَرَى [منِّي] مِنَ الْأَفْعَالِ الَّتِي تُخَالِفُ شَرِيعَتَكَ؛ لِأَنِّي عَلَى عِلْمٍ مَنْ عِلْمِ اللَّهِ، مَا عَلَّمَكَهُ اللَّهُ، وَأَنْتَ عَلَى عِلْمٍ مَنْ عِلْمِ اللَّهِ، مَا عَلَّمَنِيهِ اللَّهُ، فَكُلٌّ مِنَّا مُكَلَّفٌ بِأُمُورٍ . مِنَ اللَّهِ دُونَ صَاحِبِهِ، وَأَنْتَ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى صُحْبَتِي.

﴿وَكَيْفَ تَصْبِرُ عَلَى مَا لَمْ تُحِطْ بِهِ خُبْرًا﴾ فَأَنَا أَعْرِفُ أَنَّكَ سَتُنْكِرُ عَلَيَّ مَا أَنْتَ مَعْذُورٌ فِيهِ، ولكنْ مَا اطَّلَعَتْ عَلَى حِكْمَتِهِ وَمَصْلَحَتِهِ الْبَاطِنَةِ الَّتِي اطَّلَعْتُ أَنَا عَلَيْهَا دُونَكَ.

﴿قَالَ﴾ لَهُ مُوسَى: ﴿سَتَجِدُنِي إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ صَابِرًا﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى مَا أَرَى مِنْ أُمُورِكَ، ﴿وَلا أَعْصِي لَكَ أَمْرًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا أُخَالِفُكَ فِي شَيْءٍ. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ شَارَطَهُ الْخَضِرُ ﴿قَالَ فَإِنِ اتَّبَعْتَنِي فَلا تَسْأَلْنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ﴾ أَيْ: ابْتِدَاءً ﴿حَتَّى أُحْدِثَ لَكَ مِنْهُ ذِكْرًا﴾ أَيْ: حَتَّى أَبْدَأَكَ أَنَا بِهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ تَسْأَلَنِي.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، عَنْ هَارُونَ بْنِ عَنْتَرَةَ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابن عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: سَأَلَ مُوسَى رَبَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَقَالَ : رَبِّ، أَيُّ عِبَادِكَ أَحَبُّ إِلَيْكَ؟ قَالَ: الَّذِي يَذْكُرُنِي وَلَا يَنْسَانِي. قَالَ فَأَيُّ عِبَادِكَ أَقَضَى؟ قَالَ: الَّذِي يَقْضِي بِالْحَقِّ وَلَا يَتَّبِعُ الْهَوَى. قَالَ أَيْ رَبِّ، أَيُّ عِبَادِكَ أَعْلَمُ؟ قَالَ الَّذِي يَبْتَغِي عِلْمَ النَّاسِ إِلَى عِلْمِهِ، عَسَى أَنْ يُصِيبَ كَلِمَةً تَهْدِيهِ إِلَى هُدًى أَوْ تَرُدُّهُ عَنْ رَدًى. قَالَ: أَيْ رَبٍّ هَلْ فِي أَرْضِكَ أَحَدٌ أَعْلَمُ مِنِّي؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: فَمَنْ هُوَ؟ قَالَ الْخَضِرُ. قَالَ: فَأَيْنَ أَطْلُبُهُ؟ قَالَ عَلَى السَّاحِلِ عِنْدَ الصَّخْرَةِ، الَّتِي يَنْفَلِتُ عِنْدَهَا الْحُوتُ. قَالَ: فَخَرَجَ مُوسَى يَطْلُبُهُ، حَتَّى كَانَ مَا ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ، وَانْتَهَى مُوسَى إِلَيْهِ عِنْدَ الصَّخْرَةِ، فَسَلَّمَ كُلُّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمَا عَلَى صَاحِبِهِ. فَقَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: إِنِّي أُرِيدُ أَنْ تَصْحَبَنِي قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تُطِيقَ صُحْبَتِي. قَالَ: بَلَى. قَالَ: فَإِنْ صَحِبْتَنِي ﴿فَلا تَسْأَلْنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ حَتَّى أُحْدِثَ لَكَ مِنْهُ ذِكْرًا﴾ قَالَ: فَسَارَ بِهِ فِي الْبَحْرِ حَتَّى انْتَهَى إِلَى مَجْمَعِ الْبُحُورِ ، وَلَيْسَ فِي الْأَرْضِ مَكَانٌ أَكْثَرُ مَاءً مِنْهُ. قَالَ: وَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ الْخُطَّافَ، فَجَعَلَ يَسْتَقِي مِنْهُ بِمِنْقَارِهِ، فَقَالَ لِمُوسَى: كَمْ تَرَى هَذَا الْخُطَّافَ رَزَأَ مِنْ هَذَا الْمَاءِ؟ قَالَ: مَا أَقَلَّ مَا رَزَأَ! قَالَ: يَا مُوسَى فَإِنَّ عِلْمِي وَعِلْمَكَ فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ كقَدْر مَا اسْتَقَى هَذَا الْخُطَّافُ مِنْ هَذَا الْمَاءِ. وَكَانَ مُوسَى قَدْ حَدَّثَ نَفْسَهُ أَنَّهُ لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ أَعْلَمُ مِنْهُ، أَوْ تَكَلَّمَ بِهِ، فَمِنْ ثَمَّ أُمِرَ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ الْخَضِرَ. وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ فِي خَرْقِ السَّفِينَةِ، وَقَتْلِ الْغُلَامِ، وَإِصْلَاحِ الْجِدَارِ، وَتَفْسِيرِهِ لَهُ ذَلِكَ.

---

## 18:71-73 — verses 71-73 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing us about Musa and his companion, who was al-Khidr, that the two set out once they had come to an agreement and had accompanied one another, with al-Khidr having stipulated to him that he should not question him about anything he found objectionable until he himself initiated an explanation and clarification of it on his own. So the two of them boarded the ship. It has already been mentioned in the hadith how they boarded the ship, and that the crew recognized al-Khidr, so they carried the two of them without nawl, meaning without fare, as an honor to al-Khidr. When the ship had carried them out to sea and had entered the open depths, that is, had gone into the lujjah (the deep open water), al-Khidr stood up and made a hole in it, pulling out one of its planks, then patched it up. Musa (peace be upon him) could not restrain himself and said, objecting to him: {Have you made a hole in it to drown its people?} This lam (the letter/particle "to") here is the lam of consequence, not the lam of purpose, just as the poet said: "They give birth for death and build for ruin."

{You have certainly done a monstrous thing} Mujahid said: something objectionable. Qatadah said: something astonishing. At that point al-Khidr said to him, reminding him of the condition stipulated earlier: {Did I not say that you would never be able to have patience with me?} meaning: this act that I did, I did it deliberately, and it is among the matters concerning which I stipulated with you that you would not object to me, because you have not encompassed it with knowledge; it has an inner aspect which is a benefit that you did not know.

{He said}, that is, Musa: {Do not take me to task for what I forgot, and do not make my affair difficult for me} meaning: do not constrict me and do not be harsh with me. For this reason it was mentioned earlier in the hadith from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he said: "The first of the two lapses from Musa was due to forgetfulness."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ مُوسَى وَصَاحِبِهِ، وَهُوَ الْخَضِرُ، أَنَّهُمَا انْطَلَقَا لَمَّا تَوَافَقَا وَاصْطَحَبَا، وَاشْتَرَطَ عَلَيْهِ أَلَّا يَسْأَلَهُ عَنْ شَيْءٍ أَنْكَرَهُ حَتَّى يَكُونَ هُوَ الَّذِي يَبْتَدِئُهُ مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ نَفْسِهِ بِشَرْحِهِ وَبَيَانِهِ، فَرَكِبَا فِي السَّفِينَةِ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ كَيْفَ رَكِبَا فِي السَّفِينَةِ، وَأَنَّهُمْ عَرَفُوا الْخَضِرَ، فَحَمَلُوهُمَا بِغَيْرِ نَوْلٍ -يَعْنِي بِغَيْرِ أُجْرَةٍ-تَكْرِمَةً لِلْخَضِرِ. فَلَمَّا اسْتَقَلَّتْ بِهِمُ السَّفِينَةُ فِي الْبَحْرِ، وَلَجَّجَتْ أَيْ: دَخَلَتِ اللُّجَّةَ، قَامَ الْخَضِرُ فَخَرَقَهَا، وَاسْتَخْرَجَ لَوْحًا مِنْ أَلْوَاحِهَا ثُمَّ رَقَعَهَا. فَلَمْ يَمْلِكْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، نَفْسَهُ أَنْ قَالَ مُنْكِرًا عَلَيْهِ: ﴿أَخَرَقْتَهَا لِتُغْرِقَ أَهْلَهَا﴾ . وَهَذِهِ اللَّامُ لَامُ الْعَاقِبَةِ لَا لَامُ التَّعْلِيلِ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ لدُوا للْمَوت وابْنُوا للخَرَاب

﴿لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا إِمْرًا﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: مُنْكَرًا. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ عَجَبًا. فَعِنْدَهَا قَالَ لَهُ الْخَضِرُ مُذَكِّرًا بِمَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنَ الشَّرْطِ: ﴿أَلَمْ أَقُلْ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ يَعْنِي وَهَذَا الصَّنِيعُ فَعَلْتُهُ قَصْدًا، وَهُوَ مِنَ الْأُمُورِ الَّتِي اشْتَرَطْتُ مَعَكَ أَلَّا تُنْكِرَ عَلَيَّ فِيهَا، لِأَنَّكَ لَمْ تُحِطْ بِهَا خُبْرًا، وَلَهَا دَاخِلٌ هُوَ مَصْلَحَةٌ وَلَمْ تَعْلَمْهُ أَنْتَ.

﴿قَالَ﴾ أَيْ مُوسَى: ﴿لَا تُؤَاخِذْنِي بِمَا نَسِيتُ وَلا تُرْهِقْنِي مِنْ أَمْرِي عُسْرًا﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُضَيِّقُ عَلَيَّ وتُشدد عَلَيَّ؛ وَلِهَذَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "كَانَتِ الْأُولَى مِنْ مُوسَى نِسْيَانًا".

---

## 18:74-76 — verses 74-76 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {So they set out} that is, after that, {until when they met a boy, and he killed him}. It has already been mentioned that he was playing with the boys in a village among the villages, and that he deliberately went for him among them all. He was the best-looking of them, the most handsome and the fairest of them, and he killed him. It is reported that he cut off his head; and it is said he crushed it with a stone. And in another report: he plucked it off with his hand. And Allah knows best.

When Musa (peace be upon him) witnessed this, he denounced it even more severely than the first incident, and hastened to say: {Have you killed a pure soul} that is, a young one who had not committed any wrongdoing nor yet borne any sin, {who had killed no one}, that is, without any basis justifying his killing, {you have certainly done a horrible thing}, that is, one plainly abominable.

{He said: Did I not tell you that you would never be able to have patience with me?} Thus he again emphasized the reminder of the original condition. For this reason Musa said to him: {If I ask you about anything after this} that is, if I object to you about anything after this time, {then do not keep me as a companion. You have received from me sufficient excuse}, that is, you have received an excuse from me time after time.

Ibn Jarir said: Abdullah ibn Ziyad narrated to us, Hajjaj ibn Muhammad narrated to us, from Hamzah al-Zayyat, from Abu Ishaq, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, who said: The Prophet ﷺ, when he mentioned someone and prayed for him, would begin with himself. One day he said: "May the mercy of Allah be upon us and upon Musa. Had he remained with his companion, he would have seen wondrous things, but he said: 'If I ask you about anything after this, then do not keep me as a companion. You have received from me sufficient excuse'" [with the word emphasized in pronunciation].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَانْطَلَقَا﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا لَقِيَا غُلامًا فَقَتَلَهُ﴾ وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَلْعَبُ مَعَ الْغِلْمَانِ فِي قَرْيَةٍ مِنَ الْقُرَى، وَأَنَّهُ عَمَدَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمْ، وَكَانَ أَحْسَنَهُمْ وَأَجْمَلَهُمْ وَأَوْضَأَهُمْ فَقَتَلَهُ، فَرُوِيَ أَنَّهُ احْتَزَّ رَأْسَهُ، وَقِيلَ: رَضَخَهُ بِحَجَرٍ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: اقْتَطَفَهُ بِيَدِهِ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

فَلَمَّا شَاهَدَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، هَذَا أَنْكَرَهُ أَشَدَّ مِنَ الْأَوَّلِ، وَبَادَرَ فَقَالَ: ﴿أَقَتَلْتَ نَفْسًا زَكِيَّةً﴾ أَيْ صَغِيرَةً لَمْ تَعْمَلِ الْحِنْثَ ، وَلَا حَمَلَتْ إِثْمًا بَعْدُ، فَقَتَلْتَهُ؟! ﴿بِغَيْرِ نَفْسٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِغَيْرِ مُسْتَنَدٍ لِقَتْلِهِ ﴿لَقَدْ جِئْتَ شَيْئًا نُكْرًا﴾ أَيْ: ظَاهِرَ النَّكَارَةِ.

﴿قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ لَكَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيعَ مَعِيَ صَبْرًا﴾ فَأَكَّدَ أَيْضًا فِي التِّذْكَارِ بِالشَّرْطِ الْأَوَّلِ؛ فَلِهَذَا قَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: ﴿إِنْ سَأَلْتُكَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ بَعْدَهَا﴾ أَيْ: إِنِ اعْتَرَضْتُ عَلَيْكَ بِشَيْءٍ بَعْدَ هَذِهِ الْمَرَّةِ ﴿فَلا تُصَاحِبْنِي قَدْ بَلَغْتَ مِنْ لَدُنِّي عُذْرًا﴾ أي: قد أعذرت إِلَيَّ مَرَّةً بَعْدَ مَرَّةٍ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ حَمْزَةَ الزَّيَّاتِ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: كَانَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ إِذَا ذَكَرَ أَحَدًا فَدَعَا لَهُ، بَدَأَ بِنَفْسِهِ، فَقَالَ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ: "رَحْمَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْنَا وَعَلَى مُوسَى، لَوْ لَبِثَ مَعَ صَاحِبِهِ لَأَبْصَرَ الْعَجَبَ وَلَكِنَّهُ قَالَ إِنْ سَأَلْتُكَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ بَعْدَهَا فَلَا تُصَاحِبْنِي قَدْ بَلَغْتَ مِنْ لَدُنِّي عُذْرًا" [مُثَقَّلَةً] .

---

## 18:77-78 — verses 77-78 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the two of them: that they set off after the first two occasions, {until, when they came to the people of a town}. Ibn Jarir reported from Ibn Sirin that it was Aylah (Eilat). In the hadith it is stated: "until, when they came to the people of a stingy town," meaning: miserly. {they asked its people for hospitality, but they refused to host them. Then they found in it a wall about to collapse}. The ascription of "wanting" here to the wall is by way of metaphor, for "wanting" (irada) among created things carries the meaning of leaning. And "collapsing" (inqidad) means falling down.

His saying: {so he set it up straight} means: he returned it to a state of standing upright. It was mentioned earlier in the hadith that he restored it with his own two hands and propped it up until he had corrected its leaning. This was a miraculous act (kharq). At that point Musa (peace be upon him) said to him: {If you had wished, you could have taken payment for it}, meaning: since they did not offer us hospitality, it would have been fitting for you not to work for them without charge.

{He said, "This is the parting between me and you"} [that is: because you had stipulated, at the killing of the boy, that if you asked me about anything after that you would no longer accompany me, so this is the parting between me and you], {Now I will inform you of the interpretation}, meaning: the explanation, {of that which you were unable to bear patiently}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْهُمَا: إِنَّهُمَا انْطَلَقَا بَعْدَ الْمَرَّتَيْنِ الْأُولَيَيْنِ ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا أَتَيَا أَهْلَ قَرْيَةٍ﴾ روى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ سِيرِينَ أَنَّهَا الْأَيْلَةُ وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "حَتَّى إِذَا أَتَيَا أَهْلَ قَرْيَةٍ لِئَامًا" أَيْ: بُخَلَاءَ ﴿فَأَبَوْا أَنْ يُضَيِّفُوهُمَا فَوَجَدَا فِيهَا جِدَارًا يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَنْقَضَّ﴾ إِسْنَادُ الْإِرَادَةِ هَاهُنَا إِلَى الْجِدَارِ عَلَى سَبِيلِ الِاسْتِعَارَةِ، فَإِنَّ الْإِرَادَةَ فِي الْمُحْدَثَاتِ بِمَعْنَى الْمَيْلِ. وَالِانْقِضَاضُ هُوَ: السُّقُوطُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَقَامَهُ﴾ أَيْ: فَرَدَّهُ إِلَى حَالَةِ الِاسْتِقَامَةِ وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ أَنَّهُ رَدَّهُ بِيَدَيْهِ، وَدَعَمَهُ حَتَّى رَدَّ مَيْلَهُ. وَهَذَا خَارِقٌ فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ قَالَ مُوسَى لَهُ ﴿لَوْ شِئْتَ لاتَّخَذْتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا﴾ أَيْ: لِأَجْلِ أَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يُضَيِّفُونَا كَانَ يَنْبَغِي أَلَّا تَعْمَلَ لَهُمْ مَجَّانًا 

﴿قَالَ هَذَا فِرَاقُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنِكَ﴾ [أَيْ: لِأَنَّكَ شَرَطْتَ عِنْدَ قَتْلِ الْغُلَامِ أَنَّكَ إِنْ سَأَلْتَنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ بَعْدَهَا فَلَا تُصَاحِبْنِي، فَهُوَ فِرَاقُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكَ] ، ﴿، سَأُنَبِّئُكَ بِتَأْوِيلِ﴾ أَيْ: بِتَفْسِيرِ ﴿مَا لَمْ تَسْتَطِعْ عَلَيْهِ صَبْرًا﴾ .

---

## 18:79 — verse 79

### Translation

This is the explanation of what had been problematic for Musa (peace be upon him), and what its apparent form had seemed objectionable, while God had disclosed to al-Khidr (peace be upon him) its inner reality. He said: I only damaged the boat in order to make it defective, [because they used to pass with it by a king among the tyrants who {seized every boat}, that is, every good and sound boat, {by force}, so I wanted to make it defective] so that he would turn away from it because of its defect, and thus its owners, the poor people who had nothing else by which to benefit besides it, would be able to make use of it. It has also been said that they were orphans.

Ibn Jurayj related from Wahb ibn Sulayman, from Shu'ayb al-Jubba'i, that the name of that king was Hudad ibn Budad. This has already been mentioned before as well, in the report of al-Bukhari, and he is mentioned in the Torah among the descendants of "al-'Is ibn Ishaq," and he is one of the kings explicitly named in the Torah. And God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هذا تفسير ما أشكل أمره على موسى، عليه السلام، وما كان أنكر ظاهره وقد أظهر الله الخضر، عليه السلام، على باطنة فقال إن: السفينة إنما خرقتها لأعيبها؛ [لأنهم كانوا يمرون بها على ملك من الظلمة ﴿يَأْخُذُ كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ﴾ صالحة، أي: جيدة ﴿غَصْبًا﴾ فأردت أن أعيبها] لأرده عنها لعيبها ، فينتفع بها أصحابها المساكين الذين لم يكن لهم شيء ينتفعون به غيرها. وقد قيل: إنهم أيتام.

و [قد] روى ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ شعيب الجبائي؛ أن اسم ذلك الملك هُدَدَ بن بُدَدَ، وقد تقدم أيضًا في رواية البخاري، وهو مذكور في التوراة في ذرية "العيص بن إسحاق" وهو من الملوك المنصوص عليهم في التوراة، والله أعلم

---

## 18:80-81 — verses 80-81 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It has already been mentioned that this boy's name was Jaysur. In the hadith from Ibn Abbas, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, from the Prophet ﷺ, he said: "The boy whom al-Khidr killed was created a disbeliever on the day he was created." Ibn Jarir related it from the hadith of Ibn Ishaq, from Sa'id, from Ibn Abbas. And this is why He said: {And his parents were believers, so we feared that he would burden them with transgression and disbelief}.

That is: his love would drive them to follow him into disbelief.

Qatadah said: His parents rejoiced in him when he was born, and grieved over him when he was killed, but had he lived, his continued life would have been their destruction. So let a man be content with the decree of God, for God's decree for the believer, in what he dislikes, is better for him than His decree in what he loves.

It is authentically established in the hadith: "God does not decree anything for the believer except that it is good for him." And the Exalted said: {But perhaps you dislike a thing which is good for you} [al-Baqarah: 216].

As for His saying [the Exalted]: {So we desired that their Lord replace him for them with one better than him in purity and nearer in mercy}, that is: a child more pure than this one, and more merciful and compassionate toward them than he was. This was said by Ibn Jurayj.

Qatadah said: More dutiful to his parents.

It has already been mentioned that they were given a girl in exchange. And it is said that when al-Khidr killed him, his mother was already pregnant with a Muslim boy. This was said by Ibn Jurayj.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّ هَذَا الْغُلَامَ كَانَ اسْمُهُ جَيْسُور. وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَاسٍ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "الْغُلَامُ الَّذِي قَتَلَهُ الْخَضِرُ طُبِعَ يَوْمَ طُبِعَ كَافِرًا". رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَكَانَ أَبَوَاهُ مُؤْمِنَيْنِ فَخَشِينَا أَنْ يُرْهِقَهُمَا طُغْيَانًا وَكُفْرًا﴾

أَيْ: يَحْمِلُهُمَا حُبُّهُ عَلَى مُتَابَعَتِهِ عَلَى الْكُفْرِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَدْ فَرِحَ بِهِ أَبَوَاهُ حِينَ وُلِدَ، وَحَزِنَا عَلَيْهِ حِينَ قُتِلَ، وَلَوْ بَقِيَ كَانَ فِيهِ هَلَاكُهُمَا، فَلْيَرْضَ امْرُؤٌ بِقَضَاءِ اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ قَضَاءَ اللَّهِ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ فِيمَا يَكْرَهُ خَيْرٌ لَهُ مِنْ قَضَائِهِ فِيمَا يُحِبُّ.

وَصَحَّ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "لَا يَقْضِي اللَّهُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ قَضَاءً إِلَّا كَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ". وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَعَسَى أَنْ تَكْرَهُوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٢١٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ [تَعَالَى] ﴿فَأَرَدْنَا أَنْ يُبْدِلَهُمَا رَبُّهُمَا خَيْرًا مِنْهُ زَكَاةً وَأَقْرَبَ رُحْمًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَدًا أَزْكَى مِنْ هَذَا، وَهُمَا أَرْحَمُ بِهِ مِنْهُ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَبَرُّ بِوَالِدَيْهِ.

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ أَنَّهُمَا بُدِّلَا جَارِيَةً. وَقِيلَ لَمَّا قَتَلَهُ الْخَضِرُ كَانَتْ أُمُّهُ حَامِلًا بِغُلَامٍ مُسْلِمٍ. قَالَهُ ابْنُ جُرَيْحٍ

---

## 18:82 — verse 82

### Translation

This verse contains evidence for applying the term "village" (qarya) to a city, because he first said {until when the two of them came to the people of a village} [al-Kahf: 77], and then said here: {and there was for two orphan boys in the city}, just as the Almighty said: {and how many a village stronger in might than your village which expelled you} [Muhammad: 13], and {and they said, why was this Qur'an not sent down upon a great man from the two villages} [al-Zukhruf: 31], meaning Mecca and al-Ta'if.

The meaning of the verse is that this wall was repaired only because it belonged to two orphan boys in the city, and beneath it was a treasure belonging to them.

Ikrimah, Qatadah, and others said: beneath it was buried wealth belonging to them. This is the apparent sense of the context of the verse, and it is the choice of Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him.

Al-'Awfi reported from Ibn 'Abbas: beneath it was a treasure of knowledge. Sa'id ibn Jubayr said the same, and Mujahid said: scrolls containing knowledge. A raised hadith (marfu') has come which supports this. The hafiz Abu Bakr Ahmad ibn 'Amr ibn 'Abd al-Khaliq al-Bazzar said in his well-known Musnad: [chain] Ibrahim ibn Sa'id al-Jawhari told us, Bishr ibn al-Mundhir told us, al-Harith ibn 'Abdullah al-Yahsubi from 'Ayyash ibn 'Abbas al-Qatbani from Ibn Hujayrah, from Abu Dharr, may God be pleased with him, [he raised it to the Prophet ﷺ] who said: "The treasure that God mentioned in His Book is a tablet of solid gold on which is written: I marvel at one who is certain of decree (al-qadar), why does he toil? And I marvel at one who remembers the Fire, why does he laugh? And I marvel at one who remembers death, why is he heedless? There is no god but God, Muhammad is the Messenger of God."

This Bishr ibn al-Mundhir is called the judge of al-Massisah. The hafiz Abu Ja'far al-'Uqayli said: there is an error in his hadith.

Reports (athar) have been narrated on this matter from the predecessors (salaf). Ibn Jarir said in his tafsir: [chain] Ya'qub told me, al-Hasan ibn Habib ibn Nudbah told us, Salamah told us, from Nu'aym al-'Anbari, who was among the companions of al-Hasan, who said: I heard al-Hasan, meaning al-Basri, say concerning His statement {and beneath it was a treasure belonging to them}: it was a tablet of gold on which was written: In the name of God, the Most Merciful, the Most Compassionate. I marvel at one who believes in decree, how does he grieve? And I marvel at one who is certain of death, how does he rejoice? And I marvel at one who knows the world and how it turns against its people, how does he feel secure in it? There is no god but God, Muhammad is the Messenger of God.

And [chain] Yunus told me, Ibn Wahb informed us, 'Abdullah ibn 'Ayyash informed me, from 'Umar the freedman of Ghufrah, who said: the treasure that God mentioned in the surah in which the Cave is mentioned, {and beneath it was a treasure belonging to them}, was a tablet of solid gold on which was written: In the name of God, the Most Merciful, the Most Compassionate. How strange is one who knows the Fire and yet laughs! How strange is one who is certain of decree and yet toils! How strange is one who is certain of death and yet feels safe! I bear witness that there is no god but God, and I bear witness that Muhammad is His servant and Messenger.

And [chain] Ahmad ibn Hazim al-Ghifari told me, Hannadah bint Malik al-Shaybaniyyah told us, she said: I heard my companion Hammad ibn al-Walid al-Thaqafi say: I heard Ja'far ibn Muhammad say concerning the word of God Almighty {and beneath it was a treasure belonging to them}: two and a half lines, the third not completed: I marvel at one certain of his provision, how does he grow weary? And I marvel at one certain of the reckoning, how is he heedless? And I marvel at one certain of death, how does he rejoice? And the Almighty has said: {and if there be the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth, and We suffice as reckoners} [al-Anbiya: 47]. She said: and it was mentioned that the two boys were preserved because of the righteousness of their father, though no righteousness of their own was mentioned, and between them and the father through whom they were preserved were seven forefathers, and he was a weaver.

What these leading scholars have mentioned, and what the preceding hadith conveys, even if it were sound, does not contradict the statement of Ikrimah that it was wealth, because they mentioned that it was a tablet of gold, and in it was abundant wealth.
