وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ [يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ] ﴾ أي: النَّاسَ يَوْمَئِذَ أَيْ: يَوْمَ يُدَكُّ هَذَا السَّدُّ وَيَخْرُجُ هَؤُلَاءِ فَيَمُوجُونَ فِي النَّاسِ وَيُفْسِدُونَ عَلَى النَّاسِ أَمْوَالَهُمْ وَيُتْلِفُونَ أَشْيَاءَهُمْ، وَهَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ﴾ قَالَ: ذَاكَ حِينَ يَخْرُجُونَ عَلَى النَّاسِ. وَهَذَا كُلُّهُ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَبَعْدَ الدَّجَّالِ، كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ [إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى] عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُتِحَتْ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ وَهُمْ مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَبٍ يَنْسِلُونَ * وَاقْتَرَبَ الْوَعْدُ الْحَقُّ﴾ [الأنبياْ: ٩٦، ٩٧] وَهَكَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ فَجَمَعْنَاهُمْ جَمْعًا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ﴾ قَالَ: هَذَا أَوَّلُ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ﴾ عَلَى أَثَرِ ذَلِكَ ﴿فَجَمَعْنَاهُمْ جَمْعًا﴾ .

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلِ الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَخْتَلِطُ الْإِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنْ يَعْقُوبُ الْقُمِّيُّ عَنْ هَارُونَ بْنِ عَنْتَرَةَ، عَنْ شَيْخٍ مِنْ بَنِي فَزَارَةَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ﴾ قَالَ: إِذَا مَاجَ الْإِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ قَالَ إِبْلِيسُ: أَنَا أَعْلَمُ لَكُمْ عِلْمَ هَذَا الْأَمْرِ. فَيَظْعَنُ إِلَى الْمَشْرِقِ فَيَجِدُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ قَدْ بَطَّنُوا الْأَرْضَ، ثُمَّ يَظْعَنُ إِلَى الْمَغْرِبِ فَيَجِدُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ بَطَّنُوا الْأَرْضَ فَيَقُولُ: "مَا مِنْ مَحِيصٍ". ثُمَّ يَظْعَنُ يَمِينًا وَشِمَالًا إِلَى أَقْصَى الْأَرْضِ فَيَجِدُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ بَطَّنُوا الْأَرْضَ فَيَقُولُ: "مَا مِنْ مَحِيصٍ" فَبَيْنَمَا هُوَ كَذَلِكَ، إِذْ عُرِضُ لَهُ طَرِيقٌ كَالشِّرَاكِ، فَأَخَذَ عَلَيْهِ هُوَ وَذُرِّيَّتُهُ، فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ إِذْ هَجَمُوا عَلَى النَّارِ، فَأَخْرَجَ اللَّهُ خَازِنًا مِنْ خُزَّانِ النار، فقال: يا إبليس، أَلَمْ تَكُنْ لَكَ الْمَنْزِلَةُ عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ؟! أَلَمْ تَكُنْ فِي الْجِنَانِ؟! فَيَقُولُ: لَيْسَ هَذَا يَوْمَ عِتَابٍ، لَوْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ فَرَضَ عَلَيَّ فَرِيضَةً لَعَبَدْتُهُ فِيهَا عِبَادَةً لَمْ يَعْبُدْهُ مِثْلَهَا أَحَدٌ من خَلْقِهِ. فَيَقُولُ: فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ فَرَضَ عَلَيْكَ فَرِيضَةً. فَيَقُولُ: مَا هِيَ؟ فَيَقُولُ: يَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ تَدْخُلَ النَّارَ. فَيَتَلَكَّأُ عَلَيْهِ، فَيَقُولُ بِهِ وَبِذُرِّيَّتِهِ بِجَنَاحَيْهِ فَيَقْذِفُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ. فَتَزْفِرُ النَّارُ زَفْرَةً لَا يَبْقَى مَلَكٌ مُقَرَّبٌ وَلَا نَبِيٌّ مُرسل إِلَّا جَثَا لِرُكْبَتَيْهِ 

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَعْقُوبَ الْقَمِّيِّ بِهِ. رَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنْ يَعْقُوبَ، عَنْ هَارُونَ عَنْ عَنْتَرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ﴾ قَالَ: الجن الإنس، يَمُوجُ بَعْضُهُمْ فِي بَعْضٍ.

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْعَبَّاسِ الْأَصْفَهَانِيُّ ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مَسْعُودٍ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ الْفُرَاتِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُغِيرَةُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ يَأْجُوجَ وَمَأْجُوجَ مِنْ وَلَدِ آدَمَ، وَلَوْ أُرْسِلُوا لَأَفْسَدُوا عَلَى النَّاسِ مَعَايِشَهُمْ، وَلَنْ يَمُوتَ مِنْهُمْ رَجُلٌ إِلَّا تَرَكَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ أَلْفًا فَصَاعِدًا، وَإِنَّ مِنْ وَرَائِهِمْ ثَلَاثَ أُمَمٍ: تَاوِيلَ، وَتَايَسَ وَمَنْسَكَ". هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ بَلْ مُنْكَرٌ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَرَوَى النَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ سَالِمٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ أَوْسٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ أَوْسِ بْنِ أَبِي أَوْسٍ مَرْفُوعًا: "إِنَّ يَأْجُوجَ وَمَأْجُوجَ لَهُمْ نِسَاءٌ، يُجَامِعُونَ مَا شاؤوا، وشجر يلقحون ما شاؤوا، وَلَا يَمُوتُ مِنْهُمْ رَجُلٌ إِلَّا تَرَكَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ أَلْفًا فَصَاعِدًا" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ﴾ : وَالصُّورُ كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "قَرْنٌ يُنْفَخُ" فِيهِ وَالَّذِي يَنْفُخُ فِيهِ إِسْرَافِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَمَا قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ بِطُولِهِ، وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِيهِ كَثِيرَةٌ.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَأَبِي سَعِيدٍ مَرْفُوعًا: "كَيْفَ أَنْعَمُ، وَصَاحِبُ القَرْن قَدِ الْتَقَمَ القَرْن، وَحَنَى جَبْهَتَهُ وَاسْتَمَعَ مَتَى يُؤْمَرُ". قَالُوا: كَيْفَ نَقُولُ؟ قَالَ: "قُولُوا: حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ، عَلَى اللَّهِ تَوَكَّلْنَا" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿فَجَمَعْنَاهُمْ جَمْعًا﴾ أَيْ: أَحْضَرْنَا الْجَمِيعَ لِلْحِسَابِ ﴿قُلْ إِنَّ الأوَّلِينَ وَالآخِرِينَ لَمَجْمُوعُونَ إِلَى مِيقَاتِ يَوْمٍ مَعْلُومٍ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٤٩، ٥٠] ، ﴿وَحَشَرْنَاهُمْ فَلَمْ نُغَادِرْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا﴾ [الكهف: ٤٧]

---

## 18:100-102 — verses 100-102 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing of what He will do to the disbelievers on the Day of Resurrection: that He will present Hell to them, meaning He will bring it forth for them and make it manifest, so that they may see the punishment and the retribution within it before they enter it, so that this may be more effective in hastening their anguish and grief.

In Sahih Muslim, from Ibn Mas'ud, he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Hell will be brought on the Day of Resurrection being led by seventy thousand reins, with every rein seventy thousand angels [pulling it]."

Then He says, informing of them: {those whose eyes were under a covering from My remembrance}, meaning they feigned blindness, feigned heedlessness, and feigned deafness toward accepting guidance and following the truth, just as the Exalted said: {and whoever is blind to the remembrance of the Most Merciful, We appoint for him a devil who becomes his companion} [al-Zukhruf: 36]. And He says here: {and they were not able to hear}, meaning they did not comprehend from Allah His command and His prohibition.

Then He says: {Do those who disbelieve think that they can take My servants as protectors besides Me?}, meaning: did they believe that this would be valid for them, and that they would benefit by it? {No, they will deny their worship of them and become opponents against them} [Maryam: 82]. Therefore He informed that He has prepared Hell for them on the Day of Resurrection as a lodging.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَمَّا يَفْعَلُهُ بِالْكُفَّارِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: إِنَّهُ يَعْرِضُ عَلَيْهِمْ جَهَنَّمَ، أَيْ: يُبْرِزُهَا لَهُمْ وَيُظْهَرُهَا، لِيَرَوْا مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ قَبْلَ دُخُولِهَا، لِيَكُونَ ذَلِكَ أَبْلَغَ فِي تَعْجِيلِ الْهَمِّ وَالْحَزَنِ لَهُمْ.

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يُؤْتَى بِجَهَنَّمَ تُقَادُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِسَبْعِينَ أَلْفَ زِمام، مَعَ كُلِّ زِمَامٍ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفَ مَلَكٍ [يَجُرُّونَهَا] 

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُخْبِرًا عَنْهُمْ: ﴿الَّذِينَ كَانَتْ أَعْيُنُهُمْ فِي غِطَاءٍ عَنْ ذِكْرِي﴾ أَيْ: تَعَامَوْا وَتَغَافَلُوا وَتَصَامُّوا عَنْ قَبُولِ الْهُدَى وَاتِّبَاعِ الْحَقِّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ يَعْشُ عَنْ ذِكْرِ الرَّحْمَنِ نُقَيِّضْ لَهُ شَيْطَانًا فَهُوَ لَهُ قَرِينٌ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٣٦] وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَكَانُوا لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ سَمْعًا﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَعْقِلُونَ عَنِ اللَّهِ أَمْرَهُ وَنَهْيَهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿أَفَحَسِبَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَنْ يَتَّخِذُوا عِبَادِي مِنْ دُونِي أَوْلِيَاءَ﴾ أَيِ: اعْتَقَدُوا أَنَّهُمْ يَصِحُّ لَهُمْ ذَلِكَ، وَيَنْتَفِعُونَ بِذَلِكَ؟ ﴿كَلا سَيَكْفُرُونَ بِعِبَادَتِهِمْ وَيَكُونُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ ضِدًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٨٢] ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ أَعَدَّ لَهُمْ جَهَنَّمَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مَنْزِلًا.

---

## 18:103-106 — verses 103-106 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Al-Bukhari said: Muhammad ibn Bashshar told us, Muhammad ibn Ja'far told us, Shu'bah told us, from Amr, from Mus'ab who said: I asked my father, meaning Sa'd ibn Abi Waqqas, about {Say, shall We inform you of those who lose most in respect of their deeds?}: are they the Haruriyyah? He said: No, they are the Jews and the Christians. As for the Jews, they disbelieved Muhammad ﷺ, and as for the Christians, they disbelieved in Paradise and said: there is no food or drink in it. The Haruriyyah are those who break the covenant of God after having pledged it. And Sa'd, may God be pleased with him, used to call them the transgressors.

Ali ibn Abi Talib, al-Dahhak, and others said: they are the Haruriyyah.

The meaning of this from Ali, may God be pleased with him, is that this noble verse includes the Haruriyyah just as it includes the Jews, the Christians, and others, not that it was revealed specifically about these or those, rather it is more general than that. For this verse is Meccan, revealed before the address to the Jews and Christians and before the Kharijites existed at all. It is general, applying to everyone who worships God upon a path that is not pleasing to Him, while supposing that he is correct in it and that his deed is accepted, when in fact he is mistaken and his deed is rejected. As God Most High says: {Faces that Day will be humbled, laboring, exhausted, entering a scorching fire} [al-Ghashiyah: 2-4], and His saying: {And We shall turn to whatever deeds they did and make them as scattered dust} [al-Furqan: 23], and His saying: {And those who disbelieve, their deeds are like a mirage in a desert which a thirsty person supposes to be water, until when he comes to it he finds it to be nothing} [al-Nur: 39].

He says in this noble verse: {Say, shall We inform you} that is, shall We tell you {of those who lose most in respect of their deeds?} Then He explains who they are, saying: {those whose effort is lost in the life of this world} that is, they performed false deeds not based on a legislated, pleasing, accepted law, {while they think that they are doing good work} that is, they believe that they are upon something true, and that they are accepted and beloved.

His saying: {Those are the ones who disbelieve in the signs of their Lord and in meeting Him} means: they denied the signs of God in this world and the proofs He established of His oneness and of the truthfulness of His messengers, and they disbelieved in the Hereafter. {So We shall not assign for them any weight on the Day of Resurrection} means: We shall not make their scales heavy, because they are devoid of any good.

Al-Bukhari said: Muhammad ibn Abdullah told us, Sa'id ibn Abi Maryam told us, al-Mughirah informed us, Abu al-Zinad told me, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: "Indeed a huge, fat man will come on the Day of Resurrection, and he will not weigh with God even the weight of a mosquito's wing." And he said: "Recite, if you wish: {So We shall not assign for them any weight on the Day of Resurrection}."

And from Yahya ibn Bukayr, from Mughirah ibn Abd al-Rahman, from Abu al-Zinad, likewise.

Thus he mentioned it from Yahya ibn Bukayr as a suspended report (mu'allaq). Muslim narrated it from Abu Bakr Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from Yahya ibn Bukayr, with the same content.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father told us, Abu al-Walid told us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi al-Zinad told us, from Salih the freedman of al-Taw'amah, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "A man who eats much, drinks much, and is huge will be brought, and he will be weighed against a single grain, and he will not weigh as much as it." He said: and he recited: {So We shall not assign for them any weight on the Day of Resurrection}.

Ibn Jarir likewise narrated it from Abu Kurayb, from Abu al-Salt, from Abu al-Zinad, from Salih the freedman of al-Taw'amah, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, as a raised report (marfu'), mentioning it with wording exactly matching that of al-Bukhari.

Ahmad ibn Amr ibn Abd al-Khaliq al-Bazzar said: al-Abbas ibn Muhammad told us, Awn ibn Umarah told us, Hisham ibn Hassan told us, from Wasil, from Abdullah ibn Buraydah, from his father, who said: We were with the Messenger of God ﷺ when a man from Quraysh came strutting in a fine garment of his. When he stood before the Prophet ﷺ, he said: "O Buraydah, this is one of those for whom God will not establish any weight on the Day of Resurrection."

Then he said: this was narrated uniquely by Wasil, the freedman of Abu Anbasah, and by Awn ibn Umarah, who is not a reliable memorizer (hafiz), and no one else corroborated him. Ibn Jarir also said: Muhammad ibn Bashshar told us, Abd al-Rahman told us, Sufyan told us, from al-A'mash, from Shimr, from Abu Yahya, from Ka'b, who said: A huge, tall man will be brought on the Day of Resurrection, and he will not weigh with God even the weight of a mosquito's wing. Recite: {So We shall not assign for them any weight on the Day of Resurrection}.

His saying: {That is their recompense, Hell, because of their disbelief} means: We only recompensed them with this recompense, Hell, because of their disbelief and their taking the signs of God and His messengers as an object of mockery. They mocked them and rejected them with the utmost rejection.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عَمْرو، عَنْ مُصْعَب قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ أَبِي -يَعْنِي سَعْدَ بْنَ أَبِي وَقَّاصٍ-: ﴿قُلْ هَلْ نُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِالأخْسَرِينَ أَعْمَالا﴾ أَهُمُ الحَرُورية؟ قَالَ: لَا هُمُ الْيَهُودُ وَالنَّصَارَى، أَمَّا الْيَهُودُ فَكَذَّبُوا مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ، وَأَمَّا النَّصَارَى كَفَرُوا بِالْجَنَّةِ، وَقَالُوا: لَا طَعَامَ فِيهَا وَلَا شَرَابَ. وَالْحَرُورِيَّةُ الَّذِينَ يَنْقُضُونَ عَهْدَ اللَّهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مِيثَاقِهِ. وَكَانَ سَعْدٌ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عنه، يسميهم الفاسقين .

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: هُمُ الْحَرُورِيَّةُ.

وَمَعْنَى هَذَا عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ الْكَرِيمَةَ تَشْمَلُ الْحَرُورِيَّةَ كَمَا تَشْمَلُ الْيَهُودَ وَالنَّصَارَى وَغَيْرَهُمْ، لَا أَنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي هَؤُلَاءِ عَلَى الْخُصُوصِ وَلَا هَؤُلَاءِ بَلْ هِيَ أَعَمُّ مِنْ هَذَا؛ فَإِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ مَكِّيَّةٌ قَبْلَ خِطَابِ الْيَهُودِ وَالنَّصَارَى وَقَبْلَ وُجُودِ الْخَوَارِجِ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، وَإِنَّمَا هِيَ عَامَّةٌ فِي كُلِّ مَنْ عَبَدَ اللَّهَ عَلَى غَيْرِ طَرِيقَةٍ مَرْضِيَّةٍ يَحْسَبُ أَنَّهُ مُصِيبٌ فِيهَا، وَأَنَّ عَمَلَهُ مَقْبُولٌ، وَهُوَ مُخْطِئٌ، وَعَمَلُهُ مَرْدُودٌ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَاشِعَةٌ عَامِلَةٌ نَاصِبَةٌ تَصْلَى نَارًا حَامِيَةً﴾ [الْغَاشِيَةِ: ٢-٤] وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَدِمْنَا إِلَى مَا عَمِلُوا مِنْ عَمَلٍ فَجَعَلْنَاهُ هَبَاءً مَنْثُورًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٢٣] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَعْمَالُهُمْ كَسَرَابٍ بِقِيعَةٍ يَحْسَبُهُ الظَّمْآنُ مَاءً حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءَهُ لَمْ يَجِدْهُ شَيْئًا﴾ [النُّورِ: ٣٩] .

وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿قُلْ هَلْ نُنَبِّئُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: نُخْبِرُكُمْ ﴿بِالأخْسَرِينَ أَعْمَالا﴾ ؟ ثُمَّ فَسَّرَهُمْ فَقَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ ضَلَّ سَعْيُهُمْ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ أَيْ: عَمِلُوا أَعْمَالًا بَاطِلَةً عَلَى غَيْرِ شَرِيعَةٍ مَشْرُوعَةٍ مَرْضِيَّةٍ مَقْبُولَةٍ، ﴿وَهُمْ يَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّهُمْ يُحْسِنُونَ صُنْعًا﴾ أَيْ" يَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّهُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ، وَأَنَّهُمْ مَقْبُولُونَ مَحْبُوبُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِ رَبِّهِمْ وَلِقَائِهِ﴾ أَيْ: جَحَدُوا آيَاتِ اللَّهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَبَرَاهِينَهُ الَّتِي أَقَامَ عَلَى وَحْدَانِيَّتِهِ، وَصِدْقِ رُسُلِهِ، وَكَذَّبُوا بِالدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، ﴿فَلا نُقِيمُ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزْنًا﴾ أَيْ: لَا نُثْقِلُ مَوَازِينَهُمْ؛ لِأَنَّهَا خَالِيَةٌ عَنِ الْخَيْرِ .

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، أَخْبَرَنَا الْمُغِيرَةُ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو الزَّنَاد، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِنَّهُ لَيَأْتِي الرَّجُلُ الْعَظِيمُ السَّمِينُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، لَا يزن عند الله جناح بعوضة" وقال: "اقرؤوا إِنْ شِئْتُمْ: ﴿فَلا نُقِيمُ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزْنًا﴾ .

وَعَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ بُكَيْر، عَنْ مُغِيرَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ، مِثْلَهُ .

هَكَذَا ذَكَرَهُ عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ بُكَيْرٍ مُعَلَّقًا . وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرٍ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ بُكَيْرٍ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ، عَنْ صَالِحٍ مَوْلَى التَّوْأمة، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يُؤْتَى بِالرَّجُلِ الْأَكُولِ الشَّرُوبِ الْعَظِيمِ، فَيُوزَنُ بِحَبَّةٍ فَلَا يَزِنُهَا". قَالَ: وَقَرَأَ: ﴿فَلا نُقِيمُ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزْنًا﴾

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي كُرَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ، عَنْ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ، عن صالح مولى التَّوْأَمَةِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، مَرْفُوعًا فَذَكَرَهُ بِلَفْظِ الْبُخَارِيِّ سَوَاءً.

وَقَالَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَبْدِ الْخَالِقِ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا الْعَبَّاسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَوْنُ بْنُ عُمَارة حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ حَسَّانَ، عَنْ وَاصِلٍ، عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ بُرَيْدَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: كُنَّا عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَأَقْبَلَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ يَخْطُرُ فِي حُلَّةٍ لَهُ. فَلَمَّا قَامَ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "يَا بُرَيْدَةُ، هَذَا مِمَّنْ لَا يُقِيمُ اللَّهُ لَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزْنًا" .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ وَاصِلٌ مَوْلَى أَبِي عَنْبَسَةَ وَعَوْنُ بْنُ عُمَارة وَلَيْسَ بِالْحَافِظِ، وَلَمْ يُتَابَعْ عَلَيْهِ. وَقَدْ قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ شِمْرٍ عَنْ أَبِي يَحْيَى، عَنْ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: يُؤْتَى يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِرَجُلٍ عَظِيمٍ طَوِيلٍ، فَلَا يَزِنُ عند الله جناح بعوضة، اقرؤوا: ﴿فَلا نُقِيمُ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزْنًا﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذَلِكَ جَزَاؤُهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ بِمَا كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا جَازَيْنَاهُمْ بِهَذَا الْجَزَاءِ جَهَنَّمَ، بِسَبَبِ كُفْرِهِمْ وَاتِّخَاذِهِمْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَرُسُلَهُ هُزُوًا، اسْتَهْزَءُوا بِهِمْ، وَكَذَّبُوهُمْ أَشَدَّ التَّكْذِيبِ.

---

## 18:107-108 — verses 107-108 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about His fortunate servants, those who believed in Allah and His Messenger and believed them in what they brought, that they will have the gardens of al-Firdaws.

Mujahid said: al-Firdaws is: the garden, in the Roman tongue.

Ka'b, al-Suddi, and al-Dahhak said: it is the garden that contains vine trees.

Abu Umamah said: al-Firdaws is the navel of Paradise.

Qatadah said: al-Firdaws is the elevated ground of Paradise, its middle and its finest part.

This has been reported as a raised hadith through the account of Sa'id ibn Bashir, from Qatadah, from al-Hasan, from Samurah, from the Prophet ﷺ: "al-Firdaws is the elevated ground of Paradise, its middle and its best part." Isma'il ibn Muslim likewise reported it from al-Hasan, from Samurah, as a raised report. It has also been reported from Qatadah, from Anas ibn Malik, as a raised report with similar wording. Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, transmitted it.

In the two Sahihs: "When you ask Allah for Paradise, ask Him for al-Firdaws, for it is the highest part of Paradise and its middle, and from it the rivers of Paradise flow forth."

As for His saying, {as a lodging}: that is, as hospitality, for al-nuzul means hospitality.

As for His saying, {abiding therein forever}: that is, staying and dwelling therein, never departing from it forever. {Seeking no change from it}: that is, they do not choose anything other than it, nor do they love anything besides it, as the poet said:

"I have made the innermost part of my heart its dwelling, I do not seek anything other than it, nor do I turn away from loving it."

In His saying, {seeking no change from it}, there is an indication of their desire for it and their love of it, given that one might imagine that a person who dwells permanently in a place would grow weary of it or become bored with it. So He informed that they, despite this permanence and everlasting abiding, do not choose any shifting away from that dwelling of theirs, nor any transfer, nor any departure, nor any relocation, nor any substitute.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عباده السعداء، وهم الذين آمنوا بالله ورسوله، وصدقوهم فيما جاؤوا بِهِ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتِ الْفِرْدَوْسِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْفِرْدَوْسُ هُوَ: الْبُسْتَانُ بِالرُّومِيَّةِ.

وَقَالَ كَعْبٌ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ: هُوَ الْبُسْتَانُ الَّذِي فِيهِ شَجَرُ الْأَعْنَابِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو أُمَامَةَ الْفِرْدَوْسُ: سُرَّةُ الْجَنَّةِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: الْفِرْدَوْسُ: رَبْوَةُ الْجَنَّةِ وَأَوْسَطُهَا وَأَفْضَلُهَا.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ هَذَا مَرْفُوعًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ ، عَنْ قَتَادَةُ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ سَمُرَة، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: "الْفِرْدَوْسُ ربوة الجنة، أوسطها وأحسنها" وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ سَمُرَةَ مَرْفُوعًا. وَرُوِيَ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ مَرْفُوعًا بِنَحْوِهِ. وَقَدْ نَقَلَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "إِذَا سَأَلْتُمُ اللَّهَ الْجَنَّةَ فَاسْأَلُوهُ الْفِرْدَوْسَ، فَإِنَّهُ أَعْلَى الْجَنَّةِ وَأَوْسَطُ الْجَنَّةِ، وَمِنْهُ تُفَجَّرُ أَنْهَارُ الْجَنَّةِ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿نُزُلًا﴾ أَيْ ضِيَافَةً، فَإِنَّ النُّزُلَ هُوَ الضِّيَافَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مُقِيمِينَ سَاكِنِينَ فِيهَا، لَا يَظْعَنُونَ عَنْهَا أَبَدًا، ﴿لَا يَبْغُونَ عَنْهَا حِوَلا﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَخْتَارُونَ غَيْرَهَا، وَلَا يُحِبُّونَ سِوَاهَا، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ 

فَحَّلْت سُوَيدا القَلْب لَا أنَا بَاغيًا ... سِوَاهَا وَلَا عَنْ حُبّها أتَحوّلُ ...

وَفِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا يَبْغُونَ عَنْهَا حِوَلا﴾ تَنْبِيهٌ عَلَى رَغْبَتِهِمْ فِيهَا، وَحُبِّهِمْ لَهَا، مَعَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ يُتَوَهَّمُ فِيمَنْ هُوَ مُقِيمٌ فِي الْمَكَانِ دَائِمًا أَنَّهُ يَسْأَمُهُ أَوْ يَمَلُّهُ، فَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُمْ مَعَ هَذَا الدَّوَامِ وَالْخُلُودِ السَّرْمَدِيِّ، لَا يَخْتَارُونَ عَنْ مُقَامِهِمْ ذَلِكَ مُتَحَوَّلًا وَلَا انْتِقَالًا وَلَا ظَعْنًا وَلَا رِحْلَةً وَلَا بَدَلًا

---

## 18:109 — verse 109

### Translation

The Almighty says: Say, O Muhammad, if the water of the sea were ink for the pen with which the words of my Lord, His wisdom, and His signs indicating Him are written, {the sea would be exhausted}, that is, [the sea would run out] before the writing of that were finished, {even if We brought the like of it}, that is, the like of the sea, another one, then another, and so on continuously, seas supplying it and being written with, the words of Allah would still not be exhausted. This is as the Almighty said: {And if whatever trees are on the earth were pens, and the sea, replenished thereafter by seven more seas, the words of Allah would not be exhausted. Indeed, Allah is Mighty, Wise} [Luqman: 27].

Al-Rabi' ibn Anas said: the likeness of the knowledge of all the servants together, in relation to the knowledge of Allah, is like a drop from the water of all the seas. Allah revealed this concerning that: {Say, if the sea were ink for the words of my Lord, the sea would be exhausted before the words of my Lord were exhausted, even if We brought the like of it as replenishment}.

He says: if the sea were ink [for the words of Allah], and all the trees were pens, the pens would break and the water of the sea would be used up, while the words of Allah would remain standing, unexhausted by anything. For no one is able to fathom His measure, nor to praise Him as He deserves, until He Himself is the one who praises Himself. Indeed, our Lord is as He says, and above what we say. Indeed, the likeness of the pleasure of this world, from its first to its last, in comparison to the pleasure of the Hereafter, is like a mustard seed amid all the earth.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: قُلْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: لَوْ كَانَ مَاءُ الْبَحْرِ مِدَادًا لِلْقَلَمِ الَّذِي تُكْتَبُ بِهِ كَلِمَاتُ رَبِّى وَحِكَمُهُ وَآيَاتُهُ الدَّالَّةُ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿لَنَفِدَ الْبَحْرُ﴾ أَيْ: [لَفَرَغَ الْبَحْرُ] قَبْلَ أَنْ يُفْرَغَ مِنْ كِتَابَةِ ذَلِكَ ﴿وَلَوْ جِئْنَا بِمِثْلِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِمِثْلِ الْبَحْرِ آخَرَ، ثُمَّ آخَرَ، وَهَلُمَّ جَرًّا، بُحُورٌ تَمُدُّهُ وَيُكْتَبُ بِهَا، لَمَا نَفِدَتْ كَلِمَاتُ اللَّهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ أَنَّمَا فِي الأرْضِ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ أَقْلامٌ وَالْبَحْرُ يَمُدُّهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ سَبْعَةُ أَبْحُرٍ مَا نَفِدَتْ كَلِمَاتُ اللَّهِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٢٧] .

قَالَ الرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ: إِنَّ مَثَلَ عِلْمِ الْعِبَادِ كُلِّهِمْ فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ كَقَطْرَةٍ مِنْ مَاءِ الْبُحُورِ كُلِّهَا، وَقَدْ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ذَلِكَ: ﴿قُلْ لَوْ كَانَ الْبَحْرُ مِدَادًا لِكَلِمَاتِ رَبِّي لَنَفِدَ الْبَحْرُ قَبْلَ أَنْ تَنْفَدَ كَلِمَاتُ رَبِّي وَلَوْ جِئْنَا بِمِثْلِهِ مَدَدًا﴾ .

يَقُولُ: لَوْ كَانَ الْبَحْرُ مِدَادًا [لِكَلِمَاتِ اللَّهِ] ، وَالشَّجَرُ كُلُّهُ أَقْلَامٌ ، لَانْكَسَرَتِ الْأَقْلَامُ وَفَنِيَ مَاءُ الْبَحْرِ، وَبَقِيَتْ كَلِمَاتُ اللَّهِ قَائِمَةً لَا يُفْنِيهَا شَيْءٌ؛ لِأَنَّ أَحَدًا لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ يَقْدُرَ قَدْرَهُ وَلَا يُثْنِيَ عَلَيْهِ كَمَا يَنْبَغِي، حَتَّى يَكُونَ هُوَ الَّذِي يُثْنِي عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، إِنَّ رَبَّنَا كَمَا يَقُولُ وَفَوْقَ مَا نَقُولُ ، إِنَّ مَثَلَ نَعِيمِ الدُّنْيَا أَوَّلِهَا وَآخِرِهَا فِي نَعِيمِ الْآخِرَةِ ، كَحَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ فِي خِلَالِ الْأَرْضِ [كُلِّهَا] .

---

## 18:110 — verse 110

### Translation

Al-Tabarani related, by way of Hisham ibn Ammar, from Isma'il ibn Ayyash, from Amr ibn Qays al-Kufi, that he heard Mu'awiyah ibn Abi Sufyan say: this is the last verse to be revealed.

He says to His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ: {Say} to these polytheists who reject your message to them: {I am only a man like you}, so whoever claims that I am a liar, let him bring the like of what I have brought, for I do not know the unseen regarding what I have told you of the past, of what you asked concerning the story of the People of the Cave and the account of Dhu al-Qarnayn, which corresponds to what actually happened, except for what God informed me of, and I tell you {that your god}, whom I call you to worship, {is one God}, with no partner, {so whoever hopes for the meeting with his Lord}, meaning His reward and His good recompense, {let him do righteous deeds}, whatever is in accordance with God's law, {and not associate anyone in the worship of his Lord}, that is, deeds by which only God's countenance is sought, with no partner. These are the two pillars of an accepted deed: it must be sincere for God's sake alone, and correct according to the practice of the Messenger of God [ﷺ].

Ibn Abi Hatim related, from the hadith of Ma'mar, from Abd al-Karim al-Jazari, from Tawus, who said: a man said, "O Messenger of God, I take my stand at the places of pilgrimage seeking God's countenance, and I also love that my position be seen." The Messenger of God ﷺ did not respond to him at all, until this verse was revealed: {So whoever hopes for the meeting with his Lord, let him do righteous deeds and not associate anyone in the worship of his Lord}.

Mujahid and others likewise reported this as a mursal (report with a missing link at the end) narration.

Al-A'mash said: Hamzah Abu Umarah, the freed client of the Banu Hashim, related to us, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, who said: a man came to Ubadah ibn al-Samit and said, "Tell me about what I am going to ask you: what do you say of a man who prays seeking God's countenance, yet also loves to be praised; who fasts seeking God's countenance, yet also loves to be praised; who gives charity seeking God's countenance, yet also loves to be praised; and who performs the pilgrimage seeking God's countenance, yet also loves to be praised?" Ubadah said, "He has nothing. God Most High says: 'I am the best of partners, so whoever has a partner along with Me, that deed belongs entirely to him, I have no need of it.'"

Imam Ahmad said: Muhammad ibn Abd Allah ibn al-Zubayr related to us, Kathir ibn Zayd related to us, from Rubayh ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi Sa'id al-Khudri, from his father, from his grandfather, who said: we used to take turns attending the Messenger of God ﷺ, spending the night with him in case he had a need or something arose at night, so that he could send us on an errand. The number of volunteers and those on watch increased, and we would talk among ourselves. The Messenger of God ﷺ came out to us and said, "What is this whispering? Did I not forbid you from private whispering?" We said, "We turn to God in repentance, O Prophet of God. We were only speaking of the Messiah (the Antichrist) and our fear of him." He said, "Shall I not tell you of what I fear for you more than the Messiah?" We said, "Yes indeed." He said, "Hidden shirk (associating partners with God), that a man should stand to pray for the sake of another man's presence."

Imam Ahmad said: Abu al-Nadr related to us, Abd al-Hamid, that is, Ibn Bahram, related to us, saying: Shahr ibn Hawshab said: Ibn Ghanm said: when I and Abu al-Darda entered the mosque of al-Jabiyah, we met Ubadah ibn al-Samit. He took my right hand with his left hand and Abu al-Darda's left hand with his right hand, and went out walking between us while we were whispering to each other, and God knows best what we were whispering about. Ubadah ibn al-Samit said, "If one or both of you should live long, you will soon see a man from the very midst of the Muslims, meaning from among the general body, who recites the Qur'an as it was transmitted through Muhammad ﷺ, repeating and reciting it from the beginning, declaring lawful what it makes lawful and forbidden what it makes forbidden, and settling wherever it settles, yet he will bring you no more benefit than the head of a dead donkey brings benefit."

He said: while we were like that, Shaddad ibn Aws, may God be pleased with him, and Awf ibn Malik appeared and sat with us. Shaddad said, "The thing I fear most for you, O people, is what I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ mention, of hidden desire and shirk." Ubadah ibn al-Samit and Abu al-Darda said, "God forgive us. Did not the Messenger of God ﷺ tell us that Satan has despaired of being worshipped in the Arabian Peninsula? As for hidden desire, we already know what that is, it is the desires of this world, its women and its other appetites. But what is this shirk you are warning us of, O Shaddad?"

Shaddad said, "What do you think, if you saw a man praying for the sake of another man, or fasting for the sake of another man, or giving charity for his sake, would you consider that he had committed shirk?" They said, "Yes, by God, whoever prays for another man's sake, or fasts for his sake, or gives charity for his sake, has indeed committed shirk." Shaddad said, "I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: whoever prays to be seen has committed shirk, whoever fasts to be seen has committed shirk, and whoever gives charity to be seen has committed shirk."

At that, Awf ibn Malik said, "Will God not take, from all such deeds, whatever was sincerely sought for His countenance, and accept what was purely for Him while discarding what had a partner mixed into it?" Shaddad said in response, "I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: God says, 'I am the best of partners for anyone who associates a partner with Me. Whoever associates a partner with Me in anything, then all of his deed, little or much, belongs to the partner he associated with Me, and I have no need of it.'"

Another route for part of this: Imam Ahmad said: Zayd ibn al-Hubab related to us, Abd al-Wahid ibn Ziyad related to me, Ubadah ibn Nusayy informed us, from Shaddad ibn Aws, may God be pleased with him, that he wept, and it was said to him, "What makes you weep?" He said, "Something I heard from the Messenger of God ﷺ, which I remembered and it made me weep. I heard the Messenger of God say: 'I fear for my nation shirk and hidden desire.'" I said, "O Messenger of God, will your nation associate partners with God after you?" He said, "Yes, though they will not worship a sun, a moon, a stone, or an idol, but they will show off in their deeds. And hidden desire is that one of them wakes up fasting, and then some desire of his presents itself to him, so he abandons his fast."

Ibn Majah related it from the hadith of al-Hasan ibn Dhakwan, from Ubadah ibn Nusayy, with this content. Ubadah has some weakness in him, and there is doubt about whether he actually heard from Shaddad.

Another hadith: the hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: al-Husayn ibn Ali ibn Ja'far al-Ahmar related to us, Ali ibn Thabit related to us, Qays ibn Abi Hasin related to us, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "God says on the Day of Resurrection: I am the best of partners. Whoever associates any partner with Me, that deed belongs entirely to him."

Imam Ahmad said: Muhammad ibn Ja'far related to us, Shu'bah related to us, I heard al-Ala relate from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, narrating it from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, that He said: "I am the best of partners. Whoever does a deed in which he associates someone else with Me, I am free of it, and it belongs to the one he associated with Me." He alone transmitted it by this route.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Yunus related to us, Layth related to us, from Yazid, that is, Ibn al-Had, from Amr, from Mahmud ibn Labid, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "The thing I fear most for you is the lesser shirk." They said, "What is the lesser shirk, O Messenger of God?" He said, "Showing off (riya). God says on the Day of Resurrection, when He recompenses people for their deeds: go to those for whom you used to show off in the world, and see whether you find any reward with them."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Muhammad ibn Bakr related to us, Abd al-Hamid, that is, Ibn Ja'far, informed us, my father informed me, from Ziyad ibn Mina, from Abu Sa'id ibn Abi Fadalah al-Ansari, who was one of the companions, that he said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say, "When God gathers the first and the last for the Day of Resurrection, the day about which there is no doubt, a caller will call out: whoever associated anyone with God in a deed he did for God's sake, let him seek its reward from someone other than God, for God is more free of need of any partners than any other partner."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah both related it, from the hadith of Muhammad ibn Bakr, that is, al-Bursani, with this content.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Ahmad ibn Abd al-Malik related to us, Bakkar related to us, my father, that is, Abd al-Aziz ibn Abi Bakrah, related to me, from Abu Bakrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Whoever makes his deeds heard, God will make it heard about him, and whoever shows off, God will show it off about him."

Imam Ahmad said: Mu'awiyah related to us, Shayban related to us, from Firas, from Atiyyah, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, who said, "Whoever shows off, God will show it off about him, and whoever makes his deeds heard, God will make it heard about him."

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Yahya ibn Sa'id related to us, from Shu'bah, 'Amr ibn Murrah related to me, he said: I heard a man in the house of Abu 'Ubaydah, that he heard 'Abdullah ibn 'Amr relating to Ibn 'Umar, that he heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Whoever makes people hear of his deed, Allah will make it heard, He will expose him before His creation, belittle him and humiliate him." [He said]: Then the eyes of 'Abdullah shed tears.

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: 'Amr ibn Yahya al-Ayli related to us, al-Harith ibn Ghassan related to us, Abu 'Imran al-Jawni related to us, from Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The deeds of the children of Adam will be presented before Allah, mighty and majestic is He, on the Day of Resurrection in sealed scrolls. Allah will say: Cast this one away and accept this one. The angels will say: O our Lord, by Allah, we saw nothing from him but good. He will say: Indeed his deed was for other than My face, and I do not accept today from deeds except what was intended for My face."

Then al-Harith ibn Ghassan said: A group narrated from him, and he is a Basran, there is no harm in him.

Ibn Wahb said: Yazid ibn 'Iyad related to me, from 'Abd al-Rahman al-A'raj, from 'Abdullah ibn Qays al-Khuza'i, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever stands up for prayer out of showing off and seeking to be heard remains in Allah's displeasure until he sits down."

Abu Ya'la said: Muhammad ibn Abi Bakr related to us, Muhammad ibn Dinar related to us, from Ibrahim al-Hajari, from Abu al-Ahwas, from 'Awf ibn Malik, from Ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever performs the prayer well where people see him and performs it poorly when he is alone, that is a belittling by which he has belittled his Lord, mighty and majestic is He."

Ibn Jarir said: Abu 'Amir Isma'il ibn 'Amr al-Sakuni related to us, Hisham ibn 'Ammar related to us, Ibn 'Ayyash related to us, 'Amr ibn Qays al-Kindi related to us, that he heard Mu'awiyah ibn Abi Sufyan recite this verse, {So whoever hopes for the meeting with his Lord, let him do righteous deeds and not associate anyone in the worship of his Lord}, and he said: This is the last verse revealed from the Qur'an.

This is a problematic report, for this verse is the last verse of Surat al-Kahf, and al-Kahf is entirely Meccan. Perhaps Mu'awiyah meant that nothing was revealed after it that abrogates it or changes its ruling, rather it remains established and clear in judgment, and this became confused for some of the narrators, so it was narrated according to the meaning as he understood it, and Allah knows best.

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: Muhammad ibn 'Ali ibn al-Hasan ibn Shaqiq related to us, al-Nadr ibn Shumayl related to us, Abu Qurrah related to us, from Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, from 'Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever recites in a night: {So whoever hopes for the meeting with his Lord, let him do righteous deeds and not associate anyone in the worship of his Lord}, he will have light from 'Adan Abyan to [Mecca], filled with angels." This is exceedingly gharib (singular/rare in its chain).

End of the tafsir of Surat al-Kahf, and all praise is due to Allah.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

رَوَى الطَّبَرَانِيُّ مِنْ طَرِيقِ هِشَامِ بْنِ عَمَّارٍ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ قَيْسٍ الْكُوفِيِّ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنَ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: هَذِهِ آخِرُ آيَةٍ أُنْزِلَتْ .

يَقُولُ لِرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ : ﴿قُلْ﴾ لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِرِسَالَتِكَ إِلَيْهِمْ: ﴿إِنَّمَا أَنَا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ﴾ فَمَنْ زَعَمَ أَنِّي كَاذِبٌ، فَلْيَأْتِ بِمِثْلِ مَا جِئْتُ بِهِ، فَإِنِّي لَا أَعْلَمُ الْغَيْبَ فِيمَا أَخْبَرْتُكُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْمَاضِي، عَمَّا سَأَلْتُمْ مِنْ قِصَّةِ أَصْحَابِ الْكَهْفِ، وَخَبَرِ ذِي الْقَرْنَيْنِ، مِمَّا هُوَ مُطَابِقٌ فِي نَفْسِ الْأَمْرِ، لَوْلَا مَا أَطْلَعَنِي اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَأَنَا أُخْبِرُكُمْ ﴿أَنَّمَا إِلَهُكُمْ﴾ الَّذِي أَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَى عِبَادَتِهِ، ﴿إِلَهٌ وَاحِدٌ﴾ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، ﴿فَمَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ رَبِّهِ﴾ أَيْ: ثَوَابَهُ وَجَزَاءَهُ الصَّالِحَ، ﴿فَلْيَعْمَلْ عَمَلا صَالِحًا﴾ ، مَا كَانَ مُوَافِقًا لِشَرْعِ اللَّهِ ﴿وَلا يُشْرِكْ بِعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِ أَحَدًا﴾ وَهُوَ الَّذِي يُرَادُ بِهِ وَجْهُ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَهَذَانَ رُكْنَا الْعَمَلِ الْمُتَقَبَّلِ. لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَكُونَ خَالِصًا لِلَّهِ، صوابُا عَلَى شَرِيعَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ [ﷺ] . وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَعْمَرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْكَرِيمِ الجَزَري، عَنْ طَاوُسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَجُلٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي أَقِفُ الْمَوَاقِفَ أُرِيدُ وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، وَأُحِبُّ أَنْ يُرَى مَوْطِنِي. فَلَمْ يَرُدَّ عَلَيْهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ شَيْئًا. حَتَّى نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿فَمَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ رَبِّهِ فَلْيَعْمَلْ عَمَلا صَالِحًا وَلا يُشْرِكْ بِعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِ أَحَدًا﴾ .

وَهَكَذَا أَرْسَلَ هَذَا مُجَاهِدٌ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَمْزَةُ أَبُو عُمَارَةَ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ، عَنْ شَهْر بْنِ حَوْشَب قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ فَقَالَ: أَنْبِئْنِي عَمَّا أَسْأَلُكَ عَنْهُ: أَرَأَيْتَ رَجُلًا يُصَلِّي، يَبْتَغِي وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، وَيُحِبُّ أَنْ يُحْمَد، وَيَصُومُ وَيَبْتَغِي وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، وَيُحِبُّ أَنْ يُحْمَدَ، وَيَتَصَدَّقُ وَيَبْتَغِي وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، وَيُحِبُّ أَنْ يُحْمَدَ، وَيَحُجُّ وَيَبْتَغِي وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، وَيُحِبُّ أَنْ يُحْمَدَ، فَقَالَ عُبَادَةُ: لَيْسَ لَهُ شَيْءٌ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: "أَنَا خَيْرُ شَرِيكٍ، فَمَنْ كَانَ لَهُ مَعِي شَرِيكٌ فَهُوَ له كله، لا حاجة لي فيه". وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، ثَنَا كَثِيرُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ رُبَيْحِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: كُنَّا نَتَنَاوَبُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَنَبِيتُ عِنْدَهُ، تَكُونُ لَهُ الْحَاجَةُ، أَوْ يَطْرُقُهُ أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ، فَيَبْعَثُنَا. فَكَثُرَ الْمُحْتَسِبُونَ وَأَهْلُ النُّوب، فَكُنَّا نَتَحَدَّثُ، فَخَرَجَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "مَا هَذِهِ النَّجْوَى؟ [أَلَمْ أَنْهَكُمْ عَنِ النَّجْوَى] . قَالَ: فَقُلْنَا: تُبْنَا إِلَى اللَّهِ، أَيْ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ، إِنَّمَا كُنَّا فِي ذِكْرِ الْمَسِيحِ، وَفَرِقِنَا مِنْهُ، فَقَالَ: "أَلَا أُخْبِرُكُمْ بِمَا هُوَ أَخْوَفُ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنَ الْمَسِيحِ عِنْدِي؟ " قَالَ: قُلْنَا: بَلَى. قَالَ: "الشِّرْكُ الْخَفِيُّ، أَنْ يَقُومَ الرَّجُلُ يُصَلِّي لِمَكَانِ الرَّجُلِ". 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو النَّضْرِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْحَمِيدِ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ بَهْرَام-قَالَ: قَالَ شَهْر بْنُ حَوْشَب: قَالَ ابْنُ غَنْمٍ: لَمَّا دَخَلْنَا مَسْجِدَ الْجَابِيَةِ أَنَا وَأَبُو الدَّرْدَاءِ، لَقِينَا عُبَادَةَ بْنَ الصَّامِتِ، فَأَخَذَ يَمِينِي بِشِمَالِهِ، وَشِمَالَ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ بِيَمِينِهِ، فَخَرَجَ يَمْشِي بَيْنَنَا وَنَحْنُ نَتَنَاجَى، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا نَتَنَاجَى بِهِ، فَقَالَ عُبَادَةُ بْنُ الصَّامِتِ: إِنْ طَالَ بِكُمَا عُمْرُ أَحَدِكُمَا أَوْ كِلَيْكُمَا، لَتُوشِكَانِ أَنْ تَرَيَا الرَّجُلَ مِنْ ثَبَجِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ -يَعْنِي مِنْ وَسَطِ-قَرَأَ الْقُرْآنِ عَلَى لِسَانِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ فَأَعَادَهُ وَأَبْدَأَهُ، وَأَحَلَّ حَلَالَهُ وَحَرَّمَ حَرَامَهُ، وَنَزَلَ عِنْدَ مَنَازِلِهِ، لَا يَحُورُ فِيكُمْ إِلَّا كَمَا يَحُور رَأْسُ الْحِمَارِ الْمَيِّتِ. قَالَ: فَبَيْنَمَا نَحْنُ كَذَلِكَ، إِذْ طَلَعَ شَدَّادُ بْنُ أَوْسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَعَوْفُ بْنُ مَالِكٍ، فَجَلَسَا إِلَيْنَا، فَقَالَ شَدَّادٌ: إِنَّ أَخْوَفَ مَا أَخَافُ عَلَيْكُمْ أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ لَمَا سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ الله صلى الله عليه وسلم يقول: "من الشَّهْوَةِ الْخَفِيَّةِ وَالشِّرْكِ". فَقَالَ عُبَادَةُ بْنُ الصَّامِتِ، وأبو الدرداء: اللهم غفرًا. أو لَمْ يَكُنْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَدْ حَدَّثَنَا أَنَّ الشَّيْطَانَ قَدْ يَئِسَ أَنْ يُعْبَدَ فِي جَزِيرَةِ الْعَرَبِ. وَأَمَّا الشَّهْوَةُ الْخَفِيَّةُ فَقَدْ عَرَفْنَاهَا، هِيَ شَهَوَاتُ الدُّنْيَا مِنْ نِسَائِهَا وَشَهَوَاتِهَا، فَمَا هَذَا الشِّرْكُ الَّذِي تُخَوِّفُنَا بِهِ يَا شَدَّادُ؟ فَقَالَ شَدَّادٌ: أَرَأَيْتُكُمْ لَوْ رَأَيْتُمْ رَجُلًا يُصَلِّي لِرَجُلٍ، أَوْ يَصُومُ لِرَجُلٍ، [أَوْ تَصَدَّقَ لَهُ، أَتَرَوْنَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ أَشْرَكَ؟ قَالُوا: نَعَمْ، وَاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ مَنْ صَلَّى لِرَجُلٍ أَوْ صَامَ لَهُ] أَوْ تَصَدَّقَ لَهُ، لَقَدْ أَشْرَكَ. فَقَالَ شَدَّادٌ: فَإِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ [يَقُولُ] : مَنْ صَلَّى يُرَائِي فَقَدْ أَشْرَكَ، وَمَنْ صَامَ يُرَائِي فَقَدْ أَشْرَكَ، وَمَنْ تَصَدَّقَ يُرَائِي فَقَدْ أَشْرَكَ؟ " فَقَالَ عَوْفُ بْنُ مَالِكٍ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: أَفَلَا يَعْمِدُ اللَّهُ إِلَى مَا ابْتُغِيَ بِهِ وَجْهُهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ الْعَمَلِ كُلِّهِ، فَيَقْبَلُ مَا خُلِصَ لَهُ وَيَدَعُ مَا أُشْرِكَ بِهِ؟ فَقَالَ شَدَّادٌ عَنْ ذَلِكَ: فَإِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: أَنَا خَيْرُ قَسِيمٍ لِمَنْ أَشْرَكَ بِي، مَنْ أَشْرَكَ بِي شَيْئًا فَإِنَّ [حَشْده] عَمَلَهُ قَلِيلَهُ وَكَثِيرَهُ لِشَرِيكِهِ الَّذِي أَشْرَكَ بِهِ، وَأَنَا عَنْهُ غَنِيٌّ" .

طَرِيقٌ [أُخْرَى] لِبَعْضِهِ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ الحُبَاب، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الْوَاحِدِ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا عُبَادَةُ بْنُ نُسيّ، عَنْ شَدَّادِ بْنِ أَوْسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ بَكَى، فَقِيلَ لَهُ: مَا يُبْكِيكَ؟ قَالَ: شَيْءٌ سَمِعْتُهُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُهُ [فَذَكَرْتُهُ] فَأَبْكَانِي، سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ يَقُولُ: "أَتَخَوَّفُ عَلَى أُمَّتِي الشِّرْكَ وَالشَّهْوَةَ الْخَفِيَّةَ". قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَتُشْرِكُ أُمَّتُكَ [مِنْ بَعْدِكَ؟] قَالَ: "نعم، أَمَا إِنَّهُمْ لَا يَعْبُدُونَ شَمْسًا وَلَا قَمَرًا، ولا حجرًا ولا وثنًا، ولكن يراؤون بِأَعْمَالِهِمْ، وَالشَّهْوَةُ الْخَفِيَّةُ أَنْ يُصْبِحَ أَحَدُهُمْ صَائِمًا فَتَعْرِضُ لَهُ شَهْوَةٌ مِنْ شَهَوَاتِهِ فَيَتْرُكُ صَوْمَهُ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ ذَكْوَان، عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ نُسيّ، بِهِ . وَعُبَادَةُ فِيهِ ضَعْفٌ وَفِي سَمَاعِهِ مِنْ شَدَّادٍ نَظَرٌ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ الْأَحْمَرُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، حَدَّثَنَا قَيْسُ بْنُ أَبِي حَصِينٍ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: أَنَا خَيْرُ شَرِيكٍ، مَنْ أَشْرَكَ بِي أَحَدًا فَهُوَ لَهُ كُلُّهُ".

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، سَمِعْتُ الْعَلَاءَ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، يَرْوِيهِ عَنْ رَبِّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "أَنَا خَيْرُ الشُّرَكَاءِ، فَمَنْ عَمِلَ عَمَلًا أَشْرَكَ فِيهِ غَيْرِي، فَأَنَا منه برئ، وَهُوَ لِلَّذِي أَشْرَكَ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، حَدَّثَنَا لَيْث، عَنْ يَزِيدَ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ الْهَادِ-عَنْ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ مَحْمُودِ بْنِ لَبِيدٍ؛ أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: "إِنَّ أَخْوَفَ مَا أَخَافُ عَلَيْكُمُ الشِّرْكُ الْأَصْغَرُ". قَالُوا: وَمَا الشِّرْكُ الْأَصْغَرُ يَا رَسُولَ الله؟ قال: "الرياء، يقول الله يوم القيامة إذا جزى الناس بأعمالهم: اذهبوا إلى الذين كنتم تراؤون فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَانْظُرُوا هَلْ تَجِدُونَ عِنْدَهُمْ جَزَاءً" 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَكْرٍ أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ الْحَمِيدِ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ جَعْفَرٍ-أَخْبَرَنِي أَبِي، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ مِينَاءَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي فَضَالَةَ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ -وَكَانَ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ-أَنَّهُ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِذَا جَمَعَ اللَّهُ الْأَوَّلِينَ وَالْآخِرِينَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لِيَوْمٍ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ، نَادَى مُنَادٍ: مَنْ كَانَ أَشْرَكَ فِي عَمَلٍ عَمِلَهُ لِلَّهِ أَحَدًا، فَلْيَطْلُبْ ثَوَابَهُ مِنْ عِنْدِ غَيْرِ اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ أَغْنَى الشُّرَكَاءِ عَنِ الشِّرْكِ".

وَأَخْرَجَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، [مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ] بَكْرٍ وَهُوَ البُرساني، بِهِ 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ، حَدَّثَنَا بَكَّارٌ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي -يَعْنِي عَبْدَ الْعَزِيزِ بْنَ أَبِي بَكْرَةَ -عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ سمَّع سمَّع اللَّهُ بِهِ، وَمَنْ رَاءَى رَاءَى اللَّهُ بِهِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا شَيْبَانُ، عَنْ فِرَاسٍ، عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنْ أبي سعيد الْخُدْرِيِّ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَنْ يُرَائِي يُرَائِي اللَّهُ بِهِ، وَمَنْ يُسَمِّعْ يُسَمِّعُ اللَّهُ بِهِ" .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ مُرَّةَ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَجُلًا فِي بَيْتِ أَبِي عُبَيْدَةَ؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يُحَدِّثُ ابْنِ عُمَرَ ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "مَنْ سَمَّع النَّاسَ بِعَمَلِهِ سَمَّع اللَّهُ بِهِ، سَامَعَ خَلْقَهُ وَصَغَّرَهُ وَحَقَّرَهُ" [قَالَ] : فَذَرَفَتْ عَيْنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ يَحْيَى الْأَيْلِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَارِثُ بْنُ غَسَّانَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عِمْرَانَ الْجَوْنِيُّ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "تُعْرَضُ أَعْمَالُ بَنِي آدَمَ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي صُحُفٍ مَخْتُومَةٍ ، فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ: أَلْقُوا هَذَا، وَاقْبَلُوا هَذَا، فَتَقُولُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ: يَا رَبِّ، وَاللَّهِ مَا رَأَيْنَا مِنْهُ إِلَّا خَيْرًا. فَيَقُولُ: إِنَّ عَمَلَهُ كَانَ لِغَيْرِ وَجْهِي، وَلَا أَقْبَلُ الْيَوْمَ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ إِلَّا مَا أُرِيدَ بِهِ وَجْهِي".

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْحَارِثُ بْنُ غَسَّانَ: رَوَى عَنْهُ جَمَاعَةٌ وَهُوَ بَصْرِيٌّ لَيْسَ بِهِ بَأْسٌ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ وَهْبٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يَزِيدُ بْنُ عِيَاضٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ الْخُزَاعِيِّ، أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: "مَنْ قَامَ رِيَاءً وَسُمْعَةً، لَمْ يَزَلْ فِي مَقْتِ اللَّهِ حَتَّى يَجْلِسَ". 

وَقَالَ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْهَجَرِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَوْفِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنِ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ أَحْسَنَ الصَّلَاةَ حَيْثُ يَرَاهُ النَّاسُ وَأَسَاءَهَا حَيْثُ يَخْلُو، فَتِلْكَ اسْتِهَانَةٌ اسْتَهَانَ بِهَا رَبَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ". 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو السَّكوني، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عَيَّاشٍ ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ قَيْسٍ الْكِنْدِيُّ؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنَ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ ﴿فَمَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ رَبِّهِ فَلْيَعْمَلْ عَمَلا صَالِحًا وَلا يُشْرِكْ بِعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِ أَحَدًا﴾ وَقَالَ: إِنَّهَا آخِرُ آيَةٍ نزلت من القرآن. 

وهذا أَثَرٌ مُشْكِلٌ، فَإِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ [هِيَ] آخِرُ سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ. وَالْكَهْفُ كُلُّهَا مَكِّيَّةٌ، وَلَعَلَّ مُعَاوِيَةَ أَرَادَ أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَنْزِلْ بَعْدَهَا مَا تَنْسَخُهَا وَلَا يُغَيِّرُ حُكْمَهَا بَلْ هِيَ مُثْبَتَةٌ مُحْكَمَةٌ، فَاشْتَبَهَ ذَلِكَ عَلَى بَعْضِ الرُّوَاةِ، فَرَوَى بِالْمَعْنَى عَلَى مَا فَهِمَهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ شَقِيقٍ، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ شميل، حدثنا أبو قُرَّرة، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ قَرَأَ فِي لَيْلَةٍ: ﴿فَمَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ رَبِّهِ فَلْيَعْمَلْ عَمَلا صَالِحًا وَلا يُشْرِكْ بِعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِ أَحَدًا﴾ ، كَانَ لَهُ مِنْ نُورٍ، مِنْ عَدَنَ أَبْيَنَ إِلَى [مَكَّةَ] حَشْوُهُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا.

آخر [تفسير] سورة الكهف ولله الحمد

---
